# Tamacahut n Ëmed Xemmar

# Yahia Bellil

Macahu …

Tamacahut-iw ad telhu, ad teḍbeɛ am usaru, ad tuɣal annect n ujgu !

Ɣef yiwen ugellid -Agellid ala Rebbi- yuɣ tlata tlawin.

Yal yiwet deg-sent, yesɛa yid-s aqcic. Mi mmden warrac-nni, yefka-yasen tibḥirt, ttɛassan-tt d ddala, axaṭer yessefsad-as lɣella yiwen lxelq urǧin t-yeẓri. Arrac uɣen awal; bḍan gar-asen ussan n ddurt.

Yiwen yiḍ, iɛus nnuba-s umeqqran deg-sen -qqaren-as Ḥmed Xemmar-, yesla i lheffa tetteddu mehli mehli metwal amkan n letmar. Yegguber lḥeyya-s armi s-d-tban; ar iẓer d acu-tt, ur yeẓri ara. Iwet-itt s uṭiɣan, iḥus yemken-itt, meɛna ur teɣli ara : tewwi tiyita, terwel.

Ḥmed yedda deffir-s, lakayen mačči d ayen ara d- yeṭṭef : Aɣiwel d aḍu ; yal asurif deg-s amrar. Yeḍfer lemrira n yidammen armi tt-yuweḍ, yebded-as ɣef tewwurt. Yaf ɣef umnar yiwet tmeṭṭut, tweṣṣa-t ɣef trewla : “Annaɣ a mmi, ur tuklaleḍ ! rwel! Waɣzen tura i d-yekcem, yettejreḥ. Ma yesraḥ-ik-id ad k-id-yeɛnu. Nekk d tameṭṭut-is, meɛna ur k-ttakeɣ ara.

1 Tamacahut-a, tettawi-tt-id Nna Ṭawes. Aṭas i ibeddlen deg-s mi d-teqqel ɣer tira.
deg ufus. Ad k-yečč ur tuklaleḍ ! Ɣiwel asurif !

- D aya i yi-d yuwin ɣer-s, i s-yerra Ḥmed. Yerna-yas : Bɣiɣ ad nnaɣeɣ yid-s.

- Tawwurt teldi. Ruḥ ad tkecmeḍ ɣer-s.

Ḥmed yegr asurif ad yezger amnar. Teḥbes-it tmeṭṭut-nni. Teɛqel-it d bu tissas, lakin tugad fell-as ma ixuṣ deg tḥila. Tenna-yas : “Ad k-weṣṣiɣ tecfuḍ i wawal. Mi ara tkecmeḍ ɣer-s, ini-yas d acu i k-id-yehman; netta ad ak-d-yefk sin n yisekkinen : yiwen, afus-is n uẓref; wayeḍ, afus-is d uffal. Kečč ddem win akken n wuffal. Ini-yas : Kečč ad tzuxeḍ gar tlawin-ik. Nekk ad refdeɣ uffal ; d win i d lektal-iw. Yerna, nṭeg-as ɣer tlemmast n tɣerɣert”.

Yuɣ-as awal Ḥmed. Nnuɣen netta d Waɣzen, yenɣa-t Ḥmed. Yuɣal, imir, ɣer tmurt n baba-s, ad yini i watmaten-is ayen yeḍran.

- Teẓram aniwa i ɣ-yettakren tibḥirt neɣ ala ?

- Mel-aɣ-t-id ! Ad naweḍ ɣer-s ad d-yefk ayen ur yečči !

- D Waɣzen !

- Rǧu ! i s-rran. Tebda tettali-ten-id tziri tawraɣt. Kemmlen awal : Yettfakka-k Rebbi ad aɣ-ifakk ! Tagi d lɣellaba !

Mi yeẓra uggaden, dɣa yekkes-asen tuggdin : “Ulayɣer targagayt; nɣiɣ-t !”. Widak-nni dehcen, steqsan-t : Amek ?

- Ur ttafget ara ! Nɣiɣ-t, ih ! Yerna fiḥel ma nesseɣzef awal. Yeqqim-d kan ma ad teddum yid-i ad d-nawi igerrujen n Waɣzen, ad d-nernu tilawin-is. Deg tlata yid-sent.

- Tenwiḍ ad k-nefk iman-ik ɣer tmurt n Waɣzen ? i s-yerra yiwen deg watmaten-is, d axazabi ameqqran.

Netta, ladɣa, ɣer cci akked teslatin iɣer ldint wallen-is, mačči d aɣadi i t-iɣaḍ gma-s. Wayeḍ-nin diɣen yessengugi aqerru-s am win ara iqeblen kra n temsalt, s lferḥ. Ihi, yewwi-ten ɣer wexxam n Waɣzen. Mi wwḍen, ufan tisednan-nni deg tlata, ttmirint d sser, ttrajunt deg Ḥmed; uysent ad d-ffɣent syinna. Yessken-asen-tent Ḥmed, yemla-asen tin ara yaɣ netta; ma d snat-nniḍen i nutni, ad tent-bḍun akken msebɣan. Din din msextaren, myuqqanen sin sin : tmeqqrant i umeqqran, tameẓẓyant i umeẓẓyan.

Ɛebban i zzwayel, srekben tislatin ɣef yiɛidiwen, yal yiwet deffir urgaz-is, ṭṭfen abrid n tuɣalin, srid ɣer tmurt-nsen.

Ddan tallit, ffudent teslatin-nni, neṭqent ɣer Ḥmed : “Yecqa-k ad
tenɛettabeḍ cwiṭ, ad aɣ-d-tawiḍ aman ! ” Winna yerra-asent :

“Yecqa-kent cwiṭ fad simi ara naweḍ ɣer wannu n yimsebriden; drus i yeqqimen !” Atmaten-is, mi akken yekfa awal, myeɣmazen; fran-tt ɣer uɣurru.

Dac ɛqac, dac ɛqac, almi d-ufan iman-nsen ɣef yimi n wannu-nni n yimsebriden. Bdan la ttemyexzaren aniwa ara yadren ad d-yagem aman. Yekker Ḥmed icudd yiwen yixef n umrar ɣer yiwet tḥeccaḍt, yeqqen iman-is deg wammas s yixef-nniḍen, yuder almi d anda i d-ulin waman. Yessalay-asen-d aman s tcegriḍt. Tin yemmaren ad as-tt-rren ad tt-id-yeččar, ad asen-tt-id-yeqqen deg umrar, ad tt-id-jebden d asawen. Ssarden d nnuba, swan.

Armi d lawan ad t-id ssalin netta, kkren gezmen-as amrar, yeɣli. Gullen deg tlawin-nni a tin ara yeqqiren s kra ad glun s yiri-s: “Kunnemti, xemsa ɣef yimi ! Dayen, yemmečč, ifuk !” Imir, rekben, ruḥen; ǧǧan-t din. Armi lḥan amecwar, taqcict-nni i iwessem Ḥmed i yiman-is testeɛmel teɣli-yas tbelɣet-is deg ubrid, dɣa tessuter deg yilewsan-is : “Ɣas ad uɣaleɣ cwiṭ ɣer deffir ad d…” Yiwen deg-sen yegzem-as awal :” Ddu, ur smiskin ara !

- D tabelɣet-iw i n-ǧǧiɣ, a mmi-s n medden !

- Ruḥ; Ayen tgiḍ ad yezzi d yiri-m !

- Kunwi d gma-twen, teqqur-awen tasa, nekk ad fkeɣ iman-iw i twaɣit ! Ur mxelleɣ ara.”

Tessaker iman-is almi d aqemmuc n wannu, tessawel i Ḥmed, tenna-yas : “Atan ad d-asen ɣer-k sin wakraren : Yiwen d amellal, ma trekbeḍ-d fell-as, ad k-id-yessali sebɛa n lqamat ; wayeḍ d aberkan, ma trekbeḍ fell-as, ad k-yewt sebɛa n lqamat ddaw n tmurt. Cfu akka.”

Syinna, tɣawel tikli ad telḥeq taquffet-is.

Asmi i wwḍen warraw n ugellid s axxam, nnan ayen yeffɣen fell-asen ; zuxen i baba-tsen, xerṣum s wawal : Ḥmed yettwačč ; ma d nutni imi ẓewren, selken-d yerna glan-d s teslatin.

Yekker ugellid yewqem-asen tameɣra.

Maca, kra yekka uheggi i tmeɣra d aferṭeṭṭu itezzi deg uqerru-s, ansa ara yekk i temsalt-is : Ziɣen yebɣa ad yaɣ taǧǧalt n mmi-s.

Yiwen wass kan, yejmeɛ-d imeqqranen n tgelda-s, yeccawer-iten amek ara yexdem. Wigad i t-yuggaden saḥellen-as-tt ; wiyaḍ ugin ad as-qḍun. Yefka rray i tnefsit, yerra ɣer deffir tisirit. Yesɣer aqerru-s, yerna aḥedwil-is ɣer win n warraw-is, yuɣ tislit-is.
Kra n wid-nni yugin ad brun i nnif, yegr-iten ɣer tesraft. Yeṭṭef-iten ccraɛ n yimeḥbas : Ddren tudert n lḥif d laẓ. Yiwen n uhendaz deg-sen iṣeggem-d awal ɣef temsalt, yenna-yas :

- Ad awen-ḥkuɣ a Lislam
- Ɣef tedyant yeḍran
- Amɣar yeḍleb tislit-is
- Acamar-is d aciban
- Ɣlin-as wuglan
- Ur iṭal i laxert-is
- A Rebbi siqqel-as aman
- Tesɣerḍ-as igran
- Tefkeḍ-d ajrad i tmurt-is.

Ḥmed yekka d acu i yekka deg waman, yiwen wass ataya wakrar-nni aberkan ibedd-as zdat wallen-is. Iruḥ am win yettun lewṣaya, yehmel ur yeẓri sani, amer ad yaf talwit ; am win yewwi wasif, yufa-d azrem yeṭṭef deg-s, yeẓra kan akrar-nni, yerkeb fell-as; yeḍmeɛ tawaffɣa seg ṭṭlam ɣer tafat. Yessader i ccfer yessuli-t, yufa-d iman-is deg tmurt n lejnun. Yezwej d twaɣit : Urǧin yeccedha imeṭṭi. Kkes-d ayen ur iɛeddan fell-as.

Asmi yewweḍ lweɛd ad tekfu lmeḥna ɣef uqerru-s, d lejnun s timmad-nsen i t-yessersen, qbel tafrara, zdat tewwurt n ṣṣraya n baba-s.

Ifellaḥen imezwura i t-yemlalen xebbren-t s wayen yeḍran deg leɣyab-is. Ḥmed ur yelli d aɣefli, yebges ɣer ttar. Yenɣa kra n win tt-id-yessasin; yerra ɣer tesraft win yeddan di tmessasin ; yefka tilelli i wat wawal urzin. Deg-s, ad yesken i medden azal n leqder, deg-s ad yergel abrid i uḥemmal n lɛar.

Ssyin akin, yewqem tameɣra meqqren : imalas, iḍ d wass, d ṭṭbel ireddex.

Tamacahut-iw lwad lwad Mliɣ-tt-id i warraw n lǧewwad.
TAèURI
NO_CONTENT_HERE
# ABUNSAY¹

Talalit d gemmu n tbunsayt

Smail Abdenbi

Llan aṭas iberdan yettawin ɣer tqacuct n wedrar. Ssawḍeɣ fehmeɣ belli taẓuri am walluy ɣer tqacuct n wedrar... Mačči yiwen webrid i yellan. I kra, d taklut... Yal yiwen yessefk ad yaf abrid-is. Taẓuri n Ubunsay d abrid seg iberdan yettawin ɣer tqacuct.

Seya Takeshi

Ma llan wid yebɣan ad sɛun tabunsayt* ika ad tt-rebbin neɣ ad sbunsuyen* deg wexxam, ayagi ulac deg-s aɣbel. Yal yiwen seg-wen yezmer ad yefren taɣara (manière) iss yebɣa ad yeslal neɣ ad yawi tabunsayt. Acku, llant sḍis n tɣura iss nezmer ad nesɛu tabunsayt.

Tamezwarut d tabunsayt d-yefka ugama. Nqelleɛ-itt-id seg umedɣaɣ* neɣ akal igellil ideg llan aṭas n yedɣaɣen, ur yenfiɛ ara i yemɣan neɣ dɣa aseklu. D aseklu iɣercen si lḥif iɛeddan fell-as.

Taɣara tis snat, d tabunsayt n tiɣin, znuzun-tent yemzenza n isekla. Di tmurt-nneɣ, mačči aṭas i yellan n wid yeznuzun

1Yal awal ara tafem yesɛa itri nnig-s, ma ur tessinem ara anamek-is, muqlet ɣer taggara n umagrad ad tafem tamawalt n weḍris thegga i waya.
tibunsayin. Ulzuz (marché) n tẓuri werɛad d-ilul. Ihi taswiɛt-agi, ma nuɣ-d aseklu deg uḥabus, mi ara d-naweḍ s axxam, d nekni umi yessefk ad t-nesbunsey. Ad nuɣal tura ɣer tɣara tis kraḍ, d ayen umi neqqar tabunsayt s uɛegga. Wigi d isekla d yettlalen s wuẓu n uɛeqqa amedya n ubelluḍ n tasaft, iɣes n uberquq neɣ win n tmecmact... Tabunsayt-agi tmeɣɣi am akk isekla n tẓegwa d lexlawi. Taɣara tis ukuẓ, d talalit n tbunsayt s teskert. Tagi d taɣara yettwassnen, aṭas i tt-yesseqdacen di tmurt-nneɣ. Gezzmen-d ikerrazen neɣ imdanen s umata tiskar seg useklu, sakin teẓẓun-tent. Maca ur tettut ara, yal talmest (espèce) tesɛa akud n wuẓu. S wayen tiskar-nni azal n sin neɣ kraḍ iseggasen alamma fkant iẓuran, zemrent i yiman-nsent. Taɣara tis semmus, d talalit n tbunsayt s werkal. Taɣara-yagi daɣen tettwassen di tmurt-nneɣ. Arkal, d uẓu n tciṭa war ma negzem-itt-id seg useklu. Llan sin iberdan iss nezmer ad nerkel. Yella werkal igenni, yella daɣen werkal n tqaɛet. Taɣara taneggarut iɣef ad nemmeslay, d talalit n tbunsayt s uleqqem. Ayagi daɣen d amahil yettwassnen ɣur-neɣ seg zik. Ɣer zdat, ad nemmeslay ɣef tɣura-yagi yiwet yiwet. Maca, zdat ad nemmeslay ɣef seddis tɣura yellan iss nezmer ad nawi neɣ ad neslal tabunsayt, ad nezwir ad nemmeslay ɣef yeḥricen iɣef tebna tfekka (corps) n useklu. Ad nefk tamuɣli xas ad tili d tawezlant.

# Aseklu (arbre)

D acu i d aseklu ? Ma neɛreḍ s tewzel ad as-nefk tabadut, ad nini aseklu d imɣi yesɛan lqed, teɣzi-s, tekka-d nnig n 4 lmitrat. Ma d tameddurt-is, aseklu yezmer ad yesni leqrun am wezrar. Yesɛa yiwet n lǧedra d yettaken ifurkan, ntekkes-d seg-s i tmeddurt-nneɣ n yal ass, asɣar, aqeccuc d wayen nniḍen... Maca tamuɣli-yagi txuṣ, acku tibuda mačči d yiwet, llan isekla i zemren ad sɛun aṭas n leǧdari amedya n tneqqelt. Aseklu daɣen d imɣi yezzegziwen yebḍan ɣef snat twaculin. Tawacult tamezwarut, d isekla yesɛan iferrawen hrawen amedya n tasaft, tajujet, tulmut, taneqqelt... Tawacult tis snat, d isekla yesɛan iferrawen rqiqen am yessegnan amedya n yilgel*, azumbi... Ma d tazdayt d uɣanim-nni umi qqaren abambu(bambou), wigi mačči d isekla. Qqaren-d
fell-asen imassanen, wigi d akasa (leḥcic) meqqran, annect-ilaten. Rnu i waya, tazday ma s-negzem taqacuct, ur txellef ara, tettmettat. Tasekluct (arbuste) daɣen tezmer ad tuɣal d tabunsayt. Acku tasekluct, d aseklu meẓẓiyen. Muqlet s udem uṭṭun 01. Din ad twalim aseklu d yeḥricen i ɣef tebna tfekka-s.

# Taqacuct

|Tifurkacin|Loedra|Ifurkan|Akal|Aêabus|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|(Tug. 01)|Tafekka n tbunsayt deg uḥabus.|Teɣzi n tbunsayt-agi 30 iṣantimen.| | |
|Tafrakt|Loedra|Iéuran|(Tug. 02)|Tafekka n useklu s umata.|

# Tabunsayt n ugama (sauvageon)

Aɣrac n useklu deg ugama mačči yiwet n tsebba i yellan. Kra isekla meqqin deg umedɣaɣ, wiyaḍ, tikwal ɣef weẓru. Ika ad yedder useklu-nni, yessefk fell-as ad yessiɣzef iẓuran-is akken ad yaff učči teḥwaǧ tfekka-s. Ma ulac, ad yemmet. Aɣrac iḍerru-d daɣen ma yili useklu yemɣi deg wemḍiq idergen ɣef yiṭij neɣ ixuṣ tafat. Tikwal yettili-d unemgal n waya. Aseklu yemɣi deg wemḍiq yemmugren aṭas iṭij, rnu i waya, lexṣas n waman. Liḥala nniḍen yesseɣracen aseklu d aḍu. Asembiwel n useklu yal ass diri-yas-t. Tasebba taneggarut i ɣef nezmer ad nemmeslay, ma yili mɣin isekla deg wemḍiq n tkessawt. Acku ikes-iten lmal, ur sen-yeǧǧaǧǧa yara ad gmun. D imi d qqaren tuksa n tbunsayt d taɣawsa iweɛren cwiṭ. Acku akk tibunsayin d yettak ugama sɛant iẓuran ɣezzifen aṭas. Ɣef waya, yal ma neffeɣ ɣer tuksa n tbunsayin, yessefk fell-aɣ ad nawi yid-neɣ ifecka n tuksa. Ifecka i nezmer ad ten-neḥwiǧ d widen n uɣizi iss ad nessekfel iẓuran n tbunsayt d wid n wegzame iss ad negzem iẓuran-nni ɣezzifen. War ma nettu aḍellaɛ neɣ taylut ideg ad nawi aseklu d nekkes. Acku aseklu ma t-id-nekkes, yessefk ad nettel iẓuran-is de wakal, ad ten-neffer. Ma ulac, yezmer ad yemmet. Tikwal nezmer ad naff aseklu igerzen i tbunsayt maca ur nzemmer ara ad t-id-nekkes. Amek ad nexdem? Tifrat-is d arkal igenni. Muqlet, ɣer zdat ad tafem amek nrekkel taciṭa deg genni.

# Arkal n igenni

# Aéru

# Aéru

(Tug. 03)

(Tug. 04) Aseklu-yagi yeḥṣel deg iɣisi - Muqlet s iẓuran acḥal i ɣezzifit. n tqaɛet gar sin yeẓra. - Ayen yefren, yugar s waṭas ayen d ibanen.
# Tabunsayt n tiɣin (achat)

Tiḥuna yeznuzun tibunsayin di tmurt-nneɣ ur gtent ara. Xas llant, ur ttwasnent ara. Acku taẓuri-yagi d tamaynut, mazal yers lsas n wulzuz-is. Mačči am di tmura n l'Europe, tiḥuna yeznuzun tibunsayin mačči d yiwet i yellan. Nnig n lqern aya seg-mi d-ilul wulzuz n tẓuri n ubunsay. Qeṭṭun-d tibunsayin-nsen si tmura n Ccin Kurya, d Japon. Nekni tura nezmer ad nruḥ ɣur tḥuna yeznuzun isekla, sakin ad nefren aseklu i d-aɣ-iɛe ǧben ad t-id-naɣɣ. Ma d naweḍ s axxam, aseklu-nni d-nuɣɣ, nezmer ad t-nesbunsey (ad t-nerr d tabunsayt). Maca ɣur-wat, ma d taɣem aseklu neɣ tabusayt, tessawḍem-t-d s axxam, yessefk ad teǧǧem ad yestaɛfu sin neɣ kraḍ wussan war ma tsembawlem-t. Asembiwel n waḍu neɣ win n wemdan dir-it am akken t-id-nenna usawen. Mi yestaɛfa useklu d nuɣ, ad nebdu leqdic-nneɣ.

(Tug. 05) Ambiwel n waṭas, yessaḍan tabunsayt.

# Tabunsayt s uɛeqqa (semis)

Talalit n tbunsait s uɛeqqa tezmer ad tili ɣur kra kan isekla, wid d yettaken iɛeqqayen. D isekla yeǧǧuǧǧugen neɣ wid d yettaken igumma (fruits). Taɣara-yagi teshel. Maca tesɛa ugur n
wakud (temps). Ma neẓẓu aɛeqqa, yessefk fell-aɣ ad-t- neǧu ad yemɣi azal n ukuẓ (4) neɣ semmus (5) iseggasen. Sakin ad nezmer ad nini belli nesɛa tabunsayt. Taẓeyt n uraǧǧu tessaweḍ inaẓuren n iǧuǧǧagen imudduren ad fernen neɣ ad senyafen tiɣaryin nnidḍen ika ad slalen neɣ ad awin tabunsayt. Maca yelha ma ijerreb wemdan akk tiɣura. Ma neddem-d aɛeqqa n lmecmac neɣ win uberquq, ur ilaq ara ad t-d-nekkes seg imi-nneɣ. Acku ileddayen n wemdan neqqen imɣi deg uɛeqqa. Deg isekla, yal talmest (espèce) tesɛa akud n wuẓu. Nezmer ad neẓẓu aɛeqqa-nneɣ srid deg wakal n uḥabus. Ur ilaq ara ad as-nessuggut aman. Alamma yemɣi uɛeqqa, yefka-d iferrawen. Akka, ma nmuqel s iferrawen, nezmer ad nẓer ma ixuṣ aman neɣ ala. Amḍiq n trusi uḥabus deg yella yemɣi, yessefk ad yili yemmugger mliḥ tafat n yiṭij. Akka ad teddrem talalit d gemmu n tbunsayt-nwen seg uɛeqqa armi tuɣal d tabunsayt.

# Tabunsayt s teskert (bouturage)

Tabunsayt s teskert d ayen X isehlen aṭas. Ma tcawrem imɣaren d temɣarin-nneɣ, ad wen-d-inin amek. Acku wid i ɣ- d-yezwaren, sɛan tamusni i zemren ad aɣ-tenfeɛ aṭas deg wennar n tẓuri-yagi. Tamezwarut n tmezwura ad nefren taciṭa i d-aɣ-iɛeǧben, ad negzem iɣef-is. Muqlet s unuɣ ad walim amek nezmer ad negzem tiskar si tciṭa. Tiskert-nneɣ yessefk ad tesɛu di teɣzi azal n 20 neɣ 25 iṣantimen. Ad tt-d-negzem, sakin, ad tt-neǧǧ deg weqbuc n waman kra n ussan. Imir, ad nheggi aḥabus n wakal akken ad tt-neẓẓu. Tiskert-nni d

# (Tug. 06)

- Agzam n tciṭa

- Atan umedya n semmus (5) teskar i wuẓu
negzem, yessefk fell-aɣ ad tt-nheggi iwuẓu. Seg neɣz axjiḍ deg ḥabus, ad neddem aḥric n wadda n teskert ad as-d-nekkes neɣ ad as-d-negzem s lmus n lkaɣeḍ azebg si teglimt-is. azebg-nni ad yesɛu sin neɣ sin d wezgen iṣantimen di tehri. Daḥric-nni a nerr s akal ika ad nɛiwen tufɣa iẓuran war ma ɛeṭṭlen. Meskud mazal tesɛa iẓuran iǧehden, tiskert-nneɣ, ɣas teǧǧuǧǧeg d ixulaf, yessefk fell-aɣ ad tt-nessedreg seg yiṭij. Ma ulac ad takaw, sakin ad teqqar. Ihi, ika ad tedder teskert-nneɣ, ad tuɣal d tabunsay, mačči di ṭlam i ilaq ad tt-neǧǧ. Amḍiq yelhan i trusi n uḥabus, d win deg tella aṭas n tafat war ma yemmugger iṭij.

# Tabunsayt s werkal (marcottage)

Arkal ɣur ikerrazen n tmurt-nneɣ d amahil yellan d aqbur. Sseqdacen-t seg zik ika ad slalen aseklu si tciṭa war ma gezmen-tt-d si lǧedra n useklu. Nezmer ad nini llan sin iberdan neɣ snat tɣura iss nezmer ad nerkel taciṭa. Yella werkal n tqaɛet neɣ ayen umi neqqar arkal amensay (traditionnel). Yella daɣen warkal n igenni. Aneggaru-yagi d atrar (moderne). At Zik, llan sseqdacen arkal d nudder d amezwaru. Iḍerru-d waya s wefran n tciṭa rqiqen yettleɣwin sakin, ad tt-d-nesseknu alamma d taqaɛet.

Imir, ad nqis amḍiq-nni, ad neɣz deg-s axjiḍ. Ad neẓu taciṭa-nni deg wexjiḍ. Mi nerra fell-as akal, ad nsers fella-s aẓru. Taẓeyt n weẓru-nni, tettaṭṭaf taciṭa deg wakal ur d tettuɣal ara s amḍiq-is. Ad tt-nesway kra n wagguren alamma tefka iẓuran. Mi tefka iẓuran, ad negzem taciṭa-nni s iẓuran-is akken ad tt-neẓẓu deg wakal n tqaɛet neɣ win uḥabus.

Arkal igenni am win n tqaɛet, mgaraden kan deg kra n tɣawsiwin. Ad nefren taciṭa nebɣa ad tt-nerr d tabunsayt. Taciṭa-nni ad as-d-negzem azebg si teglimt-is s lmus n lkaɣeḍ am akken nexdem i teskert d nudder usawen. Maca amḍiq n wegzam yessefk ad iḥaz ɣer daxel tiṭ-nni ansi d ǧǧuǧǧugen ifurkan. Ayagi yeshalay aṭas i tciṭa ad tefk iẓuran. Mi nekfa seg uheggi n tciṭa, ad nɣum amḍiq-nni s wakal. Amek ad d-yeḍru waya ? Ad neddem acekkar n blastik ad nettel iss akal-nni yersen ɣef tciṭa. Deg wemḍiq n ucekkar n blastik nezmer daɣen ad nesseqdec aḥabus meẓẓiyen. Ad neflu talemmast n uḥabus-nni s lmus n lkaɣeḍ.

Tehri n fellu, ad yili azal n tehri n teskert-nni. Sakin, ad ncerreg
seg yiwen yidis aḥabus-nneɣ, ad neccekcem tiskert-nni ɣer tlemmast uḥabus, ad t-ncud s ugeṭṭum akken ur ifessex ara ma ad t-neččar d akal. Mi neččur aḥabus-nni d akal, ad t-nesway s waman kra n wagguren alamma yefka iẓuran. Imir, ad d-negzem taciṭa-nni s iẓuran-is, ad tt-neẓẓu deg uḥbus. Akka i d iḍerru werkal iss nezmer ad neslal tabunsayt neɣ aseklu.

# Tabunsayt s uleqqem (greffer)

Aleqqem di tẓuri n ubunsay telha-d aseklu d iẓuran-is. S imeslayen nniḍen, nezmer ad nleqqem aseklu, nezmer daɣen ad nleqqem iẓuran. Maca iẓuran, d tamacahut nniḍen, ad nuɣal ɣer-sen ass nniḍen. Aleqqem d amahil yettwasnen di tmurt-nneɣ, uryemgarad ara d uleqqem nesseqdac i tbunsayin. Acu kan, aleqqem tikwal yettaǧǧa-d ccama ur ntekkes di lǧedra n useklu, yecmutuy tabunsayt. Nettleqqim aseklu neɣ tasekluct deg yiwet n liḥala. Ma naff agerz n lǧedra igerzen yeklal ad yuɣal d tabunsayt. Acu kan aseklu nefren ur ilaq ara ad yili meqqer di leɛmer, kraḍ (3) neɣ semmus (4)iseggasen. Nezmer ad nleqqem aseklu-nneɣ ma yili di lexla. Nezmer daɣen ad nenqel aseklu-nni s aḥabus, sakin ad t-nleqqem.

|---|---|---|

# Tame$ra

# Rabha Aissou

Yuli wass, bdan medden a d-ttifriren si tesga ma d azrug yettawin $er wexxam n Wardia Iâisawen ussan-agi ur yessin ara taguni. Tiftilin zgant ceâlent. Avan la d-iteddun d imxulaf maççi kan êala tiftilin n taddart i iceâlen lumaâna u$alent acêal i tiyav i wakken a d-beggnent tame$ra.

Yal yiwen di taddart d ugur swayes yeîîes ass-agi: wa yettxemmim ansi ara d-ijab lehna, wa, yeb$a ad yessem$er avellaâ i wakken ad yessefreê Wiza. Sekra yekka yiv s te$zi-s, l$aci reffden ssrusun. Lumaâna simmal yettaé yiv di nnûaf simmal bdan wuguren a ttexcawaten wa deffir wa. Iéri yebda a tettisliw, siwa iéri n Wiza luked wid faydeg i$ab yid-s i yeqqimen ad hesbent itran.

Wiza la tesseêsab acêal i s-d-mazal i tme$ra-s, ussan la iteddun $ur-s amzun di laâmer-is i la ttan$asen, ur teéri ara ma yella iwata-yas-d a tru ne$ a tâeggev ne$ a ttarou u a tessusem, a tt-ttawint lba$at ur teéri d acu i s-ffren wussan. Akken kan yebda yiîij a d-ineqqer tagnawt, teîîef abrid-is $er tala. Maççi d aman i ixuûûen deg wexxam lumaâna tu$al-as d tannumi tarniv Wiza teb$a a testaâfu seg uxemmem.
Teméi-s yak tesâedda-tt di ti$ilt At Äli, gar wexxam d tala âlaxaîar Waôdiya ur tezmir ara a d-tessiwev aman si tejmiât almi d axxam d$a yezga kan ubidun yenîev $ef weârur n yelli-s.

Ad teddu am win yettfarasen deg wussan-is. Akken tneûûef abrid temlal-d udem $er wudem uked Saâdiya n Ämer d$a tezwar-itt-id s westeqsi am win yeb$an ad iéer ma yella d acu ibedlen tini-yas :

- «Ihi timlilit ar ass lejmaâ».
- «Di lehna». Terra-yas Wiza s usevsu i wakken ad as-tekkes ccek lumaâna agu yellan deg wul n Wiza ur iâeîîel ara i$umm-d asevsu i d-yufraren $ef wudem-is.

Wiza teéra belli maççi d leêmala i izaden almi i tt-id-testeqsa. Teâlem yis-s belli aîas i tejbed i wakken a tejjten wexxam i tt-yu$en. Aîas i tessefra$ Saâdiya tini-yasen «ur tesâi ara imawlan bezzaf xfifet» lumaâna acemma ur yezmir a d-yessenfed zdat zzin n Wiza.

Wiza tem$i-d di âedni am tre$let ur yeéri êedd aéar-is. èran kan belli «tagi d Wiza n At Ämer baba-s $ef yisem-is i leêêunt acêal n têuna di Tizi». S lehdur-agi i tettqabal yemma-s kra n win yeb$an a tt-yerkev.

Baba-s di leâmer yelli am win tt-iwalan deg asmi i d-rsent Wiza aked yemma-s di ti$ilt-agi lumaâna zgan sellen yis-s. Wiza tezga-d awal fell-as $ef ssâaya-ines lumaâna di leâar di yella win iwalan yeîîef-as-d afus ne$ yedda-d $er tama-s.

Seg wasmi i d-teffe$ Wiza $er ddunit teooa-d lâella n yemma-s te$li-d $er irebbi n setti-s u sennig-sent ur tessin yiwen. Teddun wussan leêêun u setti-s tewwev leâfu n Rebbi u teggra-d Wardiya d yelli-s a tent yessegririb lêif.

Akken kan tdeqqer Wiza avar, tebda tikli $er loiran d$a wa a s-d-yefk taleqqimt wa a s-d-yefk aceîîiv. Akka i d-tekker Wiza s tleqmatin n medden âlaxaîer Wardiya ulansi i s-d-yekk kra.

Tudert-agi ur s-d-tekki ara seg wul i Wiza âlaxaîer twala tizya-s kullec yugar fell-asent ma d nettat di leâmer tessin tawant, tezga kan afus $ef lêenk.

Acukan, Wiza teêûa s zzin-is d$a d aya kan i d-yettarran deg-s tarwiêt, u tessaram ammer a d-yas wass ideg a tbeddel fell-as ddunit.

Tu$al-d Wiza si tala tufa bdan medden a d-tnejmaâen i wakken ad âerken lesfeno n taddart akken a d-beggnen tame$ra. Akken kan tekka di tewwurt bdant te$ratin a tseqsiqent.
tegzem-itt lefqeâ, allen-is ççurent-d d imeîîi, d$a tebra i usagem yellan $ef weârur-is deg wemnar u tuzzel $er texxamt-is i wakken ur d-tsell ara. Anda i s-yehwa teffer, ti$ratin flant imeééu$en-is u sya $er da ad tsel i yiwet tini-yas : - «Teffer iman-is i wakken ad tiâziz maççi muêal, d tislit».

Akken d-tekcem Wardiya temdel tawwurt deffir-s, Wiza texéer-itt am win yeb$an a d-yekkes taâkemt $ef weârur-is tini-yas : - «Teériv a yemma $as ini-yasent i tlawin i la iâerrken ad êebsent u ad nnejmaâent s ixxamen-nsent tame$ra ur tettili ara…».

Wardiya têulfa i yiman-is tulwat, d$a tebra (i yiman-is) $er lqaâa, tewwet âecra deg wudem-is u teqqim a thedder weêd-s am win yeshetrifen tini-yas : - «Anna$, seg wasmi i d-tlulev i uroa$ ass-agi a d-yawev, taggara teb$iv ad tessevsev deg-i lxalat. Anna$, nekk ferêe$ ini$-as ass-agi a kem-ééu$ am tneqlet taggara zi$en teggulev ur tessinev lehna… Tezgiv tettwaxeérev s îîerf n tiî, nekk ferêe$ ass-agi nni$-as a m-yu$al ccan. Anna$ a yelli, âudde$ fiêel ma mmeslaye$-kem, teériv belli akka llant akk dagi maççi d aêemmel i kem-êemmlent : ta terra-yi-d lxir i s-zzewre$, ta tewwi-tt-id tugdi n Rebbi, wwint-tt-id tismin i wakken ad tessenqed… Taggara teb$iv a sent-id-tekkev seg wul».

Tekfa Wardiya ashetref taggara am win tt-id-yessakin treûûa allen-is di yelli-s tini-yas : - «Ardemani, ini-yi-d ay$er teb$iv ad tessexsiv lferê-agi ? Aha-kem, b$i$ ad ére$...». Wiza yekkaw yimi-s, la itennev yiles-is, lehdur u$alen am tkurt deg yedmaren-is. Texéer Wiza di yemma-s a s-tiniv ass-agi i d-ldint wallen-is fell-as, twala lqedd-is teréa teâkemt, twala taglimt-is yess$er yiîij am ulemsir n lâid. Treûûa allen-is deg-s u twala belli êaca tarwiêt i mazal kan tenîev $er yi$es u a ten-yezzazal lêif $ef ddunit.

Wiza tasa-s la tqeddeê, ur teéri sani a terr udem-is; lumaâna twala belli iwata-tt-id kan a teîîef imi-s imi ula i s-ternu i yemma-s d$a tesfev imeîîawen-is tini-yas : - «Nni$-am-d ayagi alaxatar aîas n t$awsiwin i yi-ixuûûen di ssdeq-iw u ssetêa$ amek ara ten-id-sneâte$ zdat lberrani». Wardiya tger-d nnehta tini-yas : - «Anna$ a yelli tiniv-iyi-d kan d aâlaw ne$ d taqendurt i kem-ixuûûen ! Yak teériv a yelli, seg
wasmi i d-tlulev i m-d-bdi$ aheggi lumaâna imi ulac win i $- yezzewren kra nekk d ayagi i wumi ssawve$.

Wardiya teéra belli maççi d lehdur-agi ara s-yekksen anu$ni i yelli-s d$a tesleqqem-as :

- Aha tura kra sekra gar-a$ d useggas ad am-$erme$ ayen i kem-ixuûûen, ma d ass-agi efk-iyi lehna.

Wiza tebra i yeéri-s u thuzz aqerru-s tessusem. Ma d Wardiya tefhem belli lehna u tt-id-tsaê ara lumaâna tebded tidet u i yezmev fell-as ad tqabel.

Lahnawi bdant a d-keccment, yal adellaâ a t-vefrent te$ratin, tislit teâzel di texxamt ass-agi, ur ilaq ara a d-teffe$.

Sya $er da a d-teldi tewwurt n texxamt anda tu$al Wiza d$a ad tezwir ad tekcem Wardiya ssyin ad tevfer yiwet si tnebgawin i d-yusan akken ad tbeggen lehna-s i teslit.

Tezwar Wardiya u tevfer-itt Farruoa taoaret-nsent seg wasmi i d-rsent dagi. Terfed-d Wiza allen-is twala Farruoa tekcem-d s uvellaâ gar ifassen-is, yeççur almi yewwi tacwawt d$a t$awel tessers-it di tesga seg wakken yewwi fell-as limala. Wiza tfuk fell-as ddunit, ma d Farruoa tewwet $er daxel udellaâ teddem-d lêenni, ûûabun terna-d lkettan tini-yas i Wiza:

- Ayagi d lmektub-im.

Wiza kfan deg-s idammen, tué-d $er $ur-s, tekna-d aqerru-s, tsellem fell-as, tini-yas :

- Ad am-ibarek Rebbi.

£as ulamma tekker s ibeddi, lqaâa la tettezzi yis-s, temmekta-d asmi teggul Farruoa ur teênit ur d-tekcim Wiza axxam-is.

Ass-agi teb$a a s-tini ay$er ? D acu i s-d-tekkes ? Lumaâna yeggugem yiles-is siwa allen-is i la iceââlen. Farruoa tebra i uqerru-s tini-yas :

- Kullec d lmektub, ad ig Rebbi d ayen ara $-d-yawin yakk lehna.

Thegga-d iman-is a d-teffe$, tezwar-d Wardiya teldi-yas- d tawwurt ssyin tedda-d yid-s. Wiza kkawent tgecrar-is, sekra n tmara tuza almi d tasga d$a teqqim a testaâfu ma yella iwata-yas-d laâfu. Laâqel-is yenhewwal ur teéri anwa ara tessevlem, d Mesîafa ne$ d yemma-s ne$ d iman-is ne$ ammar d Wardiya ççan lexlawi, ççan izilan, i tt-yeooan tedda am lmal ur nesâi rrebg i wakken ad as-d-tawi acu ara teçç tameddit.
Mesîafa, wissen anida t-yu$ lêal ass-agi. Wissen ahat la izehhu ne$ ammar yen$a-t wugur ula d netta. Ardemmani, d acu n wugur ara yaven? Yak netta d Mesîafa At Äli ula d taddart ur tettnejmaâ ara ma yella ulac-iten.

Mesîafa asmi i d-yeldi allen-is yufa-d Wiza zdat-s, d taqamet yetthuzzu wavu n teméi, ur yezmir ara ad ye$leq allen-is ne$ ad yerr iman-is ur tt-iwala ara netta am wid akk yettawi îîmaâ yeârev a tt-iqerreb lumaâna dexxan yu$-d akk taddart. Wiza tu$al tettuswaâd s uvad. Lexbar yewwev Wardiya, d$a tebda la tettaîîaf di tlawin anta ara s-d-ijaben inexvaben. Wiza ur tewâir ara i lbiâ $as ur tesâi ara lwali, zzin-is i$umm leâyub-is. Lbarud yewwev ti$altin Wiza terkeb s axxam-is.

Azekka-nni ûûbeê, Wardiya truê a d-téer lexbar n yelli-s t$il a d-tu$al ad tewt agerz taggara tewwet tsusmi. Ssmana seg tâedda tme$ra, tu$al Wardiya $er yelli-s ma d At Ti$ilt Äli ttraoun melmi ara d-tu$al, ttraoun, ttraoun...

U$alen medden $er cc$el-nsen, $er wuguren-nsen lumaâna taraout tu$al-asen d tannumi. Äeddan wussan, âeddant smanat, yewwev waggur, assen deg wussan am wiyav ar yiv slan medden i dderz $er wexxam n Wardiya, yiwen ur d-yembawel ara seg wexxam-is: akken i tt-tcudd, a tt-tefsi. Üûbeê zik, yiwen, yiwen i la d-yeîîillin ad iwali d acu i yevran, lumaâna ufan-d êaca tiwwura la tent-yettemyeêbak wavu aked terbaât n yeqjan werâad ffi$ent u$en tasga.

Wa, yewhem, wa yeggugem. Ma d wid i wumi ur ruêent ara vefren later u ruêen ad steqsin. Ufan belli Wardiya, yerra-tt wedrar akin, tunag $er taddart n Laâzib, seddqen-as at lxir tazeqqa u tettili nettat d yelli-s. Teddun wussan, teddun lehmum yid-sen, ma d taqsiî n Wardiya mazal wid ara tt-id-ileqfen u mazal wid ara tt-yettabaâen i wakken ad éren amek i yas-gan wussan.

Tu$al-asent i Sut Ti$ilt At Äli am tmacahut $efwaydeg i d-ttnejmaâent a tt-id-ssiwlent mi ara yili ur d-ufint ara ayen i$ef ara mmeslayent akka i teddun wussan almi d asmi i slant belli terna teqcict $er Wiza. Steqsan $ef imawlan n teqcict u nnan-as win yeéran ad yini i win ur neéri. Ma yella d At Laâzib ahat a sent-tini Saâdiya:

- «Tagi d yelli-s n..., baba-s fell-as i leêêunt acêal n têuna di...».
# Tadyant n Si Sayd At Ccix¹

Ramdane Lasheb

Di lqern iâeddan, di Tgemmunt Ukerruc deg At Dwala, yella yiwen n ccix si taddart n At Buyeêya, ssawalen-as si Sayd at Ccix. I$ra $er ccix Muêend u Lmexttar deg wat Yenni u netta d si Muêend u Mêend myussanen d imeddukel. Si Muê Sayd-agi iqqar zik, akka i yihwa, imi d bab n ddraâ, yettâeddi wawal-is. Ttqadaôen-t nezzeh. D bab n lefûiê u yessefruy. Ircel seg wat Hlal, yu$ yelli-s n lêao Ali u Sayd. Ssawalen-as Feîîa n lêao Ali u Sayd, agur deg yigenni nettat di tmurt. Qqaren-d, sut At Hlal mi ara êejbent ur seââunt ara dderya, d ddeâwa n jedd-nsent. Seg tu$ ccix teêjeb, ur tesâi ara dderya. Myefken laâhed netta yid-s, netta yenna, ma temmutev d tamezwarut, ur rni$ fell-am tameîîut; nettat tenna-yas, ur rni$ fell-ak argaz.

Assen, di taddart nni, yiwen uqcic kksen-as tameîîut-is, wwin-tt imawlen-is: baba-s n teqcict d baba-s n uqcic nu$en amennu$ ameqran. Nutni myeêmalen seg wul maca mxalafen imawlen-nnsen. Wigi ceyyâen lejmaâ ad tt-id-rren, wid-nni ugin. Wigi suturen tiririt, widak berru, nutni mtawan, b$an ad ten-bvun. Lêan imôabven ad tt-id-erren, imawlen ugin. Imiren si Sayd at Ccix êemlent nezzeh din, ttqadaren-t aîas. Iîîef deg-s 1Tadyant n Si Sayd at Ccix akken i $- tt-id-yewwi Si Wyidir Medjad si Taddart Ufella.
uqcic, inna-yas ad iyi-tt-id-terrev. Iwwev ccix iêawet, iêawet, imawlan ugin. Igguni-t uqcic-nni alammi d-yeffe$, yenna-yas :

# 1. Amek akka a ccix ?

- Yenna-yas ccix : Beddel abrid a mmi, ugin imawlen. Mi t-iwala ccix inu$na, yenîaq $er-s, yenna-yas : têemlev taqcict-a !

- Wwah a ccix ! Ma êemle$-tt ! D tudert-iw !

- Yenna-yas ccix : Ruê ! ma ur n-tbedd ara weêd-s, nekk maççi d si Muê Sayd. Iwwev ccix s axxam, iddem-d azmam, yura-yas taêerzet, ifka-yas-tt, inna-yas âalqas-tt deg ubrid n tala u $ur-k wi k-id-ittwalin. Aqcic ixdem akken i s-d-yenna ccix. Mi d-tu$al teqcict si tala, terra srid $er wergaz-is. Iffe$ lexbar di taddart, ooan-ten weêd-sen.

Lêan acu lêan, di lexôif, ssawlen-as i ccix, ad d-yas, ad yaru i tmuvint. Yaf tameîîut iwumi ara yaru, isem-is Meêjuba. Iddem-d azmam, netta yettaru aqelmun alammi d allen. Yiwen wergaz iqqim-d $er tama-s, sin ddurin-d di tkenna, wayev yedduri-d addaynin. Win d-iqqimen $ef tama-s yeârev ad t-ixnaq s weâmam. Yerra-yas ixebbic ccix deg wudem-is. Rsen-d wid nni n tkenna, yerna-d win n waddaynin, ddmen-d taqabact, qeddôen-t.

Armi d iv, suff$en-t-id di tcekkaôt, sersen-t di tezôut n Amar u Buyeêya di ttnaûfa n taddart. Deg yiv-nni, iffe$-d yiwen, ad isefqed îîaôêa-s, yufa-d tacekkaôt deg ubrid, illi-tt, yufa d ccix i yemmuten. Yessaki-d lêao Muêend u Sliman, imiren d netta i d lamin n taddart ; isekker-d taddart, âazôen fell-as. Azekka-nni, nudan, ufan wid i t-in$an.

Si Muêend u Mêend tu$-it deg usammer n tmurt, iqqim di lqahwa. Ufan-t-id ixeddamen iêzen, iggugem. Nnan-as : d acu k-yu$en ? D acu i k-ixuûen ? Yella wi k-ivelmen ?

Si Muê yerra-d nnehta, yenna :

Yewwev-iyi-d lexber d uswid

Ul-iw yettnehdil-d

Lfahem irekb-it ll$ac

T$av-iyi tarrawt n Sid

Si Muê Sayd

Tamtilt-is beôôa ulac
I$der-it llqum lyazid

Wwten-t s lêid

Qedôen-t s uqabac

Iâawed, inna :

£edren cbab

Ur t-iklal

Tamtilt-ik ur d-tettili

Asmi ixeddem deg yir laâmal

Ileêêu s wuzzal

Anda i s-ihwa i yettili

Ma d tura itbaâ leêlal

Ittwaxdaâ deg uzal

Imzel timezla uêuli

Wwin-t-id s akal aberkan, imvel dinna. Ibedd gma-s, si Muê Crif at ccix $er uqerru-s, inna-yas : « Fki$ lahed, fki$-t i ôebbi, ur seîîle$ tamart, wala acebbub, ur ttekcime$ s axxam alamma rri$-d ttaô-ik ne$ rni$-n $ur-k» Lfuci $ef tayet-is, iffe$ d lmenfi.

Iruê uqcic-nni iwumi tettwakkes tmeîîut $er-s, yeggul, yenna-yas, ma ooi$-k, ara k-âiwne$. Assen, u$alen-d sin seg wid yen$an si Tizi-wezzu, si ccôaâ.

Rekben-d $ef yiserdyan deg wasif n lqennaô ger te$zut d wat Mesbaê, wa yewwet wa, wa yewwet wayev. £lin-d di sin.

Aqci-nni, n Tgemmunt ukerruc yerwel d asawen, yemnaâ. Ma d si Ccrif, yerra d akessar, $er t$ezza. Ikka-d fell-as laâyav, îfen-t-id wid ikerzen din, wwin-t $er lqayed.

Azekka-nni, wwin-t ixeyyalen yid-sen, êekmen-as sebâa n yiseggasen. Ssyin wwin-t $er Kayan. Yewwev $er din, isâedda xemsan yiseggasen, tamurt-is akk tekfa s lbiâ.

Yiwen wass tekker tmes deg uxxam n tmeîîut unemhal n lêebs, ala tettu$u, êuzen-as sin warraw-is : aqcic d teqcict îîsen deg uxxam-nni deg tekker tmes, wi ara d-yekksen arraw-is.

Yuzzel si Muê Crif, netta âaryan, yewwev, yufa-ten îîsen deg umetôaê. Yennev-iten-id di tfarûadit, iccud-iten-id s umrar, isers-iten-id. Ufan-ten urâad ukin. Te$li yemma-tsen, tefsex. Yers-d si
Ccrif, ibaôdiyen-is r$an akk, têelj-it ak tmes. Mi d-tefven tôumit-nni, tenna-yas : D acu i teb$iv ?

Yenna-yas si Muê Ccrif : d acu i b$i$ ! Akken teb$iv arraw-im i ten- b$i$ !

Tenna-yas trumit : “D tuf$a i teb$iv ad tef$ev ! Ma ur teffi$ev ara ! Ma ur u$ale$ ara deg umkan-ik ! Nekk maççi d leflentega! Truê, tura fell-as, tenna-yas argaz-agi yen$a yiwen, icfaâ sin. D$a suff$en-t-id.

Tameîîut-nni n si Sayd at Ccix truê-d s axxam n baba-s. La d-kkaten medden $er-s akken ad tezwej, nettat tugi. Tmekta-d laâhed i tefka i urgaz-is. Seg la d-kkaten ixxamen ilhan, inna-yas baba-s, ad tzewjev ne$ ad kem-selme$. Iêers-itt, iwwet $er-s lêao Belqasem, yu$-itt :

A sidi lêao Aâli

N$il-ik d argaz lâali

Tefkiv yelli-k i wakli

Asmi yesla si Muêend u Mêend, yewwi asefru, yenna-yas :

Awwah a lmut d-yettassen

£er lbaz meééiyen

Wagi d lwaâd Rebbi

Zwao-ik a t-id-xeîîben

Iâdawen-ik ferêen

Kul wa ansi d-yeîîili

A sidi Amar u Brahemâ

Aql-a$ netwehhem

Yeâreq-a$ ubrid ad nawi.

Teqqim $er lêao Belqasem d acu teqqim, ssyin truê-d, yu$-itt Muêend at Allal, yiwen umarkanti n at Meêmud. Teqqim d acu teqqim, di$en truê-d.

Ar taggara yu$-itt si Ëmed u Larbi si taddart n At Buyeêya. Netta yemmut d amezwaru, ma d nettat temmut d tam$art di lgirra-nni n 54.
# Tidet yeskiddiben

# Youcef Achouri

«Ur zmireɣ ara a d-ssfehmeɣ ambiddel i yeḍran yid-s! Ur zmireɣ ara daɣen ad as-d-jebdeɣ awal, ul yeččur, tagnit teḍyeq.»

Ttalint-tt-id nnhati n tidiwin yerɣan, d tawḥidt, ur tufi win iwumi ara teḥku tabaḍnit i ixemten acḥal aya deg texzant n wul-is. U yerna tura aql-aɣ deg lweqt anda win i wumi teḥkiḍ ad yettaḍṣa fell-k. Ayen i tt-yuɣen, mačči d ayen i ḥekkun medden, imi d tabaḍnit ger-as d win teɛna temsalt. Ul-is yesderduf si zdaxel i d-yesṭebṭub, iɛewwel a d-yerẓ idmaren-is akken a d-yeffeɣ ɣer berra.

Di tazwara, tella tettcukku deg-s, lameɛna tura ulac din ccek; tidet tban-d am yiṭij d-yeṭṭilin yal ṣṣbeḥ ẓran-t akk medden. I wacu, d acu n ssebba imi tt-yeɛzel deg wusu, s teɣzi n wacḥal d aggur aya?! Anda llan wussan-nni n zik? Anda-t lḥamu-nni-ines n zik? Anda llan iḥulfan d ccuq-nni-ines n zik? Anda d-gran wawalen-nni ẓiden ḥlawen? Anda-tt leḥmala d tayri-nni n zik? Anda llan rrwayeḥ, d tmelsa ifazen i d as-yesnum? Anda yella wusu-nni yeḥman, anda yettḥar melmi ara d-yekcem s axxam?!

Tura ibeddel mačči d winna tessen yakan! Yuɣal d wayeḍ, tura zrin acḥal d aseggas, segmi ten-yecrek wusu n leḥlal, tecrek-iten ula d tarwa!
Zzwaǧ-nsen yella-d d zzwaǧ n tayri, yerbeḥ, qbel ad myezwaǧen, llan myussanen. Ddren yiwet tmacahut n tayri i ten-yewwin ɣer yiwen umaḍal n tirga, ssyen, targit-agi-nsen teffeɣ ɣer tafat, zewǧen. Kemmlen di tayri-nni, werǧin nnuɣen, werǧin d-msukkasen. Tezga tayri-nni am umassaɣ ger-asen, yal yiwen deg-sen yettnadi amek ara yessefreḥ wayeḍ, amek ara yeddu di lebɣi n wayeḍ.

Iseggasen ttɛeddin zerben am waḍu, leḥmala-nsen werǧin tenqis, simmal tettfukti, simmal tgemmu, alarmi uɣalen medden ttawin-ten d amedya!

Netta, yalla ixeddem d anemhal deg yiwet tkebbanit tameqqrant. S yisem-is d anemhal amatu n tkebbanit-agi, teṭṭuqqet fell-as lxedma; tikkwal ur yesɛi ara ula d ussan i westeɛfu, tikkwal yettuḥettem fell-as ad iɛeṭṭel di lxedma alarma d iḍ. Qrib yal ass akken. Acu kan tannumi-ines ur ibeddel deg-s wacemma. Mazal taftilt-nni n tayri tettreqriq deg wul-ines, nettat si tama-s ur tbeddel ara, d tin n zik, d tin n tura. Yal mi ara iɛeṭṭel deg lxedma neɣ yella kra n ccɣel i t-yeṭṭfen, ini yessawel-as-d di tilifun akken ad yettwennes xerṣum s ṣṣut-ines, acku mi tt-yeẓra s wallen-is neɣ yesla i ṣṣut-is, yettruḥu-yas ɛeggu n lxedma, tettnefsusi fell-as tɛekkemt. Yella yal mi ara d-yekcem yettales-as-d amek yesɛedda ass-ines di lxedma. Ur iteffer fell-as kra, ama meẓẓiy, ama meqqer.

Tesɛa akk isalan i ilaq a ten-tẓer ɣef wergaz-is. Teḥṣa ula s wayen itezzin deg uqerru-ines d wayen iḍarrun di lbiru-ines, acku tikkwal yettcawar-itt ula di lumur n lxedma-ines.

Ul-nsen yezga yelli, wa ur yesɛi tabaḍnit ɣef wayeḍ. Ddren amzun d yiwen wemdan! S yisem-is d anemhal amatu, tikkwal yettinig ɣer tmura n lbarrani deg ukatar n umahil-ines.

Mi ara s-tessewjed tabalizt-ines, yal tikkelt tettuqam-as tabrat di kra n leǧyub n tmelsa-ines. Tabrat n tayri, yettawi-tt yid-s d aɛwin. Ula d netta daɣen, mi yekker ad iruḥ, yettaǧǧa-yas-d tabrat s tuffra di kra n teɣmert n wexxam.

Mi yal yiwen deg-sen yufa tbarat n wayeḍ, mi tt-yeɣra a tt-yeffer, akken ad as-iɛiwed taɣuri. Mi ara ten-tessemlil teswiɛt, ayen akk ara yexdem deg wass tameddit mi d-yekcem s asensu ad as-t-id-iɛiwed di tilifun, ad yemmeslay yid-s qbel ad yeṭṭeṣ. Yal iḍ akken alarmi d ass ideg ara d-yuɣal ɣer tmurt.
D acu yeḍran?! Ttezzem deg yiman-is. Yella kra i d as-tesxaṣṣ? Yella kra ideg testehza? Ma yella kra i d as-tekkes? Ma yella kra ideg t-teḍlem?

Texdem leḥsab-is ur yelli kra, ur telli ssebba ara t-yeǧǧen ad ibeddel akk annect-a! Ad ibeddel tikli-ines, ad ibeddel tannumi-ines di setta (6) wagguren-agi ineggura. Yal ass ttezzem deg yiman-is, yal ass testeqsay deg yiman-is. Tettnadi ɣef tmental i t-yeǧǧan ad ibeddel, agemmuḍ yiwen-is.

«…Anda yella bu wul-nni leqqaqen? Anda tella leḥnana-nni, anda-tt tayri-nni? Ala, d awezɣi, ur cukkeɣ ara a tt-yexdem!»

Tebda tettmeslay d yiman-is, ur teẓri sani ara tt-tessufeɣ taluft-agi d-yerzan fell-as, ur teẓri amek ara ffɣen igemmaḍ-ines. Tuɣal tettwali-t amzun d lweḥc! Tettwali deg wudem-is ḥaca tebrek: «abrid-agi d-yuɣ wergaz-a, ur yessufuɣ ara ɣer liser! Ih, a zzman ideg d-negra, leḥlu yeqqel d lqareṣ, tidet teqqel teskiddib, tafat teqqel d ṭṭlam; Tayri teqqel d nneqma. Tezdeg teqqel tumes. D tidet ibeddel mačči d cwiṭ! Idewwer udem-is fell-i, nebla ccek tella kra n tin i t-yewwin deg webrid n lkaf. Nebal ccek tella kra n tin i t-iḥewṣen, imi di tallit-agi ideg nella kullci yezmer a d-yeḍru. Netta yebɣa ajdid, ma d nekk yerra-yi di rrif am uɣerbal aqdim».

Mi tenheq a d-tebru i tala: « Amek i ibeddel beɛd amecwar d-nelḥa jmiɛ, ziɣemma yeskiddib fell-i! Ih, ɣef nekk yellan d maɣu, ɣef nekk yellan d nniya. Ziɣ netta yattaḍṣa fell-i, nekk ur d-wwiɣ s lexbar! Ah, a win yeẓran d anta-tt tagi i t-yessegrarben, amek i texdem? Nebla ccek tɣurr-it s thuska-ines. Anda tt-yessen? Anda tt-yemlal? Ahat si tid i ixeddmen-yid-s?... Maca, tid ixeddmen yid-s di lbiru ssneɣ-tent merra, akken ma llant zewjent s yexxamen-nsent, acḥal d abrid i ččant tagella d lemleḥ n wexxam-iw! Ahat si tid i d as-yettilin? -Tebda tḥetteb-itent-id s yismawen-nsent akken ma llant- Ula d nutenti zewjent, s yexxamen-nsent! D awezɣi ad tili si tid ixeddmen yid-s, neɣ si tid i d as-yettilin. D anta-tt tagi ihi? D anta-tt tagi ihi?! »

Asteqsi-agi, yuɣal d asentel n yal ass, imi tura tella tin izedɣen ul n wergaz-agi. Asteqsi-agi, icewwel-itt, yecɣeb-itt alarmi tuɣal tekreh iman-is.

Teqqim weḥd-s ala nettat d rray-is, tettxemmim anda-tt tifrat. Tesla i zzhir n tkerrust n wergaz-is teḥbes-d ɣer tewwurt. Teǧǧa akk ixemmimen-ines di rrif, imi d-yekka si tewwurt, tessaked-it.
seg tṣegnint alarmi d tifednin. Zik, d netta i d as-d-yeqqaren d acu ara d-texdem d imensi, tura ur d-yeclig deg wacemma, yeqqel sellaw am yemɣi yeṭṭef uɣurar!

«...Ahat itett-d imensi si berra, netta d tmeɛzuzt-ines ! Anwa i yeẓran, d acu ara t-yeṭṭfen ur tt-ixeddem ara?! Deg yimi a la tuččit, mačči am zik d aɛemmec kan i yettɛemmic iman-is. Zik awal-ines ḥaca ɣef nnwal, ayen yebɣu niwleɣ-t-id yettcekkir-it-id. Ass n wass-a, s kra din iruḥ! Iiih! ... I txeddem ddunit taɣeddart, anda yella tqaṣur-nni-ines, anda yella wawal-nni aẓidan? Tura ad as-tiniḍ awal s yedrimen i t-id-yettaɣ, neɣ ad as-tiniḍ d agugam! Yuɣal a d-neṭqen yeɣraben n wexxam ar netta xaṭi! Zik alarma yeṭṭeṣ ɣef ukersi ara iruḥ s usu ad igen, ma d tura yuɣal am ucewcew mi yečča imensi a t-tafeḍ yekcem usu. Yal mi ara d-yekcem qqareɣ deg wallen-is am win yebɣan ad iyi-d-yini kra. Acuɣer ur yesɛi ara tabɣest a t-id-yini, acuɣer yettarra awal ɣer daxel?! Alarmi d tura i ḥṣiɣ, d tagi i d lɛada n yergazen, ḥettben iman-nsen zdat tlawin-nsen. Ahat yessetḥa, neɣ ur yesɛi ara tabɣest a t-id-yini akka srid udem s udem! Tidet qerriḥen mačči menwala yezmer a tt-id-yessiwel…

Tura, ilaq-iyi a d-afeɣ abrid ara yi-ssiwḍen ɣer tidet s uqamum-iw. Ilaq ad ssiwḍeɣ akeddab ar tawwurt, ilaq ad ẓreɣ tameṭṭut-agi-ines tamaynut.

Isteqsiyen-agi zgan deg wallaɣ-is, tiririt fell-asen mazal-itt tɛelleq. Zarlfal “de temps en temps” tessawal ɣer lbiru anda ixeddem akken ad tẓer ma dinna i yella. Yal mi ara tessiwel a t-taf dinna, netta ireffed, nettat ur thedder ara. Tsell-as kan mi d as-d-yeqqar “alu, alu”… nettat ad tegzem fell-as nebla ma texṣer fell-as awal.

Turǧa azal n tsaɛet tɛawed tessawel, tikkelt-agi mačči d netta i d as-d-yerran, d axeddam-nniḍen i d-yerran deg wemkan-is.

Testeqsa-t ɣef wergaz-is yerra-yas-d:

- Tura kan i yeffeɣ si lbiru.

Tessawel-as ɣer umafus (tilifun n lǧib ) tenna-yas:

- Anda telliḍ? Nettat, tella tettraǧu ad yeskiddeb fell-as ad as-yini aqlih di lbiru. Imi s-d-yerra yenna-yas:
Ur yelli din ccek, iban am zzit ɣef waman. Iruḥ ad yečč imensi netta d teɛzizt-is. Ul-is idemmek yeččur yebɣa ad ifelleq: «Ah ya yiwen uxeddaɛ, ay anekkar, ur k-ttsamaḥeɣ ara…d awezɣi ad tselkeḍ seg ifassen-iw, a k-id-feḍḥeɣ, ad ɛerriɣ i tidet am llufan mi ara s-tekkseḍ tattalt. A d-iban uberriḍ-ines. Tɣelṭeḍ di leḥsab-ik, tɣileḍ mazal-iyi d nniya, tɣileḍ d tabuheyyuft, xas ɛiwed leḥsab-ik yexṣer! Ẓriɣ kullci, ɣef tiṭ-iw kullci, d kečč i d nniya, d kečč i d abuheyyuf». Idammen-is rekkmen am useqqi di teccuyt, ger wallen-is tettwali ḥaca tebrek. Amzun akken yella win s-yerran ccac ɣef waṭṭiwen-is.

«…D awezɣi ad idireɣ yid-s, d wezɣi ad idireɣ d wergaz yecban wagi seddaw yiwen n ssqef. D awezɣi ad aɣ-d-tḥerr yiwet tewwurt ɣer daxel! Tura yegra-yi-d kan ad ssilɣeɣ arraw-nneɣ, a ten-heggiɣ akken ad qeblen beṭṭu ger-i d baba-tsen. Lameɛna qlil akkan wannect-a, ilaq ad ẓreɣ tagi iḥewwṣen irgazen. Ilaq a tt-id-feḍḥeɣ».

S kra yekka yiḍ, ur d-iris ccfer ɣef gma-s. Tettxemmim amek ara tandi tifexxet ara ten-id-yeṭṭfen, ara ten-id-ifeḍḥen. Ṣṣbeḥ zik mi yeffeɣ wergaz-is ɣer lxedma, teḍfer-it deffir. Yal ass akken ansi yekkes aḍar a t- terr nettat, akken ad-tẓer anda akka yexdem lɛecc-is. Anda akka yesɛa axxam-nniḍen. Tuɣal tettruḥu ɣer tkebbunay yessekruyen tinezduɣin, tebɣa ad as-teffeɣ seg wexxam akken meqqar ad as-teǧǧ listeɛ netta d tmeɛzuzt-is.

Tameddit, mi d-yekcem testeqsa-t ɣef wahil n lxedma-ines uzekka. Azekka ad iliɣ di lbiru alarma d 18: 00, imir sɛiɣ yiwet temlilit d ineɣmasen deg wexxam n tɣamsa, taneggarut-agi ur ẓriɣ ara ɣef wacḥal ara tt-fakeɣ!

Ɣur-s nettat, teddez tebrez, azekka a t-texdem d ccɣel. Azekka-nni qbel 18: 00, tella deg yiwet tkerrust tettqabal-d tawwurt tameqqrant n tkebbanit ideg ixeddem wergaz-ines. Takerrust-agi, tekra-tt-id akken a tt-tessexdem deg wahil i d-thegga. Di ṭunubil, ad as-tiniḍ di ssilun i tella! Teṭṭef-itt tergigit, tidiwin, tugdi…lameɛna deg wul-is teqqar-as: « D tagnit ur nlaq ara a tt-sruḥeɣ, ilaq ad ssiwḍeɣ ɣer yeswi». Xas ulamma iḍul uraǧu, ddqiqa ɣur-s d aseggas!

Cwiṭ kan attah telli-d tewwurt tameqqrant n tkebbanit, twala takerrust n wergaz-is yefka-tt-id wemnar ɣer berra. Teḍfer-it
deffir, ansi yekka nettat deffir-s, azniq yettak-it i wayeḍ. Si tezribt ɣer tezribt: «Ah a yiwen ukeddab, tesɛiḍ timlilit d tɣamsa! Wagi mačči d abrid yettawin ɣer wexxam n tɣamsa. Ah ya yiwen uxeddaɣ, a yiwen unekkar! Tḥareḍ melmi ara tawḍeḍ tejjmeḍ-tt degmi akka tzerbeḍ tikli! »

Iteddu, yewweḍ ɣer yiwet lbaṭima d taɛlayant, yeḥbes yers-d si tkerrust-ines yekcem si tewwurt, yuli: « Ah, ziɣ dagi i tella tinna iheggṣen irgazen! Dagi i d as-yekra axxam, si leɛḍil ar d as-yaɣ lbila! »

Netta yekcem, nettat deffir-s. Twala-t yeḥbes deg wunnig wis-rebɛa (4), yesṭebṭeb deg tewwurt n yiwen wexxam. Nettat, yuɣ-itt lḥal deg wunnig wis-tlata (3). Tuɣal-d ɣer uɛessas-nni yellan ɣer tewwurt, testeqsa-t:

- D anwa i d axxam n Yeḥya? Yerra-yas-d:
- Dagi, di labaṭima-agi ulac anezdaɣ isem-is Yeḥya.
- Ur skiddib ara felli, s wallen-iw i t-walaɣ mi yekcem ɣer waxxam, deg wunnig wis-4.
- Unnig wis-4 llan deg-s 2 yexxamen; amezwaru d axxam n si Yidir, ma yella d wayeḍ d axxam n Dduktur Meẓyan.
- Xas ur ttḥewwis ara amek ara yi-tesɣelṭeḍ. ɛni yefka-yak lmelḥ ufus?! Iweṣṣa-k a t-tṣetreḍ. Ula d ayen ẓrant wallen-iw ad iyi-teskiddbeḍ! Nniɣ-ak walaɣ-t s wallen-iw imi yekcem s axxam, deg wunnig wis-4!

Ur tumin ara aɛessas-nni, tuli s unnig wis-4. Deg wunnig wis-4, tufa dinna 2 yexxamen, yiwen ɣef uẓelmeḍ wayeḍ ɣef uyeffus, tqerreb mliḥ ɣer tewwurt n wexxam yellan ẓelmeḍ, temḥeṣ mliḥ tira yellan ɣef tewwurt, tufa yettwaru “axxam n mass Iɣil Yidir”, tuɣal-d ar tewwurt yellan yeffus tufa yura deg-s “ axxam n Sliman Ugemmun”. Tura newweḍ-d ar ɣur-s: “yuker ḥeḍreɣ, yeggull umneɣ”!

lameɛna nettat tesseḥreṣ d akken tameddit-agi a tt-tefru, akken tebɣu tili teswiḥt, akken bɣun ffɣen-d igemmaḍ-ines.

Temmeɣ, tessers aḍad-ines ɣef tqeffilt n nnaqus, nnaqus yendeh, cwiṭ kan akka attah telli-d tewwurt-nni, tban-d yiwet teqcict d tacebḥant, d tamelḥant, tzad di thuska. Ad tili ger 19 d 20 iseggasen di leɛmer-is:

- Azul. I d as-d-tenna teqcict-nni.
- Azul a yelli, d wagi i d axxam n Si Yeḥya?

- Ala a xalti, tɣelṭeḍ di tansa.

“Ihi axeddaɛ-agi deg wexxam-agi-nniḍen, axxam-agi aẓelmaḍ i yella”. I s-tenna deg yiman-is. «Nebla ccek, d isem ukerray amezwaru i yeǧǧa ɣef tewwurt, akken ad iyi-yesseɣleḍ, a faqu!». Dɣa tesṭebṭeb ɣef tewwurt-nni, Ata yeffeɣ-d yiwen wergaz, ad yesɛu ger 50 d 55 iseggasen deg usemmud-is, dɣa tenna-yas:

- Si Yidir dagi i yella ɣur-wen?

- Ur ssineɣ ara Si Yidir-agi, tɣelṭeḍ di tansa.

- Lemmer ahat…

- Nniɣ-am xaṭi !

Dɣa yerra-d tawwurt ɣef wudem-is, tuɣal tewhem, anda-tt tifrat, teṭṭef aqerruy-is tettxemmim. «Awwah, d awezɣi ad uɣaleɣ s axxam alamma sskefleɣ-d tidet». Tegzem-itt di rray-is, ur tettruḥu ara alamma tefra-d ccɣel-is, tuɣal tuli ɣer wunnig wis-setta, tessikid-d ssyinna, tedduri akken ur tt-id-iẓer yiwen. «Ur ttruḥuɣ ara ssya, ɣas ulamma ad sɛeddiɣ iḍ dagi, alamma d ṣṣbeḥ».

Ismektiyen-ines rran-tt ɣer deffir, smektan-tt-id s wussan n zzhu, tayri d rrezg i sɛeddan di sin. Temmekta-d ussan n tesnawit, n tesdawit, acku akken i llan qqaren alammi i d-tedda ɣur-s d tislit. Tuɣal tettxemmim ɣef uzekka n warraw-is ara d-yekkren d igujilen, ɣas ulamma lwaldin-nsen mazal-iten d imudduren: « Ah ya ddunit, ideg i d-negra! »

Si ddqiqa ar tayeḍ, tessikid ɣer ssaɛa i yellan deg ufus-is alammi tt-tufa qrib ad taweḍ d 22:00, netta mazal-it ar daxel, tsenned ɣer lḥiḍ, teqqim tettraǧu. Seg wakken teɛya, truḥ am wakken yettsawam-itt-id yiḍeṣ. Lexbar alammi d-tesla ar wunnig wis-tlata n sin yergazen heddren gar-asen, yiwen ṣṣut ur tessin ara bab-is, ma d wayeḍ teɛqel-it, mebla ccek, d ṣṣut n Si Yeḥya.

Dɣa, ters-d s lemɣawla, d tazzla, Si Yeḥya ur t-id-telḥiq ara, iṣubb-d, twala argaz-nni i s-yellin tawwurt yuɣal ar daxel.

Teẓdem ɣef tewwurt-nni, tekkat deg-s s ifassen d iḍarren, tettsuɣu:

- Llit tawwurt ay iḍan neɣ a wen-d-awi imsulta.
Telli-d tewwurt, yeffeɣ-d wergaz-nni yesɛan ger 50 de 55 iseggasen deg usemmud-is.

- Anda-tt tmeṭṭut-agi i iḥewwṣen irgazen? Nettat tettayzag trekkem.

Tekcem s axxam-nni, tufa-n snat tlawin, yiwet ad tesɛu ger 40 d 50 iseggasen, ma yella d tayeḍ meẓẓiyet deg usemmud!

- Iih, d kemm i d tameṭṭut-is tamaynut, a taɣeddart, a tin iḥewwṣen irgazen.

Teẓdem fella-s, temmeɣ-as ɣef temgerṭ akken a tt-texneq, taqcict terwel ɣer baba-s akken a tt-iḥudd.

Baba-s n teqcict, iqubel-itt-id s leɛqel, yeɛreḍ amek ara tt-id-yerr ar leɛqel-is, akken ad tethedden.

- Tebɣiḍ a d-tiniḍ Si Yeḥya ?

- Ih, ay udem uxeṣṣar.

- D acu-yam-t ?

- D argaz-iw, thuddem axxam-iw, tesdermem ddunit-iw. Zik, qbel a ken-yissin, nella nettidir, di rrezg ar yiri.

- Rreyyeḥ, thedden, aha ssefhem-iyi-d kullci, ales-iyi-d tamacahut-im; aql-i yid-m a kem-ɛiwneɣ, ur ttagad, ɣas ma yella kra ixeṣren a t-nṣeggem, aha rreḥ.

- Xaṭi, mačči s areyyeḥ-inek i d-usiɣ, usiɣ-d akken a ken-id-feḍḥeɣ. Ur tettagadem ara Rebbi?! Yewwi-ken ṭṭmeɛ, acuɣer ur testeqsayem ara ma yesɛa tawacult neɣ xaṭi?! Acuɣer ur testeqsayem ara ma yesɛa tameṭṭut, weqbel ad as-tefkem yelli-twen?!

Dinna, dduktur Si Yidir, yemḥeṣ tamsalt, yewwi-d lexbar s wacu i itezzin deg uqerru n tmeṭṭut-agi.

- Lameɛna ur d as-nefki ara yelli-tneɣ ! Ur yelli d aḍeggal, ur t-nnuseb !

- Berka tikerkas, ur skeddib! S wallen-iw i t-walaɣ mi d-yekcem, mi yeffeɣ seg wexxam-agi.

- Ayagi d tidet!

- I kečč, acuɣer i tnekreḍ sgellin mi k-id-steqsaɣ fell-as ?

- Nniɣ-am reyyeḥ, thedden, tura ad am-d-ssfehmeɣ tamsalt s ttbut; Nekk d amejjay di taɣult n tarrawt, argaz-im yettdawi ɣur-i, ata qrib 6 wagguren-aya, aṭṭan-is d ɛeggu di tuzuft.

- Acuɣer deg wexxam i yettdawi mačči dila clinique-inek?!

- Argaz-im mačči d menwala, yerna d netta i d-yessutren deg-i.
akken ad yettdawi ɣur-i deg wexxam. Nekk qebleɣ, awi-d kan ad yeḥlu, d wagi i d iswi n yal amejjay i yettqadaren tawuri-ines. Ɣur-i kif-kif, atah ukaram-ines ma tebɣiḍ a t-teɣreḍ, deg-s tislaḍ akk d ikayaden, ax a t-teɣreḍ ax!

- Teṭṭerḍeq d imeṭṭi, ɣlin-d seg wallen-is annect iqerqac, imiren terreqreq, teɣli ur teẓri anda i tedda. Mɛawanen fella-s refden-tt s ameṭreḥ, ssawlen i wergaz-is Si Yeḥya:

- Alu! Si Yeḥya?! Uɣal-d tura, atan tameṭṭut-ik dagi ɣur-neɣ, tenṭer!
# Tadyant n Tafat d U$ilas

# Nora Mahi

YIDIR: nuda$ igenni tamurt anda ara kem-wali$, acêal aya ur n-tûubbev $er wexxam nwi$-as yella wayen i kem-yu$en, ne$ d laêoubegga i têeobev!

Ëêeq Rebbi ar d-iban wemkan-im mayfat ur kem-nwala ara.

# TAFAT

dayen a yidir wellah ar d lweqt iyi-tt-yekksen, jidatenîer di lahlak ur numin ara ad tt-id-yaf unebdu agi id-iteddun, yemma waêd-s ur as-t-zmir ara, $ef waya i nekkini kan imi t-id-yewwi lêal, ur tetett ara ala ayen i as-nessemcaê am llufan, lmakla ines akk nezza-as-tt am waman akken ad as-tshil i wseblaâ.

YIDIR: d ayen umne$ s wazal inem deg wexxam nne$... mazal ur d-ifukk ara awal tafat tebda yettbeddil wudem-is ûûifa; yella d amellal, yu$al d aweôdi yu$al d azegga$ am toiêbuî ne$ am tewzit (d tadellaât yewwan mliê).

Tafat tekker-dwaêd-s akk d sin watma-s yiwen yuger-itt s (5iseggasen) ma d wayev yuger-itt s (03 iseggasen), seg wass mi id-kker tella tetturar akk d watmaten-is d sin warraw n xalt-is wiss ssin d tizya n gma-s nni amenzu ismawen nsen (yidir, a$ilas) kkren-d tturaren akkenni, arrac agi acku ur asen d-sâi ara yemmatsen taqcict ssaâezzen Tafat d ayen izaden, di$enna nettat tessen amek i tessiêmil iman-is, acku terna iles êlawen i ûûifa nni.
ines : taqeddet as-tiniv d tancirt, taksumt d tiqit uyefki, tiîd aâeqqa uzemmur, ta$enjuôt xas kkes yis asennan, taqemmuct d taxatemt, tammast d ameqyas, taqejjiôt d tawaract n wudi, rnu d tagrurzant. Lêaûun ala ayen nettwali deg isura ne$ tzemrev ad iniv d albaâv itt-yebna akken tt-yebna di d texmam ines,imi-s ala ameslay éiden id-itef$en deg-s : ur yessin ala ne$ âegze$, ala yirbaê, anâam, anef d nekk ara yekren, ulac u$ilif… Ihi $ef wakka ulac win ara yeslen i tamment nni d wudi id-itef$en di tcenfirin ines ur tt-id-yettmenni ara, ad as-isel amer d yiwen wass; ma d ayen nniven ttwalin-t yebâed akken yebâed igenni $ef tmurt, maca maci d awez$i win tt-iwalan yeqqaô-as ahat ammer !

Seg wasmi i d-kren xedmen ala ayen s wayes ara âeddin zdat Tafat, zgan ttna$en bbuger asen anwa akked ara teqqim ne$ akked ara turar, lêaûun Yidir d U$ilas u$alen am wemcic d u$erda ala imen$i ; d acu yezga d A$ilas i yettawin tama n wadda, d ameéyan rnu seg wass mi d-yekker d amevâafu acku iêuza-t une$lul ( ur yewwiv ara agur fell-as tekcem-d fell-as yiwet n teslit netat tâelleq-d ifzimen n lfeîîa, d$a seg wassen ur yufi iman-i). Ur as-tenni ara yemma-s ad yidir almi as-tenna i Öebbi acu i ak-xedme$ ?

Lahlak deg id-yerfed idis ad yaven wayev, tiî d-yersen fell-as mi yewwev $er yiv yettarra-tt ala i tu$wisin, ur yeggan ur yesgan alma tezzi-yas jida-s lêaoa ur as-teooi di lmelê, aman, imeûlaê, ad tektil irkulli i d wamek ara yeqqen allen-is ; tewwev-d yiwet n tallit yemma-s taâya deg weqcic agi amaâlal, ur teooi îbib wala îîaleb,yessawev-itt lêal teîîalab di Öebbi ad t-yejmeâ akken ad tethenni.

Ma d Yidir llah ibarek si zik yeohed,ilul-d yekmel, hraw yi$es-is, mi yemmed d netta i yeîîurcen $ef U$ilas yessen amek id-yettawi amur-is amer ad t-id-yekkes deg imi n yizem, mi yexdem kra n tderdurt yessen amek ara yesâeddi iman-is ; ur as-teqqarev ara dyiwet n  tâebbuî i ten id-yesâan ; Yidir tezga teqqaô-as yemma-as : « wahme$ amek in-tsemdev 09 waguren deg uâebbuv-iw,ur d-ffi$ev ara meqbel lawan » ; aqcic d tifelfelt A$ilas simmal yettem$uô, simmal yettishil, yettu$al di rrif ala $ef Tafat id-yettfakka awal.

Ass mi kecmen $er lakul wa yettiêmil ma yfat iâeîîel wayev ur d-yusi ara akken ad yeqqim d netta $er Tafat, almi u$alen watmaten-is ur asen d-cliâ ara acku tteklen-tt $ef warraw n xalt nsen ; mi iten twala xalt nsen zgan d imen$i tferq asen nnuba akken ad ttawin Tafat di lakul ; ma yfat
tedda-d d U$ilas ad temmeslay d win as-yahwan ad taêbes $er win teb$a ; ma yella tedda-d d Yidir win tt-id-imuqlen d amuqel ad ineggez fell-as ad t-yexnaq ; yessawev-it lêal almi yu$al xasmaci d nnuba-s ad tafev yusa-d ad iâas ma yella win d-yemmeslayen yid-s ur tettaki nettat d U$ilas alma yeffe$-d wissen seg wansi ad t-yesseglilez di tmurt mi yekfa yid-s ad yu$al $er U$ilas ad ikemmel ayen yeqqimen ; ad as-d-yekkes Tafat ad tt-id-yawi seg ufus imiren ad ibeddel mavi udem : « tezriv ala kem i nesâa d tugdi i ttagade$ fell-am, la tettwaliv arrac tura d lewêuc kan akka i kem-id-ttgabaôen, ma yefka we$yul-ina deg-m afus nekkini ur tettake$ ara ».

Yekker ad iôuê $er lâeskeô yugad $ef Tafat as-yezzi gma-s d$a ad ttmal $ur-s iôuê $er gma-s n Tafat amenzu iâemmeô-astaqeôôut-is wisen s wacu, almi tt-id-yaêbes di lakul ; ur tefhim tigert acu i d ssebba wala anwa i as-yeccemcucden lekdubat $er tqeôôut-is, maca ur terri ara mavi $er Yidir. Inîaq-d fell-as U$ilas yessawev-it$er lêiv, yenna-yas : « ula d keçç xas ulamma d mmi-s n xalti urd-ttas ara $er wexxam ma yella ulac win yellan ne$ ur d-ddi ara xalti, la tettwaliv Tafat tu$al d tameîîut s ûûifa-inna-ines ula d keçç yezmer ad ak-i$ur cciîan… ». A$ilas yeffe$-d seg wexxam ur yaâqil abrid, amer tlli yis tmurt attan teseblaâ-it.

Aqcic yeffe$-d ur yaâqil abrid, srid $er zagu anda iêemmel ad yeqqim $er wasif-nni dinna yesregrugen deg waman yeqqim $er yiwet n tasaft tella dinna allen-is ttazzalent akken ttazzalen waman-nni ; yaêûa ad icedhi udem n Tafat, tura ad tu$l tudert ies ad tt-idel îlam xas ulamma d azal deg yella. Yidir, mi yesla i cce$l agi ur yumin ara ayen imi yesla lamaâna ifukk anner n lfeôê acku yekkes A$ilas d ugur xarsum ar ass mi ara d-yu$al.

Taqcict xaôben-as wussan, tu$al d taqcct n wxxam, ayen akk te$ôa wwin-t waman d asawen, arraw n xalt-is yiwen iôuê $er lâeskeô wayev yeggul deg-s gma-s ur d-ikeççem s axxam nsen, deg imi baâden fell-as din i taêûa $er wumi i yeccev wul-is, anwa i yeb$a lxaîer-is, anwa i tessaram d zwao-is ; $ef waya ad tes$fel gma-s a d-iôuê $er ssuq di tezmalt ne$ deg weqbu ad ttêiwet yemma-s ad ûubb $er wxxam n xalt-is dinn i tttwali wn âzizen $zf wul-is wagi d A$ilas.

A$ilas, iêulfa s wayen s itettêulfu Tafat, d$a ad qqimn akken deg wexxam nsen ddeqs n lawqt yiwen ur t-id-yettali wawal, ad ttmesmuqalen s wallen nitni msefhamen melba ma mmeslayen.
yal wa yezôa acu i yeb$a wayev ad t-id-yini mebla ma yell-id imi-s. Mi tekker ad ttôuê $er wexxam ad twaliv aqcic yenne$na ççaçaôent-d wallen-is d imeîîawen annec iberquqen ad teffe$ A$ilas as-d-yessevfeô tamu$li am llufan imi kksen yemma-s, ad ibedd $ef ubalku alma t$ab $ef wallen-is ; syin akin srid ad yekcem $er txxamt ad yerr $ef yiman-is tawwurt ad yebdu tira $ef wafrayen i zed$en ul-is ad ttnarnin seg wass $er wass d wid i t- yezdin akk d Tafat ; azekka-nni ad t-ifekk i yiwet n toaôet-is ad as-tt-tawi i Tafat akken yiwen ur as-yettfaq ; taqcict s ccuq id-ttaîaf ibôatin agi s tuf$a n laâqel ad tazzel $er texxamt-is ad tessexsi tafat n teftilt ad tessi$ tacemmaât êninen id-yesrusen talwit, asirem dtayri deg teqqaô tabôat-nni.

Wwin-d s tikli agi tlata iseggasen yiwen ur ifaq yiss-n, Yidir yu$al-d di lâeskeô yufa-d maci akken yeooa Tafat i tt-id-yufa acku tbeddel fell-as ur tet$imi ara yid-s am zik ur tettqessiô ara yid-s am zik lêaûun tessawev-it ad icukk yella wayen yellan, lad$a imi ywala ula d A$ilas ibeddel zik yell yessaram ad yeffe$ $er fôansa ad ikemmel leqôaya-ines yu$al ibeddel ôôay-is acku tura yeb$a ad iôuê ad yekkes lâeskeô deg ugur, zi$enna msefhamen netta d Tafat ar d-yekfu lâeskeô ines ad yass ad ttid-yexveb.

Aqcic iôuê yeooa-d Tafat deg yi taswiât ur tettett ur tettes, degmi ad kker nettat d imeîîi almi d ass mi id-usa Oamila tewwi-yas-d tabôat n U$ilas tefka-yas-tt-id yemma-s i Oamila ur tezri n wumi-tt acu akka d-yekteb di tebôat nni tamenzut asen d-iceyyaâ i wexxam nsen, d$a ymma-s tenwa-yas d Oamila i yêemmel imi ur terri ara lmendad-is $er Tafat acku akken id-kkren.

Tazwara Oamila tessawav-itent mebla tiêila s amek tbeddel fell-as teswiât tu$al tevmaâ A$ilas d$a tusa-d tenna-yas-d tidet i Yidir. Aqcic d uccen yettandi-tent yettâassa-tent $er $ur-s A$ilas yewwi-yas-tt-id s taêôaymit acku ur yennum ara yella win i as-yettawin ayen i yenwa ad yili d ayla-s, xas ulamma ad yili d gma-s deg yiwet n tâebbuî id-f$en, yeggul ar t-yerren d uccen ar Tafat ad tili d ayla-s yiwen ma yewi-yas-tt : « yesâedda-tt fell-i abrid-a, d acu am wakken yeqqaô wuccen : ma yesâedda-tt fell-i abrid nâell baba-s, ma yesâedda-tt fell-i meôtayen nâell baba ». Ihi msefhamen netta d Oamila ad mâawanen, nettat ad as-d-ttawi tibôatin i as-tettak yemma-s qbel ad tent fekk i Tafat, akken netta ad ya$ Tafat ma d nettat ad ttid-iûaê U$ilas deg imi ad yaf iman-is waêd-s ala netta
$er yidis-is ad tekkes fell-as urfan d lxiq maca ur ilaq ara ad yaêûu belli Yidir yezôa s wayen yellan ger-s d Tafat, namulli as-yini d tuksa i as-tt-yekkes.

Iceyyeâ-as-d u$ilas tlata tebôatin, yeîîef-itent-id baba-s yewwi-yas-tent-id i tmeîîut-is, acku ttwarunt s s yemru aberkan ihi banent d tibôatin n Oamila imi nitni nwan d Oamila i d tamdakult-is, tewwi-yas-tent yemma-s n Yidir, nettat srid tûubb-d $er wanda tettemlil netta d Yidir, tefka-yas-tent; tazwara netta xas ulamma yeqqaô-itent lamaâna asent-ibeddel kan tajellabt as-tent-ifek i Oamila ad tent-awi i Tafat ?

Asmi yu$al yettaf aîas imeslayen icudden $er wayen i t-yezdin netta d tafat deg wafrayen d tmu$liwin d tucviwin yu$al ma yella ur t-yaâjib ara wawal ad icerreg tabôat-nni, d$a deg yietyufa :

- “Ttmektaye$ deg wallen-im mi ttwali$ deg sent amek tt$usu$ di lebêer nsent, imeîîawen-nni nsent ad tthuzzun deg-i akken yetthuzzu lbabuô $ef lemwaoi, akken tetthuzzu tyemmat mmi-s deg urebbi ines, deg sent urttxemmime$ ara i tu$alin $erwexxam maca ur ttxemmime$ ara mavi $ertudert acku tudert-inu d kemmini, lmakla inu d imeslayen-im, amn-inu d imeîîawen-im, ticenfirin-im $er $ur-i ifent tamment ma ters $ef yiles-iw…
- lêaûun akken b$u$ mmeslaye$-d urumine$ ara adssiwve$ ad ini$ ayen ttêulfu$, tifev tfat id-yettakwagur makken kan ad ldiv imi-m ad vsev, ijeooigen imir-nni i fessun, iferîeîîa imiren i ttafen amek ara srefgen, ula d tifirellas imiren id-ttu$alent $er tmurt, tamment$er$ur-i ur iyi-di-ttawi ara dwa akken ad iyi-t-id-fkent tcenfirin-iw mi ara rsent $ef tcenfirin-im, lamaâna tura…
- A k-inaâl Öebbi ! Yidir icerreg tabôat-nni d ifettiten YIDIR : zi$en aîasi yevran di le$yab-iw, aîas i yevran sdeffir uzagur-iw rnu nekkini am yir $yul ur uki$ ; îse$ $ef yiwen yidis ttekle$ lawan-nni netta yetheggi ad iyi-êucc i yvarren-iw!
- “Tenwiv-as têrcev a mmi-s n la…! Tura ad tezrev i wumi qqaôen Yidir, isell i nnda mi ara tekkat, uriyi-semman ara yidir di rrayââ, tagrawla maci kan d win ara yrebêen maca d win ara yessiwven ad yerbaê, rnu ad yidir $er tagara, ger ane$ a gma a mmi-s n baba d yemma ad nzeô anwa ara yrebêen Tafat $er taggara.”

Ɛeddan acêal n wussan d Tafat ur tt-id-usi ula d yiwet n tebôat s$ur A$ilas d$a tusa-d s tuf$a n laâqel $er Oamila ad tekkefell-asa$bel!
TAFAT : a Oamila ttxil-m ma ur iyi-tenniv acu akka iyu$en A$ilas acku acêal aya ur iyi-n-tewwiv ara ula d yiwet n tebôat ; acêal n wussan tura ur yemlal cfeô d gma-s ur ssine$ ives ursine$ amek tga têeôôit, ugade$ amerifaq Yidir i yxeddem !

OAMILA : yahwa-yam kan ten$iv akkaiman-im melba ssebba, A$ilas iban d lwaqt i as-tt-yeksen tezriv lâeskeô maci kand uççi d yives aîas i t-yettabaâen;ma d Yidir ur umine$ ara yella wayen imi yfaq ackuwala$-t-in yettqessiô-d yid-m rnu tesnev-t ur yelli ara d win yettaooan ayen yellan deg wul-is ad t-icebbl, ayen yesâa Yidir deg wul-is yessufu$-it-id $ef yixef n yiles-is.

TAFAT : am-yekkes Öebbi a$bel a Oamila, awer tesâuv a$ilif, akka i xemme$ tazwara maca deg imi iâeîîel yurar cciîan swale$ inu almi u$ale$ waêce$ ameryella wayen nniven i yeooan A$ilas ur d-yessawal ne$ d Yidir iyfaqen i kra ne$ kra. Ihi acu ar am-ini$ a Oamila, $ur-m matewwi-yam-d xalti tabôat ur ttâeîîil ara akken ad iyi-tt-in-t-awiv ; di$en acu i b$i$ amt-id-ini$ ad iyi-siwev Öebbi ad am-nerr lxiô neck d U$ilas $ef wannecta txedmev ne$$ef sbeô tsebrev fell-$.

Oamila tes$afel kan Tafat t$ab $ef wallen teffe$-d deffir-s $er wanda ara temlil nettat d Yidir degimi id-âedda zdat tejmaât deg yeqqim netta d yemdukal-is, din i yeêûayella wayen teb$a, ur yerni ara aîas iqveâ-itt-id $er ti$ilt d abrid yedduran $ef wallen n medden.

YIDIR : tusa-d$er $ur-m,tessuter-am-d acimiulac acêal aya tibôatin, ahat yella wayen tcuk ?

OAMILA : xas ulamma tugad aye$eô akka acêal aya ur d-iceyyeâ ara maânakkse$-as a$ilif nni$-as d xeddim ahat i t-yeîîfen, tugad di$en amer ad tiliv tfaqev maâna sqenâa$-tt belli ur umine$ ara acku ur telliv ara d win i tefren ma yella wayen i tezriv, maca akken yeb$u yili lêal ilaqfell-ak ad as-tt-id-fruv akken ur teççukku ara fiêel ma tôuê adtesseqi yemma-k as-d-ini yeççeyyiâ-d din ara tcukk d ûûaê ; d$a ayen akken akk i nebna acêal aya ad t-yawi wavu.

YIDIR : tezriv ttandi$-tent,ttâassa$-tent, zri$ acu i xedme$, ma d kemmini xeddem kan ayen la m-d-qqaôe$ ad trebêev ur steqsay ara aîas, lêaûn maci aîas i yeqqimen akken as-negg tagara i temsalt agi n U$ilas i $-icebblen annecta.

Oamila tuli-d d tamenzut akken ur ttukkun ara medden yerna
cwiî itbeâ-itt-id Yidir deffir,yewwi yid-staqeôâett n côab yekcem $er wexxam yenna-yasi yemma-s urt-id-ssakayara $er imensi, yekcem $er texxamt-is yerra-d tawwurt yeddem-d tibôatin i mazal ur icerreg ara yebda yettaârav ad yaru tibôatin s tiram tid U$ilas acêal n tikal i yura tabôatur tt-id-yessufe$, tin yessexseô ad tt-iveqqeô ad d-yaru tayev, ula akkenni ur yuyis ara s tqaôâett nni n côab $er idis-is yewwwev-d wudem n ûbaê yessufe$-d snat n tebôatin as-tiniv d tira n U$ilas kkes-itent, ffer-itent mi tent-yekfa yeîîef-itent ger ifassen-is yesmuqul-itent la yettmeslay waêd-s :

”t$adev-iyi- ay A$ilas, xas ulamma êemle$-k d gma laêêundeg ne$ idammen kif kif-iten maca Tafat maci dtanudda-inek acku i nekkini i wumi tekteb ne$ ma yella ur iyi-tektib ara ad tt-ketbe$ i yiman-iw, seg zik ur tettadamev ara ta$aws ala ma yella ur iyi-tahwi ara, ad tarouv qbeld adda-k $er-sad tawev nnuba-k a gma ameéyan, ha, ha, ha…”

Ye$li $ef wusu isebbaven-is ur ten-yekkis ara, yeîîes akken almi d rrebâa (16:00mn) n tmeddit. Azekka-nni iâedda-d d tama n wexxam n Oamila yufa-tt-id tfetter icettiven imuqel-itt teêûa yaêwao-itt, mlalen anda akken nnumen ttemlilin d$a yefka-yas-d snat n tebôatin adtent-awi i Tafat, testeqsa-t$ef wegbur nsent yerra-yas-d :

”nni$-am ur teqsay ara aîas, yal ta$awsa ad tas di lawan-is. Tibratin wwvent $er Tafat ifukken anner n lfeôê, tigecrar-is ttargigint as-tiniv d tam$ert n 70 iseggasen, allen-is sregrugent seg imeîîi, urteôoi ara ad yekcem baba-s d watmaten-is ad kecmen akken ad asen-d-ssar imensi, tenna-yas i yemma-s ad tali ad teîîes.

Tessexsi taftilt am yal tikelt deg ara t$eô tabôat i as-d-iceyyeâ U$ilas, tessa$ tacemmaât deg-s id-tettasrriêa n tezwal uôumi, teldi tabôat tamenzut, tebda teqqaô-itt !

“I kemm a Tafat ! Maççi s tenfalit am ta s wayes ibeddu zik U$ilas tabôat i as-tenna deg wul-is, taqcict simmal yekkat wul-is as-tiniv yeb$a ad ijelleb deg wemkan-is ! Ahat tettemseqsiv ayen uram-d-uri$ ara acêal aya, d ûûaê axeddim yella aîas maççi d cwiî maca fki$ lwaqt i yiman-iwakken ad mi ara xemme$ ar tagara ad îfe$ ôôay ur ttendemmaye$ ara fell-as ur ttu$ale$ deg-s.

Dtidet ul-iw $er $ur-m yecven, udem-im ur yettfaôaq ara zdat wallen-iw, maca ôôay-agi u$uô ssawva$ d win ur neshil ara fell-i, cukke$ yeffe$-iyi laâqel ass mi beddle$ akk iswiren-iw ama d widenni i cudden $er tmusni inu, ama d wid akken i ttmenni$ seg wass mi
lli$ d ameéyan ad f$a$ $er Fôansa, almi d imi id-baâde$ fell-am i bdi$ ttmeyyize$ acu n tucviwin deg i $li$, tura b$i$ ad rre$ ayen mazal zemre$ ad rre$, b$i$ ad ôuêe$ $er beôôa akken ad kemle$ leqôaya-w, $ef waya b$i$ am-d-ini$ ad iyi-tsemêev,êûu kan dkemm i d taqcict tamenzut i êemle$ maca…”ur tkemmel ara tabôat tcerreg-itt almi ifettit ur yeddi d gma-s, allen-is sregrugent d isaffen, ta$ect-is tebbaêbaê almi yu$al ûûut yugi ad yeffe$ tebdatetaîaf deg ucebbub-is am taooalt mi yemmut mmi-s ne$ argaz-is ; maca si tama adtettru si tama nniven teqmev ûûut-is akken yiwen seg wexxam ur as-d-isell ara. Di îmaâ amer ad yili deg wurfan id-yenna imeslayen-nni mazal-itt tu$al-d teldi tabôat-nni tis snat, tval $ef tidet d tin ara tt-yeooen ad tteggugem acêal n wussan : ”…Tezriv a yell-is n xalt-i, ôuê mêu-yi seg wul-im, sfev-iyi ger wallen-im, ttu imeslayen-nni d yesmektiyen nni a$-yegrun yiwen wass,acku maci d nekk i d argaz i am-ilaqen,lemêibba-m $ur-i te$lev, egg leqôaô i tayri-m, ad testumnev s teméi-m, ad tafev win am-ilaqen, ad yessin azal-im, ad tettuv akk acu i sâedda$ fell-am, semmaê-iyi…”

Taqcict tcerreg-itt ula d tinna, tveqqeô-dtacemmaât-nni $ef îîabla, tettru almi dayen ur yezmir ûûut adyeffe$ seg imi-s ne$zemrent wallen-is ad ldint seg wannecten tru, tu$al tekker-d tejmaâ-itt-id, terra ifettiten sdaxel n tmacwaôt teffer-iten sddaw wusu ines, teqqim rrif umeîôaê almi tt-ye$deô yives. Azekka-nni mi d-kker tâeîîel d$a tuli-d yemma-s tufa-tt-id akkenni, mi tekker ad tbedd ad te$li tuzzel tsawel-di warraw-is wwin-tt $er sbiîar acu ur zôin ara acu i d sebba, d$a u$alen sbiîar yettak-itt i wayev, îîaleb yettak-itt i wayev almi d imi taêla irkulli, maca tavsa-nni akk n zik tôuê, Yidir seg wass mi tahlek ur tt-yeooi dnetta id-ttafen ama d imawlan-is ama d nettat itekkes fell-as lxiq.

Äeddan wussan taqcict tekker cweyya, A$ilas seg wass mi iôuê urd-yusi ala sin ne$ tlata iberdan ussan-nni kan imenza deg yekcem, syin akin deg wassen, ala mi d-yeççeyyiâ tibôatin, tid n at wexxam qqaôent-t, tid n Tafat îîarviqent-d deg ufus n Yidir i yezran acu i asent-ixeddem.

Yiwen webrid yusa-d Yidir $er wexxam n alt-is teqqim-d yid-s Tafat di texxamt inebgawen, d$a yebda yettmeslay-as-d $ef iêulfan-is d wafrayen-is i $ef yezdel seg wass mi llan d imeéyanen, taqccict ibeddel wudem-is ûûifa am waken yesseqceô-
as-d adeddic aqdim ur n-êli ara, srid tbeddel-as awal am win imi ara tiniv ur ssaâyaw ara iman-ik, texvuv-iyi ; yeffe$ kan tuli $ertexxamt-is terra-tt i ymeîîi dwin i yteksen $ef wul-is xasulamma yettvurru-tt, acku yetteqôaê-itt uqeôôu-s, maca yettifsus wul-is seg wurfan as-teqqaô : ”amek ara iêmile$ Yidir, ma yella ur câife$ ara deg wayen iyi-xdem gma-s ad qeble$ wagi, d acu xas yevra-d wannecta ger-i d U$ilas, ur zri$ ara ayen urzmire$ ara ad t-karhe$, ne$ ad as-îfe$ ccaêna, di$en ur d awez$i ad ili$ deg yiwen wexxam akk d U$ilas.”

Acêal n wussan mebâed mi as-yemmeslay Yidir $ef wafrayen-is, ur d-yuli s axxam nsen, almi d-yewwev wassen, atan yuli-d yufa-d Tafat teqqim deg wefrag tezzi-d s uzagur i tewwurt useqif i medlen, yeldi-d tawwurt sttawil, nettat teqqim t$as, yeqqen-as-d allen-i s deffir yu$al izmev-itt-id $er yedmaren-is, tergagi tu$al tedduqqes-d tenwa-yas d A$ilas tekkes-d ifassen-is z lem$awla tufa-d Yidir.

TAFAT : tessexlaâv-iyi a Yidir, nwi$-as d albaâv imakraven!

YIDIR : nude$ igenni, tamurt anda ara kem-wali$, am waken igenni iôfaâ-ikem, lqaâa tesseblaâ-ikem, win ur d-nesteqsa ara fell-am kemmini ur testeqsayev ara ?

TAFAT : ala wellah ara d lwaqt iyi-tt-yeksen, jida tahlek d ayen izaden ur numin ara ad tt-id-yaf unebdu agi id-iteddun, lmakla ur tt-tettett alma teééev am waman, nessemcaê-as-ten a llufan ur nesâi ara tu$mas, yemma ula d nettat ur tezmir ara d$a ala i nekk imi tt-id-yewwi lêal namulli ad tettmeooid alma tessenzah-d fell-a$ at taddart.

Yesser afus-is $ef tcenfirin-is, ykna $er $ur-s nettat ur temmamev as-tiniv d azeqquô yerkan yessuden-itt ur d-nni awal d$a din i yufa leb$i-s ; imiren kan tekcem-d yemma-s n Tafat acku ur yerri ara tawwurt deffi-s rnu mi d-yekcem akken yaêsa deffir-s kan i tella xalti-s, tetteddu-d s ttawil imi tewwi-d tacekkeôt n weslen i texsi ines, tameîîut tekcem-d teqquô deg wemkan-is tesssar tacekkeôt-nni Tafat tefrawes, texlaâ d$a tuzzel tekker deg imi id-degger Yidir fell-is tuli $er texxamt-is.

Yidir yekker-d $er xalt-is la yettmeslay yid-s awal ur tt-id-yuli seg wayen twala acku imiren kan lmux-is yewwev si ttexmam $er wanda ur tettarrav ara.

YIDIR : a xalti semmaê-iyi wellah ar d cciîan i a$-i$uôôen ma nuki d yiman nne$ rnu ma nwi$ ayen n dir $er Tafat acku ttmenni$-tt d
tameîîut-iw n laêala lamer ad iyi-tt-tefkem ad ase$ ad tt-id-xevbe$, seg zik ssareme$-tt !

# YEMMA-S N TAFAT

ma yella teb$iv-tt maci akka i xedmen yergazen iâeqlen rnu akk d wumi akked d yell-is n xalt-is, di$enna tesâa irgazen u$uô ara tt-id-ssutrev maci d yell-is n webrid, ôuê tura ma teb$iv ad tt-ta$ev ceyyeâ-d imawlan-ik ad as-d-inin i wergaz ne$ yiwen seg warrac i melmi imi ad tasem.

Yidir yeffe$-d, yezha wul-is, s wayen akka twala xalt-is nettat ad ttxemmen $er wayen n dir $ef yell-is d$a ad ttagad lefvuêegga xas ulamma tugi Tafat nettat ad ttetêetemm, sya $er zdat ad iyi-têemmel s sshala.

# YEMMA-S N TAFAT

akka i kem-id-ôebbe$ teb$iv ad ttessemrir$ev nnif nne$ deg umejôiw, teb$iv atmaten-im ur ttâawaden ara ad refden iqeôôa nsen ger at taddart, ma d tura atan yeb$a ad yass ad kem-id-yexveb, amer ad yali wawal n xaîi seg imi-im ad ini$ ayen yellan i watmaten-im ad sâeddin dbiêa-m tazuli$t, tesliv ne$ xaîi!tôuê ad mmeslay tsu$ fell-as : ”zqef-iten, ur b$i$ ara ad sle$ i yiwen wawal n zzayed, ur tettetêiv ara tesâiv idammen n wudem ad ttqablev atmaten-im d baba-m, ooze fell-i.

D$a tveggeô-itt $ef wusu teffe$-d ; Tafat terra-tt i lwaâd imeîîi almi tt-i$eééa wudem-is ur tâedda ara smana $ef temsalt-agi usan-d wexxam n Yidir ad xevben Tafat msefhamen ad ifak U$ilas lâeskeô ines ad tt-awin netta qqimen-as-d ala tlata (03) waguren akken ad sduklen lfeôê.

Yidir f$ent-as tirga $er tafat seg wass mi i as-tt-id-fkan d nitni deg wexxam d aheggi i tme$ôa.

Tewwev-d tme$ôa ala (15) n wussan i as-yeqqimen, yusa-d U$ilas yeîîef lexbeô am taôûaût t-iêuzan $er wul maca awal ur t-id-yuli $er yiwen deg-sen ama d Tafat ama d Yidir yu$ tiyita deg wul ur d-yeccekta ur d-yenni aêê $er $ur-s d Tafat seg d-kka tyita acku tbeddel-it s gma-s, amer d Yidir telli ur yettaqbal ara Tafat amer yeéri tlaêêû yid-s ; yu$al ur d-ikeççem alma d udem n ûbaê, ma d tibôatin nni d-yettaru U$ilas yefka tent i Oamila yugad amer ad tent-taf Tafat sya $er zdat.

Yiwet n tikelt temlal-d Oamila A$ilas d$a taêbes $ur-s :

# OAMILA

semmaê-iyi- ay A$ilas ur nwi$ ara annecta akk ad yas s$ur Tafat, ass mi i as-ttawi$ ibôatin nni id-ççeyyiâev tettagi ad tent-teîîef, d$a ad tentan $ur-i ma teb$iv ak-tent-id-rre$ ?

# A£ILAS

ala, fiêel carreg-itent ur tent-êwaoe$ ara rnu éri$ d Yidir
ara ta$ acku tenna-yi-d yiwet n tikelt nekk nni$-as wali win i $er yemmal wul-im.

Aqcic meskin awi-d kan ur yeççemmit ara Tafat imi ad tu$al d tameîîut n gma-s, maca si tama nniven ilaq ad yaf tifrat i temsalt am ta acku u yettezmir ara ad yidir deg wexxam deg ara yettwali tin i$ef yesleb ger ifassen n wegaz nniven xas ulamma ad yili d gma-s, rnu ad idiren seddaw n yiwen sqef.

Ass-a d lexmis d urar n lêenni n Tafat d Yidir, atan yerbaê di tegrawla nni id-yesker ger-as d gma-as ur n-aâlim s kra, maca A$ilas ame$bun ass-a d ass n lmut-is, ass-a i yemvel wul-is akk d isirem-ines, Tafat di texxamt terra-tt ala i ymeîîi ass-a ad taêûu iruê-as U$ilas u yettili ara usirem ad mlilen; A$ilas yezziwziê am akken ur ifeôôeê ara i yiman-is, yewwi lxevôa $er exam n eslit, yugem-d aman, yeddez, yezzuzer, lêaûun ur yeççi ur yeswi ur yestaâfa, rnu $ef wannecta yewwi-yasen-d ivebbalen akk yesnen ad wwten di lâeôc asen-wten.

Tislit tedda-d netta yusa-d sdeffir nsen ççan inebgawen, u$alen ansi id-kkan, ala wid d-yeqqimen $er wurar, yewwev-d yiv ura imiren i yaêma iwala tislit mi d-res ad tecvaê d wergaz-is, yu$al ijbed-it-id Yidir ad yecvaê akk id-sen dinna i t-yen$a acku yeb$a as-d-yesbeggen irbaê-it, ur âeîlen ara ulin $er texxamt nsen simi iwala taftilt texsi yeffe$ axxam melba wa yarren ddahn-is, yeîîef abrid srid $er zagu yesla i waman sregrugen akken sregrugent wallen-is, iâella tamrart $ef tasaft-nni dinna yuli meqbel ad iâellaq iman-is yeooa-d imeslayen agi: “ma yella a Tafat yefka-yam wul-im ad tidirev deg yiwen wexxam akk d winna akked kem-zdin acêal n yesmektiyen d t$awsiwin, nekkini yur sâi$ ara tazmert nni, maca ttmenni$-am lahna melba i$ilifen akked d gma, acku mazal êemle$-kem ar tura $ef waya ilaq d neck ara am-yeooen annar, nekkini ur zmire$ ara ad iêmile$ tayevnin, a$iô kemmini tudert-iw yedl-itt îlam d usigna, ma d kemm semman-am Tafat, aff tafat tura ma telliv d s tidet d Tafat.
# Taklit n tayri

# Djamel Benaouf

# A tt-buddeɣ d tajmilt i weltma-tneɣ

# Zakiya Ɛeggad

# (neɣ Fuziya akken i s-nessawal nekni)

Wissen dɣa amek yella wul-im ?! Wissen ma yennejbar, neɣ werɛad ?! Nniɣ-am tzedreḍ deg wanu (lbir) ur nesɛi lqaɛ, wissen anwa wagi i kem- yeskulin ?! Wissen ma yuklal meqqar, Neɣ ar daxel ay ul ?!

Yettwawwet dɣa di lemtel : «Yekla yuẓam, yerẓa remḍan-is ɣef yemqerqer ». Niɣ (yak) qqaren daɣen: « tayri d taderɣalt », tayri taderɣalt yezzuɣuren bab-is ɣer wanda tebɣa nettat, mačči ɣer wanda yebɣa netta. Ahat a yi-d-tiniḍ : Wi k-yennan akka kkuliɣ a wagi ? Xuḍi nekk mačči d menwala !...

- Nniɣ-am ssneɣ akk tigi. Lemdeɣ-tent deg wallen-nni-inem yecban tamda n tirga, tinna akken yellan daxel n « yefri n leɛǧayeb , iɣef yesberber wedrar n Yemma tadrart deg Aweqqas. »

Ɣriɣ-tent di twenza-m ideg tewcem tayri, ɣas tura s isekkilen imecṭuḥen i wumi ur tezmir a ten-tɣer tmuɣli n menwala, nekk ɣriɣ-ten-id ! Sseɣreɣ-ten-id i wid yettnadin ad issinen tayri s 1Ṣṣenf-agi n tira ssawalen-as s taɛrabt «lxaṭira . Aql-aɣ nefren-as-d isem i t-iwulmen s tmaziɣt : «Tawengamt» i d-yessumer gma-tneɣ Derwic Ɛumar si Lmerruk. Tawengamt tekka-d si : Tawengimt (lxaṭer = mémoire).

2 D tamedyazt, d taɛeggalt n tiddukla Numidya. Tewweḍ sanda ara naweḍ, ass n 17/08/06 ɣef 1 n ṣṣbeḥ (5 wussan segmi tettwaru twengamt-agi). Truḥ akken d tilemẓit, d lal n 35 iseggasen. Ṭṭes di talwit a Fuziya weltma.
talqayt. Ɣas ma tura s isekkilen d ireqqaqen nezzeh, cban inzizen n wul i wumi ur tezmir tiṭ a ten-id-tefren, nekk ferneɣ-ten-id! Ferẓeɣ-ten-id am umejjay-nni yeṭṭfen «sskanar . Ɣas tura s » isekkilen n tmess ireqqen, tinna i d-yettaǧǧan ccwami ideg tetthabi tmuɣli n win ur njerreb taruɣi. Ɣas tura s idammen, am tecraḍ ideg ggwten izamulen, yal wa amek ara sen-yefk anamek; ma d inumak-nsen n tidet ur yelli seg-sen win yellan d amaɣud (iquden) ɣur kra; ttarran yes-sen lada. Ɣur kra-nniḍen; ttarran yes-sen yir tiṭ, neɣ tiṭ n tismin. Ɣur wiyaḍ (rrehṭ neɣ ṣṣenf-agi, ixulef wiyaḍ-nniḍen); jebbden-d yes-sen lwelha, neɣ tamuɣli n medden i wakken ad ɣren deg-sen lmertat akk d tlufa i ten-izedɣen i lebda; i wakken a d-grin daɣen d ccfaya ur tseffeḍ tatut. Ma d nutni (izamulen-nni), ttweḥḥin-d akk s nnger… Ɣas tira-nni (yuran di twenza) tikkwal teggar-d tiɣri tagugamt, tinna akken yecban tarṣaṣt i ineqqen amdan s tsusmi. Ala tarwiḥt n win tesseqlalleḥ i d as-isellen deg yifer-is iɛuẓẓgen. Ɣas tikkwal tettnazaɛ-d, anazeɛ-ines igellu-d s lmertat umuḍin i wumi ur isell ara wemdan anezmar, ala ameɛlal i d-tettaweḍ. Ɣas ma tikkwal tesrugmut, taɣect-ines d asxertem i wumi ur ifehhem leɛqel. Ala tiselbi i tt-yessnen. Ɣas tikkwal tiɣri-ines d tilemt ur s-isell ara ula d lmal agugam. Ala Ḥessas nnda i s-isellen di takin (takwin) ugama yecban targit. Ɣas tikkwal tiɣri-ines d axemmim, d tidmi, d takti, d ayen i d-yettrusun kan di lbal, ur tt-id-tettaf ara tgezzant-nni yekkaten xeṭṭ-rrmel. Ɣas tikkwal tiɣri-ines d asuɣu, d acerɣit, d ameǧǧed yessergagayen tasa. D acewwiq-nni i d-yessrusuyen lweḥc… Ɣas tikkwal d ṣṣut izuffan n waḍu «ɛyaṭ u qeyyama , winna akken yessengugulen kra yellan… Ṣṣut-is, ahat yecba aṭerḍeq n rrɛud, kra yellan yessexmet-it, kra yellan yessers-d fell-as tigdi; ala wid i wumi tennerna tigdi, wigi tigdi-nni-nsen tettuɣal-asen d tissas. Akka am tyaẓiṭ : «tayaẓiṭ ur nettarew, tin ur nzeddel ɣef tmellalin, ass n rrɛud i s-ggaren timellalin akken ad tesgerger fell-asent . Ɣas tikkwal, ṣṣut-is » yettwannay-d s yal tameslayt, anagar tinna-akken-nneɣ (wissen teɛreq-as, wissen yettu-tt, wissen yessetḥa yes-s, yettɛudd-tt d lɛib ?) ; nekk, gziɣ-t imi d-yerḍel awal sɣur wiyaḍ «lḥubb , » smektaɣ-t-id s wawal leḥmala , segmi d-yemmekta , yerna-yas- d takna tayri . Ɣas tikkwal d tiɣri, neɣ d ṣṣut, neɣ d anazeɛ, neɣ d « asrugmet, neɣ d ameǧǧed, neɣ d aslilew, neɣ d asbuɣer, neɣ d
nnehtat, neɣ d ajefjef (alejlej), neɣ… anda ẓriɣ nekk d acu-t !?

Ḥṣiɣ kan d aneznaz n wanza yessergagayen ulawen, d aneznaz-nni i ttagaden akken medden; winna akken n win yettwanɣan s yir lmut (dagi, qesdeɣ-d tayri), yettwanɣan am yetbir ɣef waman, yettwanɣan werɛad i ten-yeswi. Ɣas tura s isekkilen n nnur i yeddal cciṭan s tbernust-ines n lɛar, s tbernust-ines n tallest (ṭṭlam). Yesberber fell-as, yessedrag-itt i tmuɣli ; d acu ara twali tiṭ yeddreɣlen di ṭṭlam uṭellis ? ala tiṭ n lmalayek (ineglusen) ara tt-iwalin, ma stufant ɛad, neɣ ma ur keḥḥlent ara s taẓult ilili !

Nekk, nniɣ-am: Ɣriɣ aya, mačči kan di temlixt n tmelɣiɣt n twenza-m, mačči kan di limarat n icerriḍen, neɣ n yezrigen yellan deg uyendur, yellan deg wenyir n twenza-m ; ɣriɣ -t di lbext-im yuran deg ufus-im azelmaḍ yellan d azehri. Ɣriɣ-t ula di tira-nni taḥerfit, tinna akken i zemren ad arun yakk yemdanen s ifassen-nsen di lkaɣeḍ (ur tt-ttarun ara s tinna-akken-nneɣ, ma uran-tt xuḍi a tt-zelgen, wa yettaru-tt akka: «ḥemleɣ» -deg wemkan n ḥemmleɣ-, yeqqel d asif. Wa yettaru-tt akka : «Rriɣ» -deg wemkan n «riɣ - am iriran!) ; tinna akken i ttarun yemdanen, tikkwal s ifassen-nsen teǧǧa tezdeg, s ifassen-nsen yeččuren d ilefḍan, yeččuren d inǧan, yeččuren d imbuxxen neɣ d busfus. Ih ! tikkwal ttarun-tt ula s ifassen-nsen yebbeqnunnsen deg idammen… Amek ?!...

- Llan wid ur nettaru la s lmidad, la s ssmex, la s wayen-nniḍen ; ur ssinen ara maḍi ad arun.

Wid-nni, Ssawalen-tt-id s yimi afuḥan, s yimi i itetten amurḍus. Qqaren-tt-id s yiles n weksum ur nesɛi iɣess, qqaren-tt-id s yiles ur nesɛi iɣess, yessibnin akedded n yiɣess, yettsummun adif n yiɣess. Ssawalen-tt-id s yiles ur nesɛi tilas, s yiles i itemmɣen akin i tlisa, iles-nni i wumi ur zmirent ad qerrɛent tuɣmas, iles-nni yessnen amek ara yenneḥwaṣ, yessnen amek i yettmelliṣ. Niɣ (yak) acḥal d abrid i yemneɛ si tuffẓa n tuɣmas i s-yellan d ẓẓerb ! Niɣ (yak) acḥal d tikkelt i yessaweḍ bab-is (mačči d iman-is i yessawaḍ, d bab-is i yessawaḍ) ɣer uwezɣi ; neɣ ɣer lmuḥal ! Netta (iles) yezga yeffer, yettuɣal ɣer wexjiḍ-is am wezrem, niɣ qqaren «iles yessawal-itent, aqerruy yettaɣ-itent».

A yi-d-tiniḍ : D acu i d imeslayen-agi ur nesɛi lmeɛna ?! D acu i d yir imeslayen-agi imeqqerṣa ? Imeslayen-agi yecban aderbal neɣ yecban abeḥnuq-nni yehban, winna akken yettmenṭaren deg
igudiyen, winna akken i wumi ur d-tzeg tfawet ! Nniɣ-ak a win ur nessin : Ma yella kečč tulet-inek leggaɣet, tecba leḥrir, nekk ul-iw ḥercaw, yecba tazeggart.

- Ɣas ul-im ḥercaw, ɣas yecba tazeggart, llan wid yecban amger zemren a t-id-qemmḍen si lǧedra, zemren a t-id-ḥuccen seg iẓuran.

- Nniɣ-ak : Ma keččini a winnat, tulet-inek d taleqqaqt am tqeṭṭiṭ-nni yegzer wemcic. Nekk, ul-iw d aẓru n tefza neɣ n tnicca.

- Ɣas ul-im d aẓru, llan wid yecban anhiz (afḍis ameqqran), a t-sdegdgen, a t-bḍun d ticwayin.

- Nniɣ-ak, a winnat : Ma kečč, tulet-inek d adɣes, teshel i weskaf ! Nekk, ul-iw d timess, ur yezmir ḥedd a t-yennal.
