- Ɣas ma ul-im d timess, llan iseḥḥaran yetturaren s tmess akken bɣan, tikkwal tetten-tt d tuččit.

Nniɣ-am, tenniḍ-iyi-d. Tenniḍ-iyi-d, nniɣ-am : Tugiḍ ad tfehmeḍ tasusmi yettmeǧǧiden, akken i d-ssenṭaqeɣ nekkini arqiqqes n lecfar n wallen-im. Nniɣ-am, tenniḍ-iyi-d. Tenniḍ-iyi-d, nniɣ-am : Tugiḍ ad teɣreḍ tadyant n tayri gar : «Zulixa d Sidna Yusef . Tenniḍ-iyi-d, nniɣ-am. Nniɣ-am, tenniḍ-iyi-d :

Walaɣ acḥal d isura n irebbiten n tayri : widak-nni n «Bac muhend es d sitti Hanem , widak-nni n «Fendi wa ḥaramihi ,» widak-nni i ɣ-yerran tayri d asqecmeɛ, i ɣ-yerran tayri d alelluc netturar yes-s akken i ɣ-yehwa…

Tgugmeḍ, ters-d fell-am tsusmi ! Ḥṣiɣ tugiḍ ad tawiḍ mayna ! Kemmini yečča zzux. Kemmini yenwan iman-im d leɛlali. Kemmini yenwan iman-im d aggur, d tiziri, d igenni s lekmal-is !

Amek ara tawi mayna teqcict n ccuq ?! Taqcict i d-yekkren di lɛezz d ddlal, taqcict i d-yetturebban s ḥlu-ḥlu neɣ s ttnefcic?!

Meɛḍureḍ i telliḍ, aḥlil !…

Fiḥel awal, ɣas teṭṭfeḍ ssabeɛ-inem ar ɣur-m ; maca, gziɣ tasusmi-m, yenna-yi-d lexyal n tili-m : Sel mliḥ a wagi ! Nekk mačči d menwala. Nekk, ur lliɣ ara si tidak-nni i ẓẓuɣuren wulawen-sent. Nekk seg tid yezwarayen leɛqel, mačči seg tid-nni i iteddun kan s lewhi.

- Ḥṣiɣ, ayagi yakk d zzux kan i yennernan deg-m. Ayagi yakk d awham kan i twehmeḍ deg yiman-inem. Ayagi yakk d nnefs kan i kem-yulin, teḍra-yam am tculliṭ-nni yeččuren d nnefs, nǧeɛ-itt kan ad tuɣal d tilemt, d ulac…
Ma ɣur yiman-im d ayen-nniḍen, ɣur wiyaḍ, (akka telliḍ akka tura, wamag ma tejjteḍ neɣ ma tsuma-kem-id tewser, fiḥel awal !)

tettbaneḍ-asen-d d tamesluxt kan, daya. Yal wa amek i yebɣa a kem-yečč d tiremt : Wa d aseqqaḍ, yebɣa a kem-yečč s tawant. Wa teǧǧa-t leqnaɛa, yebɣa ad itett deg-m ad yesnagar. Wa yettwafeḥḥem (afḥam « » qqaren-t i win yeɛyan di kra n tuččit), a kem-yesselbubeɣ kan a kem-yeǧǧ. Wa yebɣa-kem d tacriḥt n teftilt, wa yebɣa-kem d tacriḥt m yiɣess, wa yebɣa-kem d tacriḥt m tassemt, wa yebɣa-kem d lemdamat (ayen yettilin daxel uɛebbuḍ, am tasa d wul), wa yebɣa-kem d iles, d adif, d lekfarat (lmexx neɣ allaɣ)… llan ula d wid i kem-yebɣan d tisigert ara yefk i yiḍan, i yemcac…

Twehmeḍ ! Tugiḍ a d-terreḍ awal !?

Ihi, mačči fell-i ara tesfelqḍeḍ, mačči fell-i ara tessiɛezzeḍ iman-im… niɣ qqaren : «Acḥal ɛzizeḍ a lleft, taberruyt teswa mitin .

Neɣ daɣen : « Ay akken tebɣuḍ tiɛzizeḍ a tiṭ, timmi tezga-d sennig-m .

Nekk, tigi yakk, jerrbeɣ-tent, «ulac afrux yufgen, ur iris ,» «ulac ttejra ur ihuzz waḍu , ulac ul ur tḥuza tayri, ulac nnif di tayri.

Tayri tecba lmut, ulac win ara tezgel, tgellu s uzegzaw akk d uquran; ɛad tugar-itt ! Imi nettat (tayri) d taderɣalt, tḍellu i medden bilɣus, tneqq-iten s tecmatin, ttekkes-asen tirwiḥin tettaǧǧa-ten d igerbuzen, mmuten ṭṭillin…

Ma ur tumineḍ ara sell i weḥbak n wul-im, sell i uneznaz n iḥulfan-im ; wali tugna-inem di tnafa, mačči d tugna-nni i m-d-yemmal lemri… Ma ur tumineḍ ara steqsi wid ijerrben, neɣ sell i tezlit-agi n Si Muḥ :

«Ay aqcic»

Cubaɣ-k, ula d nekk yiwwas ḥemmleɣ

Ssneɣ mi ara yirẓig lqut

Ssneɣ tayri yeṭṭfen tiɣilt

Terra-yi ussan d lḥentit

Rwiɣ asawen

Tayri ma tfut tedderɣel

Ula d as-d-yexdem leɛqel

S i nettwali
Mačči s Si Muḥ ara tesɛeddiḍ iman-ik, mačči s wiyaḍ. Si Muḥ akk d wid i t-yecban ẓid-it imeslayen-nsen, mačči am imeslayen-inek ileǧmanen, imessasen.

I tuɣaleḍ kan ɣer tira-nni-inek tamugezt (engagé) ?!

- D kemmini, ɛad d kunwi i yebɣan aya. D kunwi i yi-d-yeẓẓuɣren, d kunwi i yi-d-yefkan afus…

- Nefka-yak-n afus, kečč tefkiḍ deg-neɣ afus ! Nessugem deg-k ayen iwulmen, ayen ara ɣ-d-yerren asirem, ayen ara ɣ-d-icebbḥen tirga…

- Terǧam deg-i ayen iwulmen, neɣ ayen tebɣam ?! Tebɣam a wen-kemzeɣ anda tebɣam…

- I tecbuḍ-d xersum deg idaddaten-inek ?!

- Tebɣiḍ a d-tiniḍ imyura-nni-nneɣ imeqqranen, wid-nni akken i wumi yecrureq yemru (a yi-ssurfen imi ur ten-id-bdireɣ ara, ɣas ssneɣ akk ismawen-nsen) ? D tidet, wigi ur ten-cbiɣ ara, meɛni annar-agi hraw, deg-s amkan i yal yiwen…

- Terniḍ tsemmaḍ-as annar , ɣef waya i tesserwateḍ akka akken i k-yehwa !

- Ala ! Bɣiɣ kan a d-iniɣ : Yal wa amek tt-iwala, yal wa anta tiɣmert ansi tt-id-yessaked. Lemmer ur ugadeɣ ara ad rfun fell-i, lemmer ur ugadeɣ ara a tt-cerweɣ merriɣet, yili nniɣ-d : Llan deg-sen wid i tt-iwalan s tmuɣli n wiyaḍ, mačči s tmuɣli-nsen nutni. Llan deg-sen wid i tt-id-yettcebbiḥen d acebbeḥ n belɛani (belɛani d aɛemmed s twehranit, wissen ma yella s teqbaylit ?),

ssebganen-d kan tafukt akk d nnsim n tefsut, teffren uḍan n llyali n tegrest (ccetwa), teffren izilan n ṣṣmayem unebdu; llan deg-sen ula d wid i tt-yennan akken ara ɛeǧben tiqcicin, neɣ tiḥdayin (ma llant ɛad tid yeqqaren s tmaziɣt ?!) akken a sen-d-cmummḥent.

Tilmeẓyin i kem-yecban a ten-buddent i yiman-nsent, ma d tid ijewǧen a ten-buddent i yessi-tsent (ɛad ma ur ɛciqent ara yakan : di Raɣeb Ɛalama, neɣ di Jurj Wasuf, neɣ di kra n «Cab» i yessnen ad yecnu: Lmeryula ttebɣi ttesher).

- «Iruḥ wul a d-yekkes lxiqq, yufa leḥbab d imuḍan . D acu k-

yuɣen akka, a winnat ?! Aql-ik, tuɣaleḍ d akuz, tuɣaleḍ d ccluc, tuɣaleḍ d buseṭṭaf, ur tezgileḍ yiwen ! Tessawaleḍ ala i nnger !...

Weqbel ara k-iniɣ aḥlil, ahat meɛḍureḍ i telliḍ, ɣas ɣiwel err-iyi-d ɣef westeqsi-yagi : Acimi yal mi ara d-tbedreḍ tayri, yal mi ara d-tbedreḍ iḥulfan tettmektayeḍ-d yid-sen lmut?!
Ass-a a m-d-iniɣ ayen ur nniɣ ula i yiwen, acku tefkiḍ-iyi-d nnuba, teǧǧiḍ-iyi a d-smireɣ tiqqit si tedlawt-nni n lemrar i d-yeẓẓem wul-iw… Ihi ɣas sel-d a tameddakelt (mačči a taḥbibt, ɣas kkes aɣbel) : Walaɣ-tt sanda i tt-tessaweḍ tayri. Walaɣ-tt sanda i tt-teẓẓuɣer tderɣalt, walaɣ-tt mi yenta deg-s ujenwi n lexdeɛ, ajenwi n lexdeɛ i d-yekkan seg ufus n laman. Walaɣ-tt mi tt-yenɣa gma-s, gma-s i d-turew tɛebbuṭ n yemma-s ! Acku tḥemmel yiwen, tleḥḥu yid-s; nettat ahat i t-yessugmen i jjwaǧ? ahat i t-yettargun d azgen n yiman-is… netta wissen amek i tt-yundi ?! Ass-nni yerwel, acemma ur t-yuɣ, acemma ur t-yebli! Seg yimir-nni ar tura, ahat acḥal d tiḥbibin i yuqem? ahat yejweǧ, ma mačči d snat, neɣ d tlata tulawin, ma mačči ugar ?! Ahat yettu-tt maḍi ! Walaɣ-tt mi teẓẓel di tlemmast n webrid am usaru, walaɣ-tt mi tt-ɣummen s uḥayek n leḥrir (ur cfiɣ ara ɣef uḥayek-nni ma d win n Lɛecɛaci, neɣ d lemremma ?).

Aḥayek-nni i ttarrant teslatin, ass-nni yebbeqnunnes deg idammen. Ass-nni ɣas meẓẓiyeɣ, d agrud, akken meẓẓiyit igerdan-nni i iteddun ɣer uɣerbaz (lakul). Aɣerbaz-nni yecban taberrakt n wuzzal, acku yezga-d di lḥuma taẓawalit, yezga-d di Bab lḥemra (tawwurt tazeggaɣt, ahat d tawwurt n ǧahennama ).

Teẓẓel di tlemmast n «                      » webrid meskint, tewwi-tt deg yifer-is, tinna akken i yettargun talwit, tayri, tarwa… Teẓẓel zdat yimi n tewwurt uɣerbaz : Amseglu (annex) «Elǧǧewhara / » «la perle , teɣli tǧuhert zdat yisem  «Elǧǧewhara .                      »

Texnunnes deg idammen-is am tixsi yemmezlen deg wass n lɛid, ur d-yecfiɛ deg-s uɣerbaz, ur ixuṭṭ deg-s. Teẓẓel qrib zdat tewwurt n lmuxat (timasurin), imir-nni mazal-itent llant, ur d-tecfiɛ deg-s tmezgida (lǧameɛ irumyen)-nni, ur txuṭṭ deg-s ! Teẓẓel qrib zdat n lwali (ṣellaḥ, lemqam) Sidi Muḥemmed Mull ṣṣur (d aɣrab, d ṣṣur yesɛan tikeddanin akk d txemmjin, ideg ssrusuyen ticemmaɛin d yedrimen ; ttẓurunt-t lxalat, ttɣimint din ssummurent iṭij. Yezga-d di tama ufella n Sidi Lhewwari), ur d-yecfiɛ deg-s ṣelleḥ ur ixuṭṭ deg-s!

Teẓẓel qrib (s waffug n wegḍiḍ neɣ n wefrux) zdat Lalla Meryama (Meryem, yemma-s n Sidna Ɛisa) i d-yeṭṭfen tiɣilt di tmezgida n «Santa kruz , Lalla Meryama i yeldin iɣallen-is ɣer tama n «Lmariyya , amzun tessawal i wid yeḥwaǧen leɛnaya, ur d-tecliɛ di tmexluqt-nni, ur txuṭṭ deg-s !

Zziɣ ɣer tmeddakelt-nni-inu n tmara, kkreɣ ad as-iniɣ : Muqel ar wanda tessawaḍ tayri ! Atnad iḥulfan d
leḥnana i yessawaḍen ɣer nnger ! Kemm teqqareḍ : Nekk d leɛlali, nekk d aggur… kkreɣ a s-iniɣ : Ma yella tḥemmleḍ (ḥṣiɣ tḥemmleḍ), ad teknuḍ, ad tanzeḍ zdat win i tḥemmleḍ, ad tuɣaleḍ d taklit n tayri. Kkreɣ a s-iniɣ : Ayagi i m-n-nniɣ, yekka-yi-d si teqruct n wul, mačči si mraw (10) lewṣayat i d-yersen ɣef Sidna Musa; yernu mačči d kemm i tt-weṣṣiɣ, la ttweṣṣiɣ deg tidak ḥemmleɣ am yessetma, neɣ am yessi. A ziɣ tennejla, tessenser iman-is ɣef tfednin, teǧǧa-yi-d ilem ara yi-iwansen. Cerweɣ-tt merriɣet, nndama ur tt-ufiɣ. Bɣiɣ ad ttuɣ, bɣiɣ ad zhuɣ, greɣ di rradyu tasfift-nni a taɛezzult-inu , bedleɣ tayeḍ :

«              »

Ay aneznaz yekkaten Nekk yufa-yi-d di berra Ɣef teqbaylit m uxelxal Iḍ d wass ur gganeɣ … Teɣli-d tallest, texsi (tensa) tafat, berriket ddunit, yessusem rradyu, d nnuba n tezḍuṭ n yiḍ, d nnuba n tbuɣarin (asbuɣer) n yiḍ; tid akk yettwanɣan wwint-d tirwiḥin-nsent yettijjiqen deg ifassen-nsent, sṭebṭubent-d di tewwurt, ttsuɣunt-d : Sidna Ayub !... Sidna Yunes !... Sidna Nuḥ !…. Rriɣ tiwwura, rniɣ lecqayeq, medleɣ allen-iw, regleɣ (bellɛeɣ) imeẓẓuɣen-iw, lemmer ufiɣ ad rewleɣ ula seg yiman-iw. Nwiɣ a yi-d-tennal talwit, ziɣ d «avirus» i ineṭḍen deg wallaɣ-iw, yessexreb deg-i yal kra yellan d tirga yelhan, yessedrem (ihudd) deg-i kra yellan d asirem; a ziɣen d «mzelzel-ẓekwan» i inedhen deg uqerruy-iw ! Amzun d «ayat lkersi» i d-yettkerrir: «Tikkwal ɣas tura s idammen yessamsen talaba tamellalt n teslit, ma ur d-uragen ara ansi-nniḍen, a d-urugen seg yiri-s ara yezlu gma-s, neɣ baba-s. Tikkwal ɣas tura s idammen yessamsen talaba tamellalt n wegrud amecṭuḥ i wumi xetnen (ṭṭehhren). Tikkwal tura s idammen ara yessimsen talaba tamellalt (lekfen) n lmeyyet mi ara t-yeddez Ɛeẓrayen…»

Wehran ass n 11/08/2006
# Taceṭṭaḥt yeɛyan

n Kamal Buɛrab
IVRISEN
NO_CONTENT_HERE
Amdan mebla idles : yiwet tmu$li

Hamid Bilek

Yella di lemtel, qqaren : « Agdud mebla idles am wemdan mebla iles » ; ma yella a nger tamawt $er yenzi-agi ad naf deg-s sin imeslayen iteddun d tilin d tudert n wemdan, i t-icudden $er tgemmi-ines d umezruy-ines.

Imeslayen-agi d « idles » akk d « iles », mebla yis-sen amdan ad yili ur yelli imi ur iseââu kra n tmu$li $er deffir i wakken ad iéer ansi d-yekka d wansi d-yefruri ; ur iseââu kra n iseddagen ara t-yesseddun $er zdat i wakken ad iéer anda iteddu.

Ahat yezmer ad yidir wemdan u ad yeqqim d netta i d netta s tutlayt d tmeslayt taberranit, maca ur izemmer ara ad iâic akken yella ma yella ur yesâi ara icuddan $er tgemmi d yedles- ines.

Menyaf, i wakken ad yertiê u ad yidir akken iwata, ad yessemlil tameslayt-is d leâwayed n tjaddit-is. Idles d yiles, tasekkurt, timellalin.

Ass-a, mi ara nwali $er wayen iverrun deg umaval s umata, imi neb$a ne$ nugi, aql-a$ nettidir di teswiât anida, ad trekbev tamacint n gemmu ad tiliv ne$ ma yella ur tezmirev, abrid n meêêu d nnger ad yenoer.

Di tallit am tagi, nettwali d akken timusniwin teddunt $er zdat di yal aêric, maççi yal yiwen yezmer a t-yessiwev, isufar n temâict ttnernin ttbeddilen, imdanen merra îîafaren-ten, ur telli kra n talast ara ten- imenâen.
Tutlayin n tussna ufrarent-d, igduden ikesben allalen ussnanen banen, ad qablen taswiât mebla tugdi, ma d wiyiv am nekni, tilin- nne$ d tudert-nne$, deg umaval am win n wass-a, tezmer kan a d- tilili s umezruy, s tgemmi d yedles, imi yal agdud, meééi ne$ meqqer, yekseb tussna ne$ ala, d amerkanti ne$ d igellil, d acebêan ne$ d aberkan, yesâa leâwayed d yensayen yemxallafen $ef yegduden nniven.

Amgarad-agi yellan seg yedles $er wayev yesâa azal-is deg wesnarni n tmusni n t$ermiwin. Yal agdud yettêadar u yettêarab $ef yedles-is, yettqellib ad yissin win n wiyav i wakken talsa ad tennerni di lehna d talwit.

Ulamma annect-a yettban-d d awez$i, imi uget n temsal i yettaooan igduden ttna$en gar-asen. Yettili-d îîrad gar tmura ama $ef temsal n tdamsa ne$ tid n tlisa d wayen nniven. Di tallit yezrin, amnekcam ma yella yeûûawev ad ye$leb axûim-is a t- yeêkem di tmurt-is u ad i$ellet lerbaê-is. Ma d tura, d amnekcam amaynut imi s tussna, d wallalen-agi imaynuten, ur yeêwao ara ad yeédem s lâesker-ines. S lebâid ad ireûûi tutlayt-is d yedles-is.

Deg umnekcam n tallit yezrin ne$ deg win n tura, nettwali d akken ti$awsiwin timezwura yetthuddu, cuddent $er tgemmi d yedles i wakken a s-yishil ad isâeddi tikta-ines u ad yefrev tamu$li-ines akken yeb$a.

Amedya kan akka ur nebâid ara, d win nwala asmi amnekcam amarikani yeévem $ef Be$dad. Di tazwara kan, yeqûed ad yemêu icuddan n wegdud aâiraqi $er tgemmi-ines imi yese$li yakk izamulen d wayen i t-icudden s amezruy-ines.

èéedma n lâesker $ef usalay n tgemmi n Be$dad ad a$-d-yefk lexbar anida iswi-nsen d tukksa n later n t$erma d umezruy lqayen n tmurt-agi.

Imedyaten am wigi îîuqten, ula d tamurt-nne$ tâac tallit anida ayen yeânan idles d umezruy amazi$ ilaq ad yettwasfev, ad yemêu, ur d-iggeri later-is. Tallit tessawev, annect-a di Lezzayer tilellit, alarmi tameslayt tayemmat tettwakkes i warraw-is.

Nni$-d di tazwara d akken agdud ahat yezmer ad yidir s tutlayt taberranit acu kan ad iâic di tgemmi d yedles-ines. Amedya d win nettwali deg wacêal n tmura n ddunit. Tutlayt d taberranit ma d leâwayed d yedles d widak n tnaûlit, nettwali timura n marikan n wenéul, tameslayt d tasbenyulit ne$ d taburtugit maca.
idles d anaûli. Amarikani ulama ihedder taglizit ur k- yeqqar ara nekk d aglizi…

Degmi nettaf d akken awal n tilin d tudert n wegdud icudd nezzeh s idles ugar tutlayt. Di tefriqt ugafa, ulama taârabt teîîef aêric meqqren imi tesâa adabu, maca idles d leâwayed n imezda$-ines mgaraden d win n tmura n usammar alemmas.

Imedyaten îîuqten, timsal akka i teddunt, tudert n wegdud tcudd s amezruy d yedles uqbel ad tcudd $er tdamsa d tussna, $as ulamma allalen imaynuten b$an ad beddlen tilas di tudert n wemdan.

£ef waya i d-neqqar ma yella allalen d iberdan ideg neéwer, neêrec, yeooa-ten lêal, imaynuten i $-d-ibedden $ef tewwurt ne$ i $-d-ikecmen $er tesga ur sen-nezmir ara, ur sen-nessawev ara, abrid ad yenoer kan $er twa$it anida ara d-naf nettâici s loessa kan ur nesâi kra n rruê, kra n umezruy.

D wagi i d tamettant d nnger $ef waydeg yura Dda Lmulud adlis-is « Le banquet ou la mort absurde des Aztèques ». Dda Lmulud inebbeh-ana$-d i wakken ad nessali ssenoaq n tutlayt d yedles-nne$ ma yella neb$a ad nidir u ad nennerni d nekni i d nekni, ma yella imiren neb$a ad a$-tevru am widen yellan ulac-iten yeshel lêal, a nebrut kan i îîbel deg waman imi d ayen isehlen; akken qqaren : Lebni yewâer, ahuddu yeshel.

Ihi ilaq-a$ ad nefrez gar iberdan yessufu$en i wakken ad nidir d nekni s timmad-nne$ nebla ma netti lbista i wakken ad naf iman-nne$ akken i s-yeqqar unazur At Mengellat « Laûel-ik izgel-ik, win teb$iv yugi-k, mel-iyi-d wi k-ilan ».

B$i$ kan ad kfu$ s yiwen n umedya, ad telhu tmu$li deg-s d umeyyez. Wid yettekkan deg useggas n 90 di tlalit n ugezdu n tutlayt d yedles amazi$ n Tizi Wezzu, llan ukin d yiman-nsen imi di tazwara ur qbilen ara talalit n ugezdu n tutlayt kan. èran d akken ur $-yec$ib ara lêal i wakken ad nessufe$ ayen i wumi qqaren « les techniciens de la langue ». èran d akken tutlayt i wakken ad teddu $er zdat, ad tesâu lqima-s u a tebded ilaq-as ad tili di twennaî-is, ad as-d-yezzi yedles d tgemmi-ines. Ur qbilen talalit n ugezdu-agi alarmi d-yedda yedles di lsas-is. Ass-a deg-s nettwali…
# A$yul n wure$

# Habib-Allah Mansouri

# D tasuqelt n « L'Ane d’Or » n « Apulée de Madaure »

# ADLIS AMEZWARU

1- Ri$ ad awen-alse$ dagi kra n teqsivin mgaradent iwumi qqaren tinqisin timilisiyin. D lmuziga êlawen ara yeskikven timezza$in inek, êala ma ur têemmlev ara tasekla tamasôit i d-yusan seg wasif n Nil. Ad twalim iwudam inu, ah ya Rebbi ! amek ad ssiwven imdanen ad beddlen tal$a d ssifa akken ad u$alen deg taggara mavi d imdanen am waken llan deg tazwara. Ad bdu$ ihi, maca deg tazwara yessefk fell-i ad d-ini$ kra n wawalen $ef umeskar. Tiwririn n “Himiîus”, azrug n “Ifiôa”, sakin ad tmagrev “Tinaôus” i d-yezgan deg tmurt n Yisbartiyen, seg yimukan-a i d-u$e$ aéar.

Timnavin-agi, d timnavin n lehna, d tiseâdiyin, tezde$-itent tumert d lferê. D timerkentiyin s wakal nsent, d timnavin ttwabedrent deg yidlisen iqburen. Deg temnavt-agi i lemde$ tutlayt tatikit. Kra n yiseggasen umbaâd, asmi ufi$ iman-iw deg tmurt n yilatiniyen, d aberrani deg tlemmast n tmetti tarumanit, ttuêetme$ ad lemde$ tutlayt nsen mebla ma ufi$ amâiwen ara iyi-yeîîfen afus. Ihi seg tura ad awen-sutre$ ad tessurfem i win ur nessin mliê tutlay-agi $ef yigulen ara yexdem. D ungal agriki ara bdu$ tura. Ay ame$ri ttêessis ! Taqsiî-agi ad ak-teâoeb mliê.
# 2- Wwint-iyi kra n lec$al $er “ Tissalya ”, deg temnavt-agi

i d-tu$ yemma aéar. Aéar swayes zemre$ ad zzuxe$ imi yemma
tekka-d seg “ Blutrak ” ameqqran d wayaw ines afiluzuf
“Sekstus”. Wwve$ ihi $er “ Tissalya ”, tikwal ttali$ idurar, tikwal
tsubbu$ $er
amdan yesbleâ yiwet n tkaba tuqviâ. Mi s-fkan imeshanayen kra n yidrimen, yessekcem yiwen ubudid armi d afwad. Sinakin ha-t-a ibedd yiwen uqrur d ahuskay d icrir $ef ubudid-nni, yebda ccveê d umyebren ad as-tiniv d azrem. Nukni s imeshanayen nbedd kan newhem deg wayen nettwali. Ad as-tiniv d azrem-nni i d-yezzin i tâekkazt n Yakuc n tujjya. Maca deg leânaya-k kemmel-a$-d taqsiî i tebdiv. Nekk ad amne$ ayen ad a$-d-talsev, yernu mi ara nawev $er uzerbiz amezwaru ad ak-sellke$ imekli. D wagi i d asefk inu.

# 5 - Yenna-iyi :

“ Tanemmirt tameqqrant $ef usefk inek. Ad ak-d-êku$ taqsiî amek i tebda deg tazwara irkelli. Maca uqbel, ad ak-ggale$ s Yakuc n yiîij yettwalin kulci ayen ara d-ini$ tura d tidet yernu mi ara tawvev $er temdint tatisalit ad teksev ccek s timmad-ik, acku medden yakk ttmeslayen $ef tedyanin-agi yevran sdat n wallen nsen. Deg tazwara ilaq ad teérev lasel-iw. Isem-iw “ Arisîuminis ”, usi$-d seg “ Ijyun ”, ilaq ad teérev da$en d acu i xeddme$ : snuzu$ tammemt, aguglu d sselâa niven i wid sselêayen izebrizen, ttinige$ da$en deg yal tama n “ Tissalya ”, “Etulya ”, “ Byutya ”. Ihi imi sli$ snuzun deg “ Hibbata ”, tamdint tameqqrant yellan deg “ Tissalya ”, aguglu ajdid yelhan yernu s ssuma irexsen mliê, uzzle$ ad a$e$ kulci. Maca am wakken iyi-tverru lebda, ass-nni yezgel-iyi zzher. Ass-nni ssar me$ ad rebêe$ ciîîuê n yidrimen, maca kulec yufeg. Leâca-nni iruê-d yiwen umastag ameqqran “ Lubbus ” yu$-d kulci. Tazzla-agi mebla lfayda tesseâya-iyi maççi d kra. Mi d-ye$li yiv ruêe$ $er lêemmam, (6) deg ubrid-iw mmugre$-d “ Suqraî ” ameddakel- iw aqdim. Ufi$-t yeqqim $ef lqaâa, $ef uârur-is yiwen ubalîu yeqres irkelli, aqadum-is d awra$, qrib ur t-âqile$, yevâef mliê, ssifa-s tessewêac, ad as-tiniv d yiwen seg yimattaren-nni yessuturen deg yiberdan. Ufi$-t deg yir liêala, uée$ $ur-s s leâqel, nni$-as : “ Ah ya “ Suqraî ” iâzizen, d acu i k-yu$en akka ? Twalav iman-ik ? Akka ay d lefviêa ! Axxam-ik $ilen temmutev, arraw-ik sâan tura lwalyin niven, tameîîut-ik teâya deg umeîîi fell-ak, qrib i tedder$el. Baba-as akked yemma-s êettmen fell-as ad tâiwed zzwaj akken ad tesekcem tumert $er uxxam i yu$ leêzen. Keçç am alaxert, ur tetûevêiv, ur tenneêcamev aql-ik da, tbeddev sdat-i !
Yerra-yi-d : “ Arisîuminis ”, ur teériv ara tilufa iyi-yu$en, zzher- iw yekêes ”. Imi iyi-ihedder yenneêcam, yeffer udem-is deffir n ucluê ines iqersen, tafekka ines i d-yezgan gar timiî d yimessaven-is banent-d irkelli. Yeqreê-iyi mliê wul-iw mi t- wala$ deg lêif-agi, fki$-as afus-iw, wwi$-t yid-i ad yessired.

# 7- Mazal-it yeqqim $ef tmurt, i$umm aqerru-is, iâeggev :

“Deg leânaya-k anef-as i zzher ad yurar yis-i amek i as-yehwa !” Ssawve$ ad t-qenâe$ ad yeddu yid-i, kkse$ yiwen seg sin n yiselsa i lsi$, selse$-as-t s tem$awla. Deg tilawt d a$ummu kan i t-$umme$ yis-s, wwi$-t $er lêemmam. D nekk i as-yefkan zzit ad yedhen tafekka ines, taserbit ad yeskaw iman-is. D nekk da$en i as-iêukken tafekka ines, kkse$-as akk injan i yedlen aglim-is. Mi kfi$, $as akken âyi$ mliê, ur zmire$ ara ad bedde$ $ef yivarren- iw, wwi$-t yid-i $er usensu anda kri$ taxxamt, s tmara i t- zzu$re$, d netta ur yezmir ara ad yelêu, yeâya. Skecme$-t daxel n wusu akken ad yeêmu, fki$-as ad yeçç, ad isew armi yeôwa, rni$ êki$-as ula d timucuha akken ad yennecraê. Ha-t-a yu$al yettmeslay, yettseqsi. Nebda ameslay $ef waîas n temsal, armi i s-iserreê i yiwet n nnehta i d-yeff$en seg yidmaren-is, sakin yebda yekkat deg unyir-is : “ Nekk d ame$bun ur nesâi zzher ! Ssebba iyi-d-yerran deg liêala-agi d amennu$ i b$i$ ad wali$. Am wakken teériv, ruêe$ $er “ Maqdunya ” i lmend n tnezzut inu, mraw n wagguren umbaâd u$ale$-d s lfayda tameqqrant. Deg ubrid n tu$alin, uqbel ad laêqe$ $er “ Larissa ” (dagi i ri$ ad wali$ amennu$-nni) deg yiwet n talut lqayen, tettwaâezzel, $lin-d fell-i yimakaren seg yal tama.

£as akken âerran-iyi irkelli, ulac acu iyi-yeooan, ssawve$ ad asen-rewle$, sutre$ deg yiwet n tmeîîut yeîîfen yiwet n tberna ad iyi-tâiwen. Tameîîut-agi qqaren-as “ Miôuwi ”, telêa deg leâmer, maca xas akken mazal-itt temleê, tesâa sser. Ëki$-as ssebba n yinig inu d tu$alin inu, ulse$-as ssebba n tigullelt anda iyi-d-tufa. Nettat seg tama-s tbedd $ur-i akken iwata lêal, tesnubbeg-iyi $er yiwen n yimekli igerrez, yernu baîel. Sakin teârev-iyi ad cerke$ usu ines. Seg wass-nni u$ale$-as d akli, ur zmire$ ara ad as- îîixre$.

Ula d iclaê-nni iyi-ooan imakaren-nni d yidrimen-nni i êella$ asmi jehde$, xeddme$ d aêemmal fki$-as-ten, armi wwve$ $er
liêala-agi anda iyi-d-tufiv. Wagi irkelli yekka-d seg zzher inu uâwij d tmeîîut-agi tahuskayt.

# 8- Nni$-as :

“ S yisem n Yakuc “ Buliks ”, tuklalev ssexva tameqqrant, textarev ad d-tevfrev zzhu d ti$imit d yiwet n tcermuvt $ef uxxam-ik d warraw-ik ”. Netta yerra ccahed $er yimi-s, yeqqim deg umkan-is yeqqur, yenna-yi-d : “ Ess ! Ess ! ” yebda yettmuqqul $er yal tama akken ad iéer ma yezmer ad yemmeslay mebla akukru : “ Wiya-k, wiya-k ad d-tiniv lêaoa mgal tameîîut-agi yesâan adabu nnig-amagan ne$ ma ulac ad ak-ya$ ayen diri ma tessugtev awal.

# Nni$-as :

- Ay$er ? d acu-tt tmeîîut-agi tanezmart, tin yesselêayen tberna ? D timkerrert, d taseêêart yesâan adabu meqqren gar yifassen-is. Tezmer ad tessider igenni, ad tâelleq akal, ad teskew tiliwa, ad thudd idurar, ad tessekfel lmeyytin, ad tessider iyakucen, ad tessexsi itran, ad tnewwer amaval yellan ddaw n wakal.

# Nni$-as :

- Deg leânaya-k, kkes fell-i liéar-agi atrajiki, mmeslay-d s wawalen i nezmer ad negzi. Teb$iv ad ak-mmeslaye$ $ef tigawin ines n ukerrer ? Tezmer ad terr medden âecqen deg-s, ur ttmeslaye$ ara $ef wid ized$en dagi tama-s, la k-heddre$ $ef Yihendiyen ne$ Ityubiyen akked imezda$ n tama niven n ddunit. Wagi $ur-s maççi d ayen iweâren, d lleâb ne$ d aqesser. Ha-t-a d acu texdem sdat n wallen n wacêal n yimdanen.

# 9- Yiwen seg yimeâcaq ines i teîîef gar yi$allen n tmeîîut niven terra-t, s yiwen n wawal kan, d abkur, acku a$ersiw-agi ma yeggad igezzem tiwellaqin ines akken ur i$elli ara gar yifassen n yiseggaven.

D wagi i tessaram ad yevru. Yiwen seg loiran-is ula d netta yesâa yiwet n tberna, terra-t d agru ne$ d amqerqer. Ha-t-an tura ume$bun la yettâummu daxel yiwet n tbettit, yettak azul s uswe$we$ azuran i yimectariyen ines n zik. Yiwet n tmeîîut n yiwen seg yimeâcaq ines asmi i tt-tergem s leqseê tella s tadist, te$leq-as aâebbuv-is, terra llufan-nni d amgun, seg wass-nni mazal-itt s tadist, $ef wawal n medden ha-tt-an tura deg useggas.
wis îam seg wasmi terfed, aâ ebbuv-is icuff maççi d kra, ad as-tiniv d ilu ara d-tarew.

# 10-

Imdanen bdan reffun, aîas i tvur, mtafaqen ad txelles lefâayel-is. Msefhamen azekka-nni ad tt-rejmen. Maca s lfevl n ukerrer ines tfaq i wayen ttdebbiren. Am “Midya” yessawven ad tervel yiwen n wass s$ur “Kriyun” akken ad tessre$ axxam n ugellid s tmes yeff$en seg tesmert (am$ar d yelli-s r$an deg tmes-nni), timkerrert-agi tessekfel-d aéekka akken ad theggi akerrer ines. Wagi irkelli tenna-a$-t-id ussan-agi ineggura mi teûkeô. Tessawev ad teêbes imezda$-nni deg yixxamen nsen. S îul n sin n wussan ulac win yessawven ad yerreé leqfel ne$ ad yekkes tiwwura seg yimukan nsent ne$ ad yeflu leêyuv, armi tt-âuhden irkelli belli ulac win ara tt-inalen, yernu ma ixulef walbaâv lâahed-agi, ad bedden mgal-is, ad tt-âiwnen, yernu ad tt-selken. Mi tesla i yimeslayan-agi tessuffe$-iten seg lêebs anda llan. Maca win yellan deffir n takti-agi tessuffeg-it deg yiwen n yiv berriken, yiwen n yiv mebla tiziri, am netta am uxxam-is, b$i$ ad ini$ leêyuv, akal d llsas, akkenni ye$leq $er yiwen n umkan ibeâden timivi n yimilen, $er yiwet n temdint niven i d-yezgan $ef tqacuct n yiwen n udrar yeêecruref irkelli, anda ulac ula d tiqit n waman. Imi ur d-tufi ara anda ad d-tessers axxam-agi deg tlemmast n yi$rem, acku yeêreû umkan, tvegger-it sdat n tewwurt n temdint, sakin tu$al seg wanda d-tekka mebla ma teooa-d later deffir-s.

# 11-

“Tiqsivin-agi i d-tewwiv a “Suqraî” ssewhament, yernu ssefqaâent maççi d kra. A-t-an tura teskecmev-iyi anezgum ameqqran, b$i$ ad ini$ agad ameqqran. Maççi d axsif iyi-d-tessentav, d uzzal mi ara d-mmekti$ adabu nnig-amagan i tesâa tem$art-agi, adabu s wayes tezmer ad tsell i lehdur-agi i d-newwi fell-as. Tura ilaq ad neîîes zik akken ad nekkes âeggu-agi, azekka deg tafrara yessefk fell-a$ ad nerwel syagi $er umkan niven ibeâden.”

Mazal ur kfi$ awal, armi ufi$ “Suqraî” argaz n lâali win ur nu$en ara tannumi ad isew annect-a n ccrab, win yeâyan aîas, yesxerxur, tewwi-t tnafa. Rri$ tawwurt, $elqe$-tt s tsekkart, serse$ ssrir inu ameéyan tama n tewwurt-nni, ééle$ ad gne$. Deg tazwara aggad inu ur iyi-yeooa ara ad îse$, maca deg tlemmast n
yiv allen-iw bdant qemmcent s leâqel kan. Mazal ur îîise$ ara mi êulfa$ i yiwet n tyita tejhed, yernu maççi d tin n yimakaren. Tiyita-agi ur teldi ara tawwurt, teréa-tt ! Teqleâ-d ula d iqevban. Ssrir inu ameéyan, awezlan iwumi ixuss yiwen uvar, yeçça-t burekku, yenneqlab, ur faqe$ ara amek ufi$ iman-iw ddaw-s, i$umm-iyi irkellli.

# 12-

Imir-n kan faqe$ llant kra n tegnatin anda amdan ur iéerr ara acu ixeddem. Tikwal yezmer ad yeîîerveq d imeîîawen ma yefreê. Deg liêala anda lli$ ass-nni, $as akken aggad yen$a-iyi, serrêe$-as i yiwet n tevsa mi wala$ iman-iw seg “Arisîuminis” amdan u$ale$ d ifker. Ufi$ iman-iw ééle$ deg tlemmast n yivumman, ameîreê $ef uqerru-iw, i$umm-iyi irkelli, âerve$ ad wali$ ayen i verrun tama-w. Wala$ snat n tlawin lêant yakan deg leâmer, meqqrit, yiwet teîîef gar yifassen amesbaê yecâel, tayev teddem ccencafa d ssif ne$ takaba. Beddent $ef uqerru n “Suqraî” yeîîsen a m ugrud. Tin yeddmen takaba tenna : “ Ha-t-an a ultma “ Bantya ”, “Andimyun” inu ameâzuz, “Ganimad” inu, win yuraren s teméi-w, win inekren tayri-w, yernu nnig n waya ur iyi-yergim ara kan, ihegga iman-is i trewla. Yeb$a ad u$ale$ am “ Kalibsu ”-nni, tin i yeooa “ Uliss ”, ad terre$ kan i yimeîîi $ef sseâd-iw ? ” Sakin tevleq i$il-is, twehha-d $ur-i, d$a tenna-as i ultma-s “ Bantya ” : “ I umdan-agi “ Arisîuminis ” ivebren tarewla-agi, yellan tura $ef tizi n terwiêt, ha-t-an tura yeééel $ef lqaâa ddaw n umeîreê ines aqdim yettmuqqul ddaw n tiî ayen iverrun, i$il ad yemneâ, ur yettxellis ara rregmat ines. Anef-as i wagi ad lethu$ yis-s umbaâd, ri$ ad d-ini$ mebla leâvil, imir-a, tura, akken ad yendem $ef yir awal i d-yenna ivelli d lekluf ines n wass-a !

# 13-

Mi sli$ i lehdur-nni, teccef-iyi tidi tasemmavt, teîîef-iyi tergagayt, êulfa$ i umeîreê-nni yellan nnig-iw yettembiwil. Sli$-as i “ Bantya” teqqar : “ Ay$er a ultma ur nbeddu ara s uslax ines am wakken xeddment “Tibaxniyint”, ne$ ay$er ur s-ngezzem ara ddker ines ? ” Terra-as-d “ Miruwi ” $ef yisumar-agi : “ Ala, ilaq ad t-neoo ad yidir i wakken, ma ulac mavi, ad yemvel ljetta n ume$bun-agi ”. Faqe$ imir-n belli d tameîîut-agi i$ef iyi-d-yemmeslay “Suqraî”.
sakin tesmal aqerru n “ Suqraî” $ef tama tayeffust, tesenta-as takaba deg umgerv. Tejmeâ idammen n ume$bun-nni deg yiwen n uyeddid amecîuê mebla ma teooa later. Wagi ayen walant wallen-iw. Ugar n waya, ahat i wakken ad tkemmel tigawin n t$ersawt, tessekcem “ Miruwi ” afus-is deg waggas ne$ ljerê-nni armi d afwad, teqleâ-d ul n umeddakel-iw meskin yessuf$en yiwen ujjiq, ne$ yiwen usêiooew seg tgerjumt i tezla tkaba, s ssut-agi yessuffe$ tarwiêt. “Bantya” tergel aggas-nni s ccencafa, tenna : “Kemmini a ccencafa i d-ilulen deg yillel, wiya-m ad as-îîixrev ! ” Mi kfant, kkrent ad ruêent, maca uqbel mi ad ff$ent, refdent ameîreê inu, qqumcent nnig n wudem-iw, beccent-iyi, u$ale$ ttriêi$ s yir rriêa : rriêa n waman n tasa.

14- Akken kan zegrent amnar, tu$al tewwurt-nni s amkan-is, ad as-tiniv ulac d acu i tt-yu$en. Iqevban-nni kecmen s imukan nsen, tisekkarin u$alent am wakken llant zik. Nekk mazal-iyi ééle$ $ef lqaâa, serâe$, âeryan, bezge$ s ibeccan amzun seg uâebbuv n yemma i d-ff$e$. Qqime$ deg umkan-iw, ttraju$ kan melmi ara iyi-yen$en : “ Acu ara yevrun yid-i asmi ara d-afen azekka argaz-agi yemmzel ? Anwa ara yamnen s teqsiî ara êku$, xas akken ayen ara d-ini$ d tidet ? ad iyi-d-inin : “ Ay$er ur tessawlev ara i l$it, imi ur tezmirev ara, argaz am keçççini, ad tbeddev deg wudem n yiwet n tmeîîut. Ha-t-an yevleq sdat-k yiwen n urgaz yemmzel, yernu keçççini awal ur k-id-yuli, tessusmev kan ? Yernu keççini ulac acu i k-yu$en, iwacu ur k-n$int ara am netta ? Acimi i d-ooant deffir-nsent inigi izemren ad tent-yessenzen umbaâd ? Ihi akka, imi trewlev i lmut, u$al $ur-s tura ! ”

Qqime$ la ttalse$ timsal-agi deg walla$-iw, iv yelêa, tafrara qrib ad d-tbin. Ëala tarewla iyi-yegran, tarewla deg tafrara $as akken tigecrar inu ttergigint. Ddme$ tagemmust-iw, skecme$ tasarut deg leqfel, âerve$ ad ldi$ tawwurt, maca tagi i yeldin leâca-nni tugi ad teldi tura. Qqime$ la ttdewwire$ tasarut-nni acêal d abrid mebla lfayda.

15- Sin $er-s bdi$ aâeggev : “ Hi ! Anda-k ? Anda telliv ? Ldi-iyi tawwurt n usensu, ri$ ad ff$e$ uqbel tafrara. ” Axeddam-nni yeîîes deffir n tewwurt n usensu yu$-it lêal mazal
yettnuddum, yerra-yi-d awal : “ Acu ? ! Keçç i yeb$an ad yinigen deg tnafsa n yiv, ur teériv ara belli iberdan ççuren s yimakaren ? Yernu $as akken ur éri$ ara d acu abaxix i txedmev i k-yeooan teb$iv ad ten$ev iman-ik, ur nelli ara d iqerra n texsayt, d ungufen akken ad nemmet $ef derra-k.

Nni$-as : - Ass qrib ad yali, yernu d acu i zemren ad akren imakaren i yiminig yenêafen am nekk ? Ur teériv ara ay unguf belli mraw n yimdanen ur zmiren ara ad âerrin amdan yellan d aâeyran yakan ? ” Mi yesla i lehdur-agi inu, yerra-yi-d, allen-is rwint irkelli, mazal ur yeôwi ara ives : “ Maca ini-iyi-d, yezmer lêal tezliv arfiq inek d wumi tcerkev taxxamt leâca, tura tettnadiv amek ad trewlev akken ad tesmenâev aqerru-ik ? ”

Cfi$ deg ddqiqa-nni wala$ lqaâa teldi ddaw n yivarren-iw, am wakken wala$ lqaâ n umaval n wadda d uqjun n unazir “Sirbir ” yesâan aîas n yiqerra ihegga-d iman-is ad iyi-yesebleâ. Imir-n i d-nni$ i yiman-iw, ma yella “ Miruwi ” timkerrert ur iyi-tezli ara maççi d a$ivi i tt-$ave$, d asderwec i teb$a ad iyi-tesderwec, tra ad iyi-iâelqen $ef umidag.

16- Ihi, u$ale$ $er texxamt-iw, bdi$ ttnadi$ amek ara n$e$ iman-iw. Imi zzher-iw yezleg, ur ufi$ ara ta$awsa swayes ara n$e$ iman-iw, ulac acu i sâi$ bexlaf ameîreê, d$a âegve$-d : “ Ay ameîreê, ay ameîreê inu âzizen, keçç i yeôwan lmerta yid-i leâca-agi, keçç i yellan d inigi $ef wayen akk yevran iv yezrin, êala keçç i wumi zemre$ ad ssiwle$ ad yeched yid-i belli d amesli i lli$, ulac acu xedme$, mmel-iyi-d -êare$ ad ssube$ $er Unazir-mmel-iyi-d amek ara xedme$ akken ad rre$ tilisa i tudert-iw. ” Mi kfi$ lehdur-iw, ddme$ amrar-nni, sâedda$-t $ef yiwen n ujgu i d-yezgan ddaw n yiwen n îîaq, ccude$-t mliê, s îîerf niven uqme$ takerrist tejhed, uli$ $ef umeîreê, hegga$ iman-iw ad mmte$, skecme$ aqerru-iw daxel n tserrift. Mi nwi$ ad deggre$ s uvar-iw ameîreê-nni i$ef bedde$ akken ad iyi-yexneq umrar-nni, ha-t-a yeqres, d$a $li$ $ef “ Suqraî ” yeîîsen tama n ssrir inu, negrareb-d deg sin yid-ne$ $ef tmurt.

17- Imir-n kan yekcem-d uxeddam s uâeggev : “ Anda telliv, keçç iêaren $er tuff$a deg tnafsa n yiv, tesxerxurev tura ddaw n tduli ? ” Ur éri$ ara ma yella d a$elluy-nni ne$ d aâeggev n
uxeddam iyi-yesduqsen. D “ Suqraî ” i d-yekkren d amezwaru, yenna : “ Ur $liven ara iminigen imi kerhen ixeddamen n yizebrizen. Ha-t-a yiwen uêettac iyi-yesduqsen s unekcum ines $er texxamt yessufe$-iyi seg yives lqayen $as akken âyi$ maççi d kra. Ahat d takerva i yeb$a ad a$-yaker ? ”

Kkre$-d, tumert teççur ul-iw, tu$al-iyi terwiêt mi sli$ i ta$ect n “ Suqraî ”, d$a nni$-d : “ Wali tura ay aâessas n usensu, ha-t-a urfiq-iw, gma âzizen, i d-tenniv leâca-agi mi tsekrev belli n$i$-t”.

Imi heddre$, îîfe$ “ Suqraî ” gar yi$allen-iw, bdi$ la tessudune$. Maca netta imi yesraê deg-i yir rriêa n waman n tasa n temkerrerin-nni, ivegger-iyi akkin : “ Aé akkin, tettraêev am uqelwac ! ”, d$a yesseqsa-yi s leâqel ay$er i ttriêi$ akka. Nekk setêa$, ur ufi$ ara acu ara s-ini$, rri$-tt i uqesser d umesxer akken ad as-settu$ aseqsi ines, umbaâd nni$-as : “ Ilaq ad nruê tura akken ad nfaôes tikli deg tnezzayt ! ”

Ddme$ tagemmust inu, sellke$ azal n texxamt, nu$ abrid nne$.

18- Nelêa cwiî, iîij yu$ akk tamurt. Qqime$ ttmuqule$ deg temgerî n urfiq-iw anda tenta tkaba, nni$-d deg wul-iw : “ Ay aderwic, d ccrab d naddam i k-yesdubbzen d$a turgav yir tergit. Ha-t-a “ Suqraî ” ibedd sdat-k, ulac acu i t-yu$en. Anda-t waggas-nni ? I ccencafa-nni anda-tt ? I ccama-nni tameqqrant i teooa tiyita n tkaba anda-tt ula nettat ? neîqe$, nni$-as : “ Kra n yimejjayen imeqqranen ur $liîen ara mi d-nnan ma nessaget uççi d ccrab nxeddem yir tirga. Leâca mi sekre$ cwiî, sâedda$ yir taswiât, urga$ kra n tirga sefqaâent mliê, yernu ara iv-a mazal ttêulfu$ i yiman-iw umse$ s yidammen n umdan. ”

Yerra-yi-d s uzmummeg : “ Ala maççi s yidammen i tumsevn s yibeccan ! Ula d nekk urga$ zlan-iyi, teqreê-iyi mliê temgerî-iw. Ëulfa$ am wakken d aqlaâ iyi-qelâen ul-iw seg yidmarren-iw, yernu ar tura mazal ur ssawve$ ara ad rre$ nnehta akken ilaq. Tigecrar-iw mazal-itent ttergigint, leêêu$ s une$luyev. Yessefk ad ççe$ lêaoa akken ad izmire$ ad bedde$. ”

Nni$-as : “ Imekli ihegga yakan ”.

Ddme$ aqrab i bubbe$ $ef tayet-iw fki$-as a$rum d uguglu, nni$-as : “ Iya-d ad neqqim ddaw n useklu-agi. ”
19- Imi neqqim, ddme$ ula d nekk cwiî seg u$rum-nni. Simmal ttmuqule$ deg urfiq-iw, simmal yettenbeddal uqadum-is, yettu$al d awra$ am tâeqqayt n lqares. eggu yugi ad as-yekkes, simmal irennu fell-as. Ssifa-s tbeddel irkelli, uggade$ maççi d kra, nni$-as ahat d timkerrerin-nni i d-u$alent, ula imi n u$rum i gre$ deg uqemmuc-iw, $as akken d amecîuê, yewqeâ-iyi. Nnig n waya amkan-nni yeâzel, ulac win i yettâeddin syin, d ayen ikemmlen fell-i. Anwa-t umdan-agi ur nettamnen ara ma yufa sin yimsebriden, yiwen deg-sen yemmut, belli maççi d wayev i t-yen$an ? Mi yessebleâ “ Suqraî ” tiremt ines, yen$a-t fad, d aêric ameqran n uguglu i yeçça. Yernu sdat n useklu anda i neddari yettazzal yiwen n wasif aman-is d iméerfen. Nni$-as : “ Ruê ad teswev aman deg wasif-a akken ad teksev fad ”. Yekker, yebda aqelleb $ef yiwen n umkan iwatan, yessers tigecrar ines $ef lqaâa, yekna $er sdat akken ad isew. Icenfiren-is urâad nulen aman, ha-t-a yeldi waggas ines, ccencafa-nni te$li-d, uzzlen yidammen. Tafekka ines qrib ad te$li deg wasif amer ur uzzle$ ara ad t-îîfe$ seg yivarren akken ad t-serse$ $ef rrif n wasif. Ur êbise$ ara imeîîi $ef urfiq-iw ame$bun, aîas i ttru$ fell-as uqbel ad t-mevle$ ddaw n yijdi i d-yezzin i wasif. Teîîef-iyi tergagayt, uggade$ mliê $ef yiman-iw, uggade$ ad iyi-yeîîfen, d$a îîfe$ abrid n trewla. Yernu imi mazal daxel-iw tselbibat am wakken d nekk i t-yen$an, ooi$ tamurt-iw d uxxam-iw, nfi$ iman-iw, ruêe$ $er “ Etulya ” anda zed$e$, umbaâd mi âawde$ zzwaj.

20- Ha-t-an acu i d-yenna “ Arisîuminis ”, maca arfiq ines seg tazwara ur yumin ara s lehdur-agi, iâeggev yenna-d : “ Ulac acu yessewhamen am teqsit-agi, uroin sli$ i tkerkas yifen tigi ”, sakin yezzi-d $ur-i yenna-yi-d : “ I keççini, am wakken ttwali$ seg lebsa inek d lefâayel-ik maççi d menwala, tumnev s teqsit-agi? Nni$-as : - Nekk, ur ttamne$ ara s uwez$i, ayen yuran deg yigenwan ad yevru i umdan. Muqel, tidyanin am tigi zemrent ad vrunt i nekk, i keçç, i yimdanen irkelli. Tidyanin am tigi ma yella uroin vrant i wayev, ma teêkiv-tent i wiyav, yezmer lêal ad ak-mmuqlen s yir tamu$li. Ayen yeânan argaz-agi lâali, yessefk fell-ane$ ahat ad t-nesnemmer aîas-aîas imi yessawev ad a$-yessedhu îul n tsawent-agi mebla ma nêulfa-as. Yernu ula amerkub-agi inu yumer imi wwve$ $er tewwurt n temdint mebla ma sâetbe$-t, amzun maççi d aârur-is i d-iyi-baben, d imezza$ inu iyi-refden.
21- D wigi i d lehdur nne$ ineggura, newwev $er taggara n ubrid i d-newwi lwaêid. Irfiqen-nni deg sin yid-sen îîfen abrid yettawin $er tama tazelmavt, ad ruêen $er yiwen n leâzib amecîuê yellan deg temnavt-nni. Nekk ruêe$ srid $er uzebriz amezwaru i d-mmagre$ sdat n tewwurt n yi$rem, d$a steqsa$ tin yeîîfen lemêel-nni ma deg temdint n “ Hibbata ” i lli$ ? Tenna-yi-d : “ ih !” Nni$-as : “ Tesnev yiwen ssawalen-as “ Milun ”, yiwen seg yi$ermanen imezwura ? ” Teîîerveq d tavsa, tenna-yi-d : “ D tidet ! “ Milun ” inek d yiwen seg yi$ermanen imezwura, yezde$ berra n yi$rem. ” Neîqe$ $ur-s, nni$a-s : “ Ma ulac u$ilif, berka tiqecmeât tura a yemma tam$art, deg leânaya-m ma ur tenniv d acu i d ssenf n umadan i yella, akked anda i yezde$ ? Tenna-yi : twalav îîwiqan-nni ibeâden i d-yettakken $er yi$rem, d tawwurt-ihinna i d-yessuffu$en $er tezniqt ? din i yezde$ “ Milun ” inek, d yiwen unesba$ur ameqqran, maca amdan-a ten$a-t cceêêa, ireîîel s tmerna $ef waya i ye$li uzal-is gar medden. Ayen yejmeâ $ur-s d rrhinat itteffer-it deg yiwet n texxamt. Tameîîut-is, ad yili Rebbi yid-s, teôwa lmerta. Ar tura mazal-as yiwet n tqeddact kan, mi ad yeffe$, ad as-tiniv d amattar, acku maççi d iselsa i yelsa, d iclaê i yerra $ef uârur-is. ”

Imi sli$ i lehdur-agi, rri$-as s tavsa : “ Ad yeêrez Rebbi ameddakel-iw “ Dimyas ” iyi-d-yuznen $er yiwen n umdan am wagi, d netta iyi-d-yennan ma kecme$ s axxam-is ur ttaggade$ rriêa n wabu ne$ rriêa n usewwi deg tenwalt ! ”

22- Lêi$ kra n yisurifen $er sdat, bedde$ $ef umnar n tewwurt, spebîbe$ $ef yiwet n tewwurt teççur d isevra, bdi$ la ssawala$ i at uxxam. Deg taggara tejba-d yiwet n teqcict tameéyant, tenna-yi-d : “ A winnat, keçç yekkaten $ef tewwurt s zzur d acu-tt rrhina i d-tewwiv akken ad tawiv areîîal ? Ahat êala keçç ur neéri belli ur nqebbel êala rrhinat n wure$ ne$ n uzref ? Nni$-as : Qabel-iyi-d s wudem yelhan ma ulac u$ilif. Ini-iyi-d tura ma yella Mass inem deg uxxam ? Tenna-d : Yirbeê, maca ay$er asteqsi-agi ?

- Wwi$-as-d tabrat i s-yura “ Dimyas ” seg “ Kurintya ”.

- Rou dagi seg leâvil ad as-ini$.

Taqcict-nni tekcem, terra deffir-s isevra n tewwurt. Kra n lweqt umbaâd ha-tt-a tu$al-d, teldi-iyi-d tawwurt, tenna-d : “ La k-d-
yessawal ”. Kecme$, ufi$-t yeééel $ef yiwen umeîreê d amecîuê, imir-n kan i yebda imensi ines. £er yivarren-is teqqim tmeîîut-is, sdat-s ters yiwet n tgida d tilemt. Yessken-iyi-tt-id : “ Tagi i yinebgi”. Nni$-as : - “ Yerbeê ”, sakin fki$-as tabrat n “ Dimyas ”. Ye$ra-tt s tem$awla, yenna-d : “ Ad snemmre$ ameddakel-iw “ Dimyas ” âzizen iyi-yuznen inebgi yesâan azal meqqren, maççi d menwala”

23- Yessuter deg tmeîîut-is ad teffe$, yevleb deg-i ad a$e$ amkan-is, maca setêa$, bedde$ kan deg umkan-iw armi iyi-yeîîef seg tlaba inu, yejbed-iyi $ur-s, yenna : “ Qim dagi, nuggad imakaren, $ef waya ulac akersi ne$ iruka ilaqen. ” U$e$-as awal. Ikemmel deg wawal-is : “ Mi ad wali$ kan tesrifa d leêya inek yettemcabin $er win n tullas, ad ggale$ - yernu ur $ellîe$ ara ma nni$-d keçç maççi d menwala, keçç d ahaggar. Yernu ameddakel-iw “ Dimyas ” yeêka-yi-d kullec deg tebrat-agi ines. Ihi ma ulac u$ilif ur êeqqer ara axxam inu uvyiq. Tura ad ak-d-fke$ taxxamt, ur nebâid ara $ef umkan-agi iwakken ad testeâfuv akken iwata lêal. Ri$ ad ak-yeâjeb mliê lêal dagi yid-ne$. S tem$er inek ad tesme$rev axxam-agi, ad tesnerniv deg ccan-ik imi tqeblev ad teqqimev deg yiwen n uxxam amecîuê, d$a swagi ad ta$ev abrid n “ Tisyus ” ameqqran, win i$ef semman baba-k, ur neêqir ara tinnubga n “ Hikali ” tam$art. Sakin yessawel-d i tqeddact tamecîuêt : “ Futis ”, $iwel ruê awi-d ifecka n yinebgi nne$, sers-iten s leâqel deg texxamt, $iwel ddem da$en seg uxmil zzit i lêemmam, rnu-as tiserbitin akken ad yeskaw tafekka ines akked t$awsiwin niven, sin $er-s awi-t srid $er lêemmam iqerben, iban $ef yinebgi nne$ âeggu n yinig a$ezfan i yexdem.

24- Mi sli$ i lehdur-agi, mmekta$-d cceêêa n “ Milun ”, d$a uggade$ ad iyi-iwali s yir tiî, d$a nni$-as : “ Tanemmirt tameqqrant, ulac acu êwaje$, acku ttawi$ yid-i yakk ayen i tteêwiji$ mi ad inige$. £ef lêemmam, yeshel ad d-afe$ yiwen, mi ad ff$e$ ad steqsi$. Maca ayen iyi-cu$ben mliê d ayis inu iyi-d-yewwin armi dagi. Deg leânaya-m a “ Futis ”, ax idrimen, a$-as-d asa$ur d teméin. ”

Ruêe$ ad qeâde$ lqecc-iw deg texxamt iyi-d-fkan, mi kfi$ u$e$ abrid n lêemmam. edda$ uqbel $ef ssuq ad a$e$ ayen ara neçç.
Deg ssuq-nni wala$ kra n yiselman acki-ten, sersen-ten i lbiâ. Mi steqsa$ $ef ssuma nsen, nnan-iyi-d swan timivi n “sesters”, maca ugi$ ad ten-id-a$e$ s ssuma-nni, ooan-ten-iyi-d s snat n timmav n “dinyers”. Mazal ur ffi$e$ ara seg ssuq armi d-mmugre$ “Fityas”, yiwen seg yimeddukal d wumi $ri$ deg “Atina”. £as akken acêal n yiseggasen aya ur nemméir, yeâqel-iyi, yuéa-d $ur-i, yeîîef-iyi gar yi$allen-is, yebda la asuden deg-i, d$a yenna: “Lusyus” âzizen! aîas aya ur nemméir, d tidet, s yisem n “Hiraklis”, seg wasmi nekfa leqraya nne$ $er uselmad nne$ “Klityus”. D acu i k-id-yewwin $er temnavt-agi?

Nni$-as: - Azekka ad twaliv… maca acu i ttwali$ akka? Mebruk fell-ak. Zzin-ak-d ixeddamen, d anawur ameqqran i tu$alev.

- D nekk i yeîîfen lumur n usikrer. Ma teêwajev kra, aql-iyi da.

Snemre$-t seg wul, acku s yiselman i d-u$e$ sâi$ acu ara a$-iqiden i yimensi nne$. Mi iwala “Fityas” taqeffut inu, yeddem-itt, imuqel iselman-nni i d-u$e$: “Acêal i txelsev yir sselâa-agi?”

Nni$-as: “S tmara i ssawve$ ad ten-awi$ $ef yiwen n unegmar s snat n tmerwin n “dinyers”.

25- Mi yesla i lehdur, yeîîef-iyi seg yi$il, yerra-yi yid-s $er ssuq, yenna-iyi-d: “Mel-iyi-d anwa wagi i k-d-yessenzen sselâa-agi tafuêant?” Sekne$-as-d yiwen n um$ar d awezlan yeîîef yiwet n te$mert. Yessawel-as-d, ta$ect-is d tazurant tesâa lhiba n unawur, yenna: “Ha-t-a tura, ulac win imenâen seg lefâayel nwen, la imeddukal nne$ wala iberraniyen imsebriden s ssuma-agi $layen mliê swayes tesnuzum yir iselman-agi. D kunwi yerran tamurt-agi yellan d tajeooigt n “Tissalya” d aneéruf, d aéru mebla tudert, imi ternam i yal ta$awsa. Maca ad awen-ggale$ ad tt-id-xellsem $layet. Skud d nekk i yettdebbiren, ad rre$ imzenza iêraymiyen s abrid.

D$a yessenbev yiwen seg yimâiwnen ines ad yesmir sdat n medden irkelli ayen yellan deg tquffet inu, yessenbev deg-s da$en ad yerkev iselman-nni. Tigawt-agi tessefreê mliê “Fityas”, tessebgen-it-id yewâeô mliê, sakin yessuter deg-i ad a$e$ abrid-iw: “Iâumm-iyi i wass-a a “Lusyus”, dayen tura bezzaf i nesbehdel am$ar-agi, nekkes fell-as sser!”

Tadyant-agi teqreê-iyi mliê, îîfe$ abrid-iw $er lêemmam ulac acu rebêe$, la idrimen-iw, la imensi inu, wagi irkelli s lfevl n lewâara n umeddakel d wumi $ri$. Mi kfi$ asucef, u$ale$ ad wali$ “Milun”, sakin kecme$ $er texxamt-iw.
26- Mi kecme$ $er texxamt, ha-tt-a truê-d “Futis” taqeddact tenna-yi-d: “Ay inebgi nne$, la ak-d-yessawal Mass inu”. Maca sli$ yakan s cceêêa n “Milun”, sutre$ deg-s ad as-d-tini ur zmire$ ara ad n-ase$, ilaq ad sgunfu$ seg yinig, maççi d uççi iyi-laqen, d asgunfu i êwaje$.

Mi yesla i tririt-agi yusa-d s timmad-is ad iyi-yawi. Deg tazwara ugi$ ad d-ddu$ yid-s, d$a yenna-yi-d: “Ur ttu$ale$ ara $er texxamt-iw alamma truêev yid-i”, vefre$-t. Yessawev-iyi $er ssrir ines, urâad serse$ iman-iw yebda isteqsiyen ines: “Amek i yettili umeddakel-iw “Dimyas”? Amek i tettili tmeîîut-is? Arraw-is? Aklan-is imecîaê?” Fki$-as yakk isalan i yeêwaj.

Sakin yebda la iyi-yesseqsi $ef ssebba n yinig inu. Mi s-fki$ tiririyin iwatan, yezzi-d $er tmurt-iw, tasestant tewwi-d $ef yiheggaren ines, ula d lêakem s timmad-is yedda.

Asmi yefhem belli inig yesseâya-yi mliê, ur zmire$ ara ad ldi$ allen-iw seg nnaddam i d-ye$lin fell-i, ula tifyar inu ur ssawve$ ara ad tent-kfu$, u$ale$ maççi d lehdur i ttmeslaye$, d asgurmet i sgurmute$.

Mi iwala liêala inu, yeooa-yi ad ruêe$ ad gne$. Deg taggara ssawve$ ad rewle$ i um$ar-agi amecêaê iyi-yeserwan lehdur deg umkan n lmakla. Mi kecme$ taxxamt-iw, gre$ iman-iw deg wusu ad nadi$ ives.
# Ass amezwaru

# Ramdane Lasheb

Ssaâa tewwev d ttlata, aselmad n teglizit ijemmeâ lqecc-is akken ad iffe$. Di tzeqqa inelmaden irkeb-itten lêir. Ha-t yewwev-d! Ha-t yewwev-d! Akka kan ara teslev qqaren gar-asen.

Ikcem-d uselmad n tmazi$t, ssusmen akk, wid yellan bedden, wwven akk imekwan-nsen, ttrajun amek ara d-isiwel uselmad-agi amaynut. Isers izmamen-is, immuqel $er inelmaden, inna-d :

- « Azul fell-awen ».

D imeslayen imezwura i d-yenna uslemad n tmazi$t di tzeqqa n u$erbaz azzayri. Ssyin akin, yewwi-d awal $ef tutlayt d tira-s, inelmaden, nutni ssusmen, sellen kan. Awal-is yekfa-t, izmumeg-d $er inelmaden inna-ya$-d :

- « £er tikkelt-nniven ! ».

Ur neéri amek tâedda ssaâa-nni, imi yeffe$ aîas inelmaden i t-ivefren deffir am akken ur d-yettu$al ara. Am akken d targit i nurga ne$ra tamazi$t. Ala maççi d targit d tillawt, dayen tamazi$t tekcem deg u$erbaz azzayri. Ass-a d ass ara naru s isekkilen n ure$, d ass imgaraden d wiyiv imi d tikelt tamezwarut ara nemmeslay s tmazi$t daxel n tzeqqa n u$erbaz ; ulac win ara d-yinin susmet mmeslayet s tayev.
Mi wwve$ s axxam, si tewwurt i ssawle$ i yemma :

- « Ass-a, $ri$ tamazi$t ! »

Tenna-yi-d :

- « Amek-itt aka, tmazi$t-agi a yelli ? ».

Ëki$-as-d ak ayen $ri$, yemma tezmumeg, udem-is innecraê, tenna-d :

- « Tagi, fehme$-tt a yelli ! » .

ass n 14 di tuber 1995
# Amezgun n teqbaylit

# Takfarinas Nait Chabane

Gar wayen yellan di tsekla n teqbaylit d tiwsatin n tmedyazt akked tid n tesrit, ur yelli ara yakan umezgun yu$ amviq-is gar-asent. Wagi ma yella nmuqel kan $er tgemmi tadelsant deg wayen yeânan tasekla akked téuri. Armi d iseggasen-agi kan ineggura, segmi d-rnant kra n tewsatin timaynutin $er tsekla n teqbaylit, i d-iban umezgun. Aîas n inaéuren i yeb$an ad snernin. Timusniwin-nsen di ta$ult-agi, imi ttwalin belli $ur-s azal d ameqqran. £ef waya i ilaq ad d-nawi awal $ef umezgun s umata d wamek yella di teqbaylit.

Di tazwara, yewwi-d fell-ane$ ad néer d acu i d amezgun. Aîas ur nefôiz ara s telay d acu-t ne$ d acu i d azal yesâa. Ihi, amezgun d yiwet n tewsit n tsekla ne$ yettuneêsab da$en d taéuri. Ulac amezgun wer taceqquft. D nettat i d aferdis agejdan. Taceqquft-agi d avris, yesâa lebni-ines iman-is, imi yettwaxdem akken ad t-uraren izeffanen $ef usayes. Ihi, avris n tceqquft ilaq ad yesâu tulmisin-ines ara t-yessemgarden $ef yevrisen nniven akka, am wungal. Yal ûûenf n téuri, nezmer ad t-naf di tceqquft n umezgun. Deg-s tamedyazt, deg-s ccna, deg-s aéawan, deg-s dddeê… atg. Axaîer deg umezgun, maççi s wawal kan i yettâeddi yizen ; tella tenfalit n wawal. Tella tenfalit n wudem. Tella tin n
tfekka am wakken da$en i tella tenfalit s uéawan. £ef waya i tturaren izeffanen taceqquft zdat yemferoen. Tella ula d taklut di tedlegt. Tagi da$en yella deg-s yirzen. £ef waya i nezmer ad nefhem belli amezgun s wannect-agi n tewsatin yesdukel, yessewseâ tanfalit-ines armi tessawev ad d-tawi tilawt s inevruyen-is mi ara tt-id-teskan i yemferoen ad tt-walin zdat-sen, ad as-êulfun am wakken d tidet ugar n wakken ara êulfun i usefru ne$ i tezlit.

# Amek yella umezgun n teqbaylit ?

Ar ass-a werâad yennerna umezgun n teqbaylit akken ad yili am ccna n teqbaylit ma neddem-it-id d amedya. Ticeqqufin timezwura i yettuxedmen, bdant-d di rradyu, imi dinna kan i yufan tagnit inaéuren ad xedman ama d ccna, ama d cwiî n umezgun. Tugget n tceqqufin i yettuxedmen di tmurt-nne$, ttâeddayent-d, di tiliéri ta$elmawt, s taârabt, ma d taqbaylit skufren-tt kan di rradyu ula akken, ktalen-as-d swayeâ s cceêa. Ihi, ttawilat-nni ara yesnernin amezgun s tidet, ulac-iten. Maâna $as akka, aîas i iâerven ad sbedden ticeqqufin s wayen sâan gar ifassen-nsen d ttawil, imi ayen yettuxedmen yekka-d s$ur wid yeskelsen di rradyu tis snat, akka am Ccix Nurdin, Qasi Tizi Wezzu…atg. Llan da$en kra n inaéuren i ixedmen amezgun yessevsayen, di tesfifin, akka am Sliman Äazem Sliman Cabbi…atg. Acukan wigi xedmen amezgun s wudem n Ccna imi yal tikkelt tettili-d tezlit akken ad d-tcebbeê taceqquft.

Ticeqqufin yettwassnen ass-a di teqbaylit, d tid i d-yerra Muêya $er teqbaylit : Tacbaylit, Sinistri, Am win yettraoun Rebbi… Tigi merra aîas n trebbuyaâ i tent-yuraren di tmurt n leqbayel.

Deg yiseggasen-agi ineggura, degmi d-nnulfant tiddukliwin tidelsanin di tudrin akked t$iwanin, aîas i yesbedden ticeqqufin. Aîas n yelmeéyen i ikecmen $er trebbuyaâ n umezgun akken ad lemden taéuri-agi. £as akken allalen n tmusni akked n tedrimt xuûûen, meâna u$alen yelmeéyen éran ugar n zik d acu i d amezgun d wazal yesâa di tmusni akked yidles. Qqaren imusnawen n téuri-agi deg yiwen wawal « Efk-iyi-d amezgun, ad ak-d-rre$ agdud yesâa ta$erma ».

Di taggara ilaq ad néer belli aêric ameqqran n lsas n t$ermiwin ttekkin deg-s inaéuren. Mi ara n$er $ef umezruy
agrigi nettwali belli wid akk ixeddmen taéuri ne$ tasekla, sâan
azal d ameqqran di te$remt tagrigit. Wamma nekni mazal
nettraju lefnar n t$erma-nne$ melmi ara ya$. Akken ad d-
nessukkes tunti-nne$ gar idelsan ilaq ad nesmir lmidad n tutlayt-
nne$ di yal ta$ult. S lidi n walla$ i d-kkrent t$ermiwin. £urwat ihi.
Tarbaât umezgun amazi$ “ Tigawt d wawal”
TUTLAYT

# Tamazi$t-nni

# Kaci Sadi

Iseggasen ttâeddin. Cfawat tt$imint. Ëala win yeb$an ad yettu ara yettun. Yak nekni nennum tatut ula di tefsut! Ur iban ma d aâemmed i nettâemmid ne$ d aksan ur nuksan ara. Iêun Rebbi yella yimru llant tewriqin, ne$ akken i s-yenna yiwen: Ccwi kan llant nnehtat…

Liêala texlev. Ula d yiwet t$awsa ur tessefraê. Tayri teffe$ ulawen. Ur tezmir ad tesdukel imdanen. Ggtent t êsifin, u îîuqtent tmen$iwin. Ula d tussna ideg nerra tafat tu$al d alqaf gar yifassen n wuêricen, akken i sen-yehwa ad tt-sqedcen. Kellxen-as i Talsa yen$a lêif n zik seg Zik. Maca, ay$er ur nesdukul ara ayen yelhan n Zik d wayen yelhan nTura?

£er taggara, imdanen cedhan tavsa. £as akken tudert-nsen akk d tavsa. Yu$al uqelmun s ivarren. Ti$ermiwin n Ugafa ççant ddunit; igellilen n Unéul ôwan tawa$it. Tzad t$ennant, leâqel yeffe$.

Ad teérem i txeddem timawit deg ugdud yemmugren leqrun meb$ir tira. Yen$an ne$ ineqqen iman-is ur yeéri d anwa ne$ d acu i d ssebba. Imdanen $ilen d tafekka kan n Umdan i yettmettaten. Yu$ lêal ula d idles yettmettat. Akken i ttmettaten yemdanen i ttmettatent ula d tutlayin, i ttmettatent ne$ i neggrent da$en t$ermiwin.
Meâni, i wacu akk asfelsef-agi ? Awalem aîas, tifrat ulac !

Isteqsiyen ggten, tireémiyin ad d-yawi Rebbi ! Dacu kan, mi $-âerqent mavi, d$a ad tt-nerr i tejmilin. Ma maççi d tajmilt d tame$ra. Ma maççi, d tame$ra d asmekti ne$ d aâeggev deg yiberdan. Ruêet, ha-t-an aâeggev-nni yewwi-d kra. Yadra llan wid yesteqsan ne$ xersum ad ssusmen, ur leddin ara iqemmac-usen aîas, skud alla$en sebken, sanda akken i tessawev tmazi$t-nni ?

Acêal n yiseggasen i iâeddan $ef tmazi$t, ass-a ? Sani i d-tessawev ? D anwi i tt-yeb$an, d anwi ur tt-neb$i ? Acêal n wid i tt-ye$$aren ? Acêal n wid yessnen ad tt-arun ? Yadra, ahilen i ss$aren deg u$erbaz lhan ne$ dir-iten ? Wulmen ne$ ala ? Yadra teffe$-d tmazi$t i umverkel-nni n yiseggasen imenza, asmi tekcem s a$erbaz ne$ ala ? Yadra neb$a-tt ad tt-n$er nettat, ne$ neb$a-tt i wakken ad n$er yis-s ayen nniven ?

Wamma i$misen-nni ne$ tis$unin-nni yuran s tmazi$t $ef tmazi$t, ad tessevêiv ad temmeslayev fell-asen ne$ ahat ad tugadev seg wid-nni yettâeggiven d I M A Z I £ E N !

Ma d tilifizyu, ne$ axi d taqbaylit-nni n rradyu, $as ruê ay aârab ar tafsut ! Cwiîiîuê-agi i s-d-isaêen i tmazi$t yessefraê aîas IMAZI£EN ; yesru tamazi$t. Iruê ad iqeââed tamazi$t, yessexreb taqbaylit, yerna yewwet-as agejidur.

Deg walla$en n yemdanen, frant irkel s wawal. Neîîef-d Rebbi seg ucvav. Ad ibarek Rebbi, imusmawen maççi yiwen ; ma d tamusni ur tessin yiwen. Truê tennejla. Acêal n yiseggasen aya, ula d agemmay urâad i t-nqeââed. Urâad i nemsefham ula $ef yilugan n tira ne$ $ef tira n wawalen.

Yal yiwen ad ak-yeqqar ; nekk d taqbaylit-iw i iseêêan. Acêal nêemmel ad nezzi ad nennev $ef wayen ur nesâi anamak ! Acêal nêemmel ad neqqen tiî-nne$ $ef wayen yellan d llsas i tussna ! Ur iban ma d nekni kan i iteqqnen allen-nne$ $ef tidet, ne$ neb$a ad tent-neqqen ula i wiyad nniven akken ur tt-ttwalin?

Ad twehmev ur ak-yehwi ! Timsal banent i uder$al, wid yesâan allen ur tent-ttwalin ara. Yerna dayen isehlen mavi. Lemmer kan ad nebru i tidak-nni-nne$ ur nessufu$. Lemmer terbiêed ay ul, mi ara yenna$ yiwen $ef tutlayt is, amek ara isevêi ad tt-yemmeslay ne$ ad tt-i$er ne$ ad tt-yaru ? Amek teb$iv tutlayt-agi ad tesâu
amkan $ur wiyav, nettat ur t-tesâi ula $ur wid-is ? D wid i tt-yessuturen ara irewwlen fell-as ! D wid ara irewwlen fell-as i ara tt-yessuturen ! Ruhet sefrut-tt-id kunwi ! Aha îra ! Ma d aqareâ n kra n temkact, yiwen ur ye$fil. Neêrec akk $er tqerracin. Yak seg zik nettwassen s tfextin d yicangalen. D acu kan, tura d tamazi$t ara nneddi (numda) akken ad neîîef yis-s tamazi$t. D tamzi$t kan i tent-yettxelliûen !

Maççi a xir yal yiwen ad yesteqsi iman-is d acu d-yeîîef seg teqbaylit ? D acu yessen ? Ahat ad yizmir ad d-yernu kra n wayen ixuûûen deg yidlisen seg wayen ara d-yegren (yejmaâ) $ur yem$aren. Xersum d tutlayt ad yesseêbiber fell-as.

Maççi a xir lemmer yal yiwen ad ixemmem amek ara d-yernu aqcuv ne$ as$ar $er tezdemt. Akken ad iéer wemdan, lad$a win teâna temsalt (spécialiste ) acu yellan d wacu ixuûûen. Imawalen ha-t- an d ilmawen. Aîas n yimeslayen iqdimen i ilaqen ad d-nejmeâ, aîas n wawalen imaynuten i ilaq ad ten-nesnulfu.

Maççi lemmer ad nesdukel, a xir, tira n kra n wayen yellan ass-a s tmazi$t, i waken ad yishil i t$uri d « les archives » sya $er zdat ?

Ar melmi akka ara mmâawanen akk wid teâna temsalt ama d tisdawiyin gar-asent ne$ nitenti d rradyu akked Tilifizyu d HCA d CNPLET. Xersum i wakken ad walin ibaxixen-agi ara d-yettnulfun, di tmazi$t yu$alen d ta…ma…zi$t. Ne$ akken, xersum, ur tett$imi ara teqbaylit-nni gar wazul… d tanemmirt.

# TAQBAYLIT-NNI

Ussan-agi yegget wawal $ef yizerfan n wemdan, lad$a widen n tmeîîut. Yetta$ lêal, timetti anda i nedder mazal-itt teîîef deg yir ansayen. £ef waya d$a i teqqujmer kan deg yiwen wadeg d yiwen wakud. Tegguma ad taé $er zdat. Yir ansayen, rnu-yasen Lislam asertan « islamisme» d yir tamussni n wid ye$ran tikerkas.

Mi tlul êeznen wudmawen

Yeâreq ttlewliw i tlawin

Tiî teççur d imeîîawen

Amzun d ssixîa i d-ye$lin
Irgazen zemmen imawen

Ugaden w(in) (ara)ten-yesteqsin

Mi d taqcict i d-ilulen

Azzelt ffert timêezmin

Lbaruv ur t-nekkat !

Deg uxxam sexsit tafat!

S a$erbaz mi ara tekcem

Ur nevmiâ seg-s tamussni

Ad tim$ur ad tt-id-negzem

Ulamma ssebba ur telli

Ad tt-nerr s axxam ad texdem

Nnwal, asired, aôebbi

Alla$-is ad t-neoo d ilem

Akken ur tlemmed tilelli

D rray-nne$ d awal-nne$ !

Ara tevfer yelli-tne$!

D tilmeéyin d timeêbas

Lemmer yiwen ad tent-iéer

£er berra ma ff$ent yiwwas

Öwan warrac asmesxer

Amerreê ur yelhi i tullas

Dir-it zzhu d udewwer

Nnan wid yezde$ nnêas

Yeôwan deg-sent aseqcer !

Wi(n) (ye)b$an ad ikkerreâ i$san !

A(d) (a)k-yini d Rebbi i d-yennan !

Mi meqqret tedda d tislit

T$il ad beddlent temsal

D argaz-is wis ma tessen-it

S yisem-is ur (a)s-tessawal

Fell-as yeffer tabavnit

Zdat-s ur tesâi awal

Tettaf-it kan di twa$it

Ma ulac-itt ay tesâa azal

Tameîîut yerra-tt d taklit !
# Yeqqar îîfe$ di tjaddit !

Ula d-nini ma tebra

Nnan-t-id wid i iâeddan

Nekni ur $-terri tmara

Akken ad nawi tin yebran

Ma d netta asirem yella

Ad yefren tin i s-yehwan

Ccreâ yefka-yas rebâa

£as maççi d win yettéallan

Di zzwao kan i ssnen Rebbi !

Yigujilen n tmusni !

Zun wigi ye$ran ciîuê

Nettara deg-sen tafat

N$il ad as-rren rruê

I tin yeôwan lmertat

Zi$ lexdeâ îîven-t di dduê

Tem$er, lemden rregmat

I wallen yennev wecluê

Ur cikke$ ad walin tifrat

Udem i fkan i tberranit

Weroin t-tessin Teqbaylit !
# “Ugur” n tira

# Ramdane Abdenbi

Deg wedlis « Méthode de Langue Kabyle »n Si Ɛmer Ben Saɛid Bulifa, ad naf deg usebter 31 taseddart taneggarut n usefru i d-yewwi « Mzian » i «Chikh» ideg s-yeqqar :

… Chah ! a erraï our nechfi

Ar tseddoudh h'afi

Ak r'ounfoun medden i tseh'ouis

Deg usebter 87, yenna « Iouizoû » i « Chikh » :

Athaïa oull iou itkhïeq'

R'er d'akhel ifelleq'

Mi chki ara ts id nesmekthi

Aï agellid' lkhaleq'

Thefroudh ar' s lh'eq'

Ad' ar' thilidh d' ama'ani

R'erk, a Rebbi, aïd nekherreq'

Sellek ar' na'oueq'

Iak r'ourek ish'el koull echchi
# Asefru-agi yura Bulifa deg wedlis-is, yura-t ula d Dda

Lmulud deg «Les Isefra de Si Mohand », ad t-naf s wuṭṭun 126 deg usebter 266 :

# Ataya lqelb itqelleq

- Ɣer daxel iceqqeq
- Tick' ara p id nepmekti
- Ay agellid a lxaleq
- Bḍu-y-aɣ s lḥeq
- Tiliḍ fellaɣ d amâanni
- Ɣur k a Ṛebb' ay nâalleq
- Sellek aɣ nâawweq
- Yak ɣurek yeshel kulci

Imira, di 2008, ma nebɣa ad naru tamedyazt-agi, ad tt-naf s tɣara-agi :

# Taseddart taneggarut n usefru amezwaru :

… Ccah ! a rray ur necfi

Ar tedduḍ ḥafi

A k-ɣunfun medden i tteḥwis

# Asefru wis sin :

- Ataya wul-iw itxeyyeq
- Ɣer daxel ifelleq
- Micki ara tt-id-nesmekti
- Ay agellid lxaleq
- Tefruḍ-aɣ s lḥeq
- Ad aɣ-tiliḍ d amɛanni
- Ɣer-k, a Rebbi, ay d-nxerreq
- Sellek-aɣ nɛewweq
- Yak ɣur-k ishel kulci

                         Ise
Di tukkist-agi n tmedyazt taqbaylit taqburt yeggten, mačči d tawsit, d asentel, d aɣanib neɣ d anya i ɣ-iceɣben; mačči d tasleḍt, d azɣan neɣ d asefhem iɣef la nettnadi maca d isekkilen iss ttwarun yefyar-agi. Si Bulifa ɣer Dda Lmulud ɣer Uzerrad neɣɣar taqbaylit yettwarun s isekkilen n tlatinit. Seg yimiren ar yimira, tira ur beddlent ara maca nnernant, imnuda d imusnawen ssaẓergen-d idlisen n tseftit, tajerrumt d imawalen s tlatinit.

Asqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa yessaẓreg-d daɣen kra n yedlisen yecban: «Awfus amaynut n tutlayt tamaziɣt» n Sadaq Bendali, «Manuel de syntaxe berbère» n Musa Imarazen, «Amawal n tunuɣin n tesnukyest» n Kamal Buwamara, «La phonologie générative du kabyle, l'emphase et son harmonie», Moḥend U Lḥaǧ Laseb, neɣ «Les racines du berbère communes» n Muḥend Akli Ḥaddadu...

Deg yedlisen-agi i ijerred umezruy n tira n tutlayt tamaziɣt s isekkilen n tlatinit. Deg yedlisen-agi akk d widen i ten-id-yezwaren ɣer teẓrigt i ɣ-d-iban belli tegzem di rray, teddez tebrez… Imnuda d imusnawen nnan-d, imaruyen d imeskaren ḍefren-ten. Tutlayt tamaziɣt s isekkilen n tlatinit ara tettwaru, d taɣelnawt neɣ d tunṣibt.

Deg wedriraw n yedlisen-agi ad naf Dallet, Basset, Camps, Foucauld… et Laoust. D leqdic-nsen n yiḍelli iɣef nsenned imira i wakken ad d-nheggi azekka n tutlayt tamaziɣt. D ayen i d-jemɛen «irumyen-agi» i yuɣalen d lsas n leqdic n imusnawen-nneɣ imira.

Ɣas akka teddez tebrez, maca llan iɛekkiren, timeckukal d wuguren yuzzaren deg webrid n gemmu n tutlayt tamaziɣt. Kra yekka-d seg wemgarad ussnan yellan gar yemnuda d imusnawen: uguren-agi ussnanen ad ten-id-nefser di lqaɛa, ad sen-nezzi, ad ten-nesskew, ad qqaren, ad ten-nessefruri, ad uɣalen d aɣebbar, ad ten-yeddem waḍu...

Kra nniḍen yekka-d sɣur widen yugin d widen ikukran tutlayt tamaziɣt: uguren-agi isertanen nwala-ten amek i fran deg Wegraw aɣelnaw s werfad n ifassen… Tamsalt-agi n wuguren isertanen tcudd s isekkilen n tira. MACA amek ara tcudd tɣerma, idles d tgemmi tamaziɣt s isekkilen n tira talatinit, taɛrabt neɣ tifinaɣ?
Di tmurt n Lmerruk, atmaten-nneɣ n dihin fernen isekkilen n tfinaɣ s tɣara tunṣibt. Isekkilen rsen s wangalen-nsen di tsefsit Arial Unicode MS n Wegraw agraɣlan n Unicode. Amek ara xedmen yezzayriyen yebɣan isekkilen n tfinaɣ : ad arun tifinaɣ n Caker, n Besaɛud neɣ n IRKAM neɣ ahat d tin n itergiyen!

Di tmurt-nneɣ, Lezzayer, widen yettarun, yiden yeɣɣaren, widen yesselmaden d widen ilemmden tamaziɣt d isekkilen n tlatinit i sseqdacen i wakken ad arun tutlayt-nsen ɣas akka taswiɛt n ujerreb ur ɛad tekfi.

Ayen « nessaram » d akken imaziɣen n Siwa di Maṣer ad ndekwin, ad ḥrirten… ad ssutren tira n tutlayt-nsen s isekkilen n taɛrabt ma ufan kra n wallalen i wayagi. Akka yal wa di tmurt-is, di temnaḍt-is ad yaru s tin yebɣa, s tin iss yettxemmim, ma d nekni ad naru «s tagi-nneɣ »... imiren mmi-s n taɣaḍt ad t-yečč wuccen...

Ulamma ur ɛad nufi lexbar iṣeḥḥan maca tutlayt tamaziɣt ters deg useɣzan Windows Vista s sin isekkilen-is (TZ) ad tt-naf di tekwat n tutlayin deg wadda ayeffus n wegdil : TZ Tamazight (latin-français), wissen ma ters d tutlayt neɣ d anasiw ! Ahat deg wuṭṭun i d-iteddun ad naf amek ara naru tamaziɣt di Windows Vista.

Di taggara, ad nuɣal kan alamma d tigemmi-nni-nneɣ iseg d-nekkes taqsiṭ-agi n umeksa yebɣan ad yessenz tafunast-is di ssuq. «... Akka neɣ ad tuɣal ɣer tkessawt » i yenna umeksa i yemsewqen i s-yennan belli tafunast-is ɣlayet, aṭas iṣurdiyen i yessuter deg-s. Yenna-yasen : « D wagi i d azal-is, ad tenz s wazal-agi neɣ ad tt-rreɣ s adrar ad teks ».

Ihi akken i s-yenna umeksa akka neɣ ad tuɣal s adrar iseg d-tṣubb.
